# Calyx ŌĆö Technical Documentation

Complete technical reference for **Calyx** (repo `ChrisRoyse/Calyx-Dev`), an
association-native database engine written in Rust. Originally generated by reading the
source code at `C:\code\Calyx-Dev` synced to `origin/main` commit `2e7b9a2` ("Add
kernel-first funnel search", 2026-06-16), refreshed through commit `96cbc84f`
("Batch blind spot XTerm decoding", 2026-06-27), then through `32cc7dea` ("docs: codify
README asset contract", 2026-06-29), then through `dd500623` ("Merge PR #1027 ŌĆö repair
aiwonder nextest gate", 2026-06-29), then through `ab86c430` ("Materialize biomedical
evidence substrate in Aster graph", 2026-07-03), then through `57fcd478` ("Fix
mechanistic direction gates", 2026-07-07), and **most recently refreshed through commit
`8310d211` ("Make Poly runbooks public-mirrorable", 2026-07-07)** for interface and
invariant changes across the post-`ab86c430` window. HEAD is in sync with `origin/main`
at `8310d211`. New surfaces tracked in the latest (`8310d211`) refresh:
- **Biomedical blindspot audit hardening** (#1277ŌĆō#1284) ŌĆö a new structured CLI,
  `biomedical-blindspot-audit`, closes the paper-section blindspots that were previously
  prose-only: germline-versus-somatic synthetic-lethality inversion, missing patient
  context, drug lifecycle viability, external literature novelty, repeated-run stability,
  benchmark-export readiness, and transcriptomic-reversal specificity. It requires every
  audit source file, fails closed on missing/malformed source rows, and persists
  `biomedical_blindspot_audit_report.json`, `audited_hypotheses.jsonl`,
  `ready_hypotheses.jsonl`, `blocked_hypotheses.jsonl`, `benchmark_export.jsonl`, and
  `metrics.json`. Full State Verification root:
  `C:\code\Calyx-Dev\target\fsv\biomedical_blindspot_audit_final_20260707_180115`.
- **`calyx-poly` imported as a workspace crate** (`db5ebab3`, finished through `8310d211`) ŌĆö
  the workspace now has **25 crates**. `calyx-poly` is a local/read-only Polymarket
  forecasting and operations crate: public market/on-chain source ingestion, typed feature
  derivation, Calyx constellation/anchor writeback, local forecast artifacts, grounding
  against resolved outcomes, admission/risk/policy gates, scoring, backtesting, and
  reproducibility. Its boundary forbids order signing/submission/cancellation, bankroll
  management, stake sizing, Kelly/PnL optimization, and fabricated fallback data. Public
  operator runbooks are now mirrored under `crates/calyx-poly/runbooks/` and `docs/`.
- **Assay and ledger expansion from the Poly import** ŌĆö `calyx-assay` now includes FSV-covered
  rank/categorical association, distance correlation, HSIC, MIC, Granger, copula tail
  dependence, cross-correlation, conditional MI, CCM, Hawkes, point-process co-intensity,
  PC-stable causal discovery, partial correlation, and partial-network estimators. Ledger
  entry kinds gained grounding, admission, agent-forecast, policy, and score categories,
  with stable `CALYX_*` code redaction support.
- **Workspace dependency inheritance repaired** ŌĆö root `[workspace.dependencies]` now owns
  `tungstenite = 0.29.0` with rustls webpki roots and `ureq = 3.3.0` with JSON support;
  `calyx-cli` inherits `ureq.workspace = true`. This fixes Cargo verification with
  `calyx-poly` present under the `members = ["crates/*"]` glob.

- **Biomedical discovery pipeline ŌĆö real hypothesis evaluation, falsification & a
  source-mined evidence substrate** (the dominant theme of this window; extends the
  `ab86c430` molecular-vault work). A genuine end-to-end discovery flow now exists as
  first-class CLI surface: a **typed association miner** (`typed-association-miner`),
  **biomedical association validation gates** (`association-validation-gates`), a
  **hypothesis falsification sweep** (`hypothesis-falsification-sweep`, with
  source-matching constraints and asserted-relation handling), a **hypothesis evidence
  assembly bridge** (`assemble-hypothesis-evidence`), a **hypothesis evaluator driver**
  (`hypothesis-evaluator-driver` + `hypothesis-evaluate` / `hypothesis-rank`) with an
  **HTTPS evaluator provider**, **grounded cross-vault molecular chain traversal**
  (`chain-walks`), and **ledger-sealed discovery-run manifests** (`discovery-run`
  seal / reproduce / verify, with stage preflight and ledger-redaction fixes). Native
  discovery-bridge CLIs landed (`discovery-chain`, `discovery-gate`,
  `bridge-evaluate-rank`, `bridge-falsification-evaluate`). Evaluated hunts were run and
  FSV-documented across **precision oncology, oncology deep-hunt, drug-safety triage,
  metabolic/cardiovascular, neuro, infectious/immunology, and rare-disease** domains, plus
  a published **biomedical hypothesis review atlas** and a `docs/medicalsearch` markdown
  combiner + hypothesis papers.
- **Fail-closed external drug-combination source mining** ŌĆö combination hypotheses are now
  mined fail-closed and validated against a large roster of external biomedical corpora,
  each added as a source-mining/validation slice with its own FSV: **NCI ALMANAC**,
  **CDCDB**, **ClinicalTrials** (current-combination recheck + gate validation), **FDA /
  PubMed** (structured relation extraction + gate rows), **openFDA** labels, **RxNorm**
  (canonicalization + combination products + TwoSIDES safety), **DailyMed SPL**, **Europe
  PMC** (pair / relation / safety-counter / endpoint-outcome evidence, validated against
  openFDA and ClinicalTrials), **FAERS** (events + `metformin/trametinib` case validation +
  a case-quality ranker overlay), **PubChem**, **ChEMBL**, **DrugCentral**, **PharmGKB**,
  and **nSIDES**. A safety-interaction coverage rollup and independent effect-result
  validation gate the endpoint evidence. **Materialize LINCS reversal screen +
  perturbation metadata** (`materialize-lincs-reversal`) and a **novelty calibration
  splitter** (`novelty-calibration-split`) also landed, and the HEAD commit
  **fixes the mechanistic-direction gates** (`mechanistic-direction`).
- **Database-native association state ŌĆö truth moves out of files and into Aster CFs**
  (the second major theme). Multi-anchor **A37 admission state** is now persisted to a
  database-native CF with **DB-only admission sources**, and downstream gates require DB
  admission. **Partitioned RRF slot-truth, reports, and plans are persisted in the Graph
  CF** with a DB fused-RRF truth path, DB timeline import, DB plan remap, DB query offsets,
  and RRF recall gates that **require DB truth / plans / admission** (truth writes are
  delayed until recall passes; tied slot-truth rows are accepted). **`stream-fbin` is now
  DB-only / diagnostic-capable** with DB-native templates (`stream-fbin-lens-template`),
  **i8bin label anchors are DB-native** (`i8bin-labels`, derived from rows), the **lens
  catalog authority moved into the Aster DB**, and **partitioned manifests are stored in
  and read back from Aster** (`multi-anchor-readback`).
- **Graph CSR binary persistence hardened** (continues issue #996) ŌĆö the persisted graph
  CSR is now **binary-encoded**, built from **physical range scans**, **rebuilds when
  stale**, **upgrades legacy edge weights** without a full JSON parse, and **preserves
  evidence weights**; adds **collection-local edge-range readback** and graph-collection
  lifecycle cleanup (`graph-collection-state`, `graph-collection-generations`) plus a
  **vault supersession / `retire-vault`** path.
- **GPU / ONNX / embedder runtime for RTX 5090 + CUDA 13.3** ŌĆö opt-in **ONNX CUDA graph
  bindings** and **green-context streams**, **pipelined resident ONNX measurement
  batches**, a **GPU ONNX SPLADE sparse runtime**, **assay GPU co-residency guards** with
  **K-way safe co-residency derived from measured VRAM**, **CUDA 13.3 cudarc** build
  support, **Qwen3 embedding defaulted to FP16**, **RTX 5090 TEI defaults** / runtime
  policy with **FP16 TEI commissioning readback** and Calyx-owned TEI endpoints, and
  avoidance of quantized ColBERT default commissions.
- **GDELT sparse algorithmic lenses** ŌĆö a new family of **sparse / structural GDELT
  lenses** wired into the corpus loader, with DB anchor fields, action-geo anchors, and a
  row-text anchor fallback.
- **Assay signal / estimator correctness** ŌĆö the **mixed discrete KSG estimator** was
  fixed and switched to **no-replacement KSG CI subsampling**; **blind-spot detection is
  calibrated by lens pair**; the **oracle sufficiency gate** gained a calibrated lower
  bound; the **discovery-chain sufficiency gate** and **falsification evidence matching**
  were hardened; and **ensemble leave-one-out baselines** are calibrated.
- **Media transcription now fail-closed** (closes the prior `dd500623` open item #993) ŌĆö
  raw media ingest performs **fail-closed transcription** during ingest. Also: a
  **panel-manifest restore** command, an **explicit probe-matrix stale policy**, a
  **DiskANN search-frontier optimization**, **streamed SST compaction outputs**, and
  public-mirror-sync-staging / readback-manifest-format-dispatch / clippy-debt fixes.

The previous (`ab86c430`) refresh tracked these surfaces (still current):

- **Biomedical / molecular evidence substrate** (issue #884 plus the evidence-slice
  commits) ŌĆö a new **molecular-vault materializer** and a biomedical evidence substrate
  materialized directly into the Aster graph, with recorded validation-evidence slices
  from external biomedical corpora (**PubTator/PubMed**, **ClinicalTrials**, **DGIdb**
  drugŌĆōgene) and a **nonclinical bridge corpus**. Hypothesis evaluation now ranks
  genuinely-evaluated hypotheses (with full-stack verification) rather than projected/stub
  scores. New/extended paths under `crates/calyx-aster` (molecular-vault materializer) and
  the evidence-recording commands.
- **Warm resident GPU lens inference hardened end-to-end** (issues #1002, #1004, #1029,
  #1136, #1153, #1154, #1167) ŌĆö the resident lens-worker service (introduced at
  `dd500623`) is now the primary GPU ingest/measure path. Resident-route discovery gained
  a **fail-closed GPU ingest gate** (#1004), the resident service now **warms from the
  active vault** panel/registry (#1029, closing the prior p0 follow-up), `measure_batch`
  rows **stream as individual binary frames** (#1002), multi-lens measurement **fans out
  across slots** behind a fail-loud sequential-execution gate (#1153), a **resident
  panel-parallelism probe** was added to `calyx healthcheck` (#1154), and resident vault
  warmup is scoped to GPU slots. Opt-in **assay lens parallelism** landed alongside.
- **ONNX Runtime GPU execution correctness** (issues #1130, #1136, #1142, #1143, #1167) ŌĆö
  ONNX Runtime **I/O binding** and per-provider telemetry for warm lens inference (#1136);
  a `cuda` feature **unified across the GPU surface** with deploys gated on compiled
  capabilities (#1130); an audit of per-provider node placement so **int8 CPU fallback can
  no longer masquerade as GPU** (#1142); **bounded GPU shape diversity + BFC arena growth**
  on long streams and **preflighted GPU arena caps** before session init (#1143, #1167);
  and ONNX arena env knobs extracted into `onnx/arena.rs`. Windows ONNX CUDA DLL bootstrap
  wired for repo gates.
- **Deploy build-identity gate & new `calyx-buildinfo` crate** (issues #1108, #1116) ŌĆö a
  new **`calyx-buildinfo`** crate embeds a self-identity (build hash + cargo features) into
  deployed binaries, closing the #1108 incident where a runner silently served stale
  behavior for days. Adds a **verified runner deploy** and a **feature-aware deploy
  identity gate** that embeds and verifies cargo features (#1116), plus `jq`/git-dirty gate
  fixes.
- **New `calyx-fsv` crate & FSV evidence-root discipline** (issue #1014) ŌĆö a new
  **`calyx-fsv`** crate canonicalizes `CALYX_FSV_ROOT` resolution, enforcing an **absolute
  root** so per-crate test working directories stop scattering full-stack-verification
  evidence; adds a **fail-closed FSV vault-health gate** and refuses suite-wide FSV roots
  before the tmp-guard trap.
- **Graph CSR materialization & closure knobs** (issue #996) ŌĆö associations now
  materialize into a **persisted CSR sharded into a manifest + byte segments** (#996), a new
  **`materialize-graph-csr`** CLI command with weave-loom CSR persistence, a fix for silent
  empty CSR projection on checkpointed vaults, **closure replication defaulted off** with an
  rng-factor knob + closure telemetry, and **SPANN closure / query-aware pruning knobs**.
- **Search-index freshness, rebuild resumption & exact provenance reads** (issues #1080,
  #1089, #1096, #1100, #1104, #1112) ŌĆö a **derived-content watermark** keeps replay-only
  ingest `--fresh` (#1100) and never regresses a foreign writer's watermark; targeted
  ledger point-reads resolve via **commit-ordered binary search** (#1112) and **exact
  provenanceŌåÆcommit-seq resolution** (#1096); search indexes are **pinned in memory** with
  probe-matrix slot timings + perf budgets; `rebuild-search-index` **streams DiskANN
  progress** (#1080) and persists a **rebuild-required marker to resume interrupted
  rebuilds** (#1089); nav-runtime freshness is keyed to one **pinned snapshot seq** (#1104).
- **In-region / Ward guard unification & probe-matrix fail-closed** (issues #1082, #1086,
  #1088, #1094, #1120) ŌĆö the CLI **in-region guard is unified with the calibrated Ward
  guard profile** (#1094), guard calibrate **fails closed on non-dense/unknown/inactive
  slots** (#1120), the in-region guard **fails closed when it filters all probe-matrix
  candidates** (#1082), the probe-matrix slot search cache was fixed (#1086), and the probe
  matrix **fails closed on ungrounded vaults** with bounded search phases and cached query
  vectors.
- **Panel sufficiency (mutual information)** ŌĆö panel joint MI is now **floored at its
  strongest member** so sufficiency stops degrading as panel width grows, and panels fail
  closed on missing anchor audits with power-adjusted sufficiency.
- **Typed error propagation & vault ref resolution** (issues #1060, #1082, #1145) ŌĆö typed
  `CalyxError` codes and remediations are **preserved through CLI error dispatch** (#1145);
  vault ref resolution was split into a `vault/resolve` module so **CWD entries stop
  shadowing logical vault names** (#1082); `cx-list --include-slots` **hydrates from
  physical slot CFs and fails closed** (#1060); `verify-chain` vault-path parsing was
  unified.
- **Windows durability & repo-sync doctrine** (issues #1069, #1165) ŌĆö Windows **durable-write
  parent-directory sync** fixed (#1069), WSL-on-Windows worktree gitdirs **fail fast**, the
  **public mirror sync gate** was hardened (#1165), and repo-sync doctrine docs were added.

The previous (`dd500623`) refresh tracked these surfaces (still current):

- **Resident GPU lens-worker service for CLI ingest** (issue #1004) ŌĆö CLI batch ingest now
  routes through a long-lived, warm resident worker service instead of cold per-batch
  worker spawns, eliminating repeated model load/VRAM warm-up. New modules under
  `crates/calyx-cli/src/panel_commands/resident/` (`client`, `codec`, `dispatch`, `flags`,
  `protocol`, `server`) plus `cmd/ingest/worker/resident.rs` and
  `cmd/ingest/constellation/resident_batch.rs`; `measure` now uses a **binary** resident
  IPC path rather than JSON. Open follow-ups: the resident service must warm from the
  active vault panel/registry (#1029, p0), JSON IPC is still used for large multi-vector
  payloads (#1002), and ONNX Runtime I/O-binding / device tensors are not yet wired (#1011).
- **Idempotent batch re-ingest fast-path** (issue #999) ŌĆö re-ingesting an identical JSONL
  batch now short-circuits, preserving stored slots on idempotent replay and adding
  idempotent-batch readback verification; small-batch multi-lens GPU ingest perf is still
  tracked open (#999, blocked).
- **Fail-closed batch preflight** (issue #1009) ŌĆö JSONL batch ingest is now preflighted
  **before** vault startup and fails closed on mixed-batch identity conflicts rather than
  partially committing.
- **Media-derived artifact provenance** (issues #988, #976) ŌĆö raw media ingest is now
  routed through derived-text artifacts whose provenance back to the source media is
  modeled and persisted (`crates/calyx-aster/src/media_artifact.rs`,
  `crates/calyx-cli/src/media_derived_text.rs`); derived-text routing is enforced for raw
  media. Automatic audio/video transcription during media ingest remains open (#993).
- **Registry contract audit & repair** (issues #1000, #990) ŌĆö persisted registry contract
  drift is now audited and repaired **without** spinning up runtime sessions, and audits
  avoid re-hashing artifacts; built-in panel registry snapshots are materialized.
- **Physical discovery / FSV harnesses** (issues #876ŌĆō#879) ŌĆö real (no longer
  projected/stub) implementations plus full-stack-verification harnesses landed for the
  **probe matrix** (#879), **grounded discovery chain** (#878), **spectral community
  mining** (#877, with a scaled projected-eigensolver convergence budget), and
  **cross-domain bridge mining** (#876).
- **Search storage hardening** (issues #982, #984) ŌĆö fixed multi-sidecar storage, pruning
  of stale search-filter artifacts, plus binary-sidecar and batch-provenance FSV fixtures;
  `calyx-web-api` now exposes origin artifacts honestly. The Lodestar LP-mincut DFVS
  solver is wired, and dense search-index rebuild memory is now bounded.

The previous (`32cc7dea`) refresh tracked these surfaces (still current):

- **Production MCP startup is now wired into `calyxd`** (`feat(calyxd): wire production
  MCP startup`, issue #959) ŌĆö the daemon now constructs and serves a `CalyxMcpServer` in
  server mode. This **supersedes** the older "MCP transport not wired into the running
  daemon / serves only `/metrics`" gap statements that still appear verbatim in the
  per-subsystem docs below (doc 01, doc 20), which were not line-by-line re-audited.
- **`calyxd` learner-origin worker API** (issue #813) ŌĆö a new loopback HTTP service
  (`crates/calyxd/src/learner_origin/`) for website learner memory, exposing
  `POST /v1/learner-signals/batches`, `/v1/interventions/decide`,
  `/v1/interventions/{id}/outcomes`, `/v1/mastery/estimate`, `/v1/oracle/forecast`,
  `/v1/reactive/affect-signals`, and `/v1/kernel/track-spines`. Accepted writes are
  durable through Aster CFs + the Ledger hash chain (request success is never the source
  of truth); reactive-affect audit reasons are persisted.
- **`calyx-web-api` Prometheus `/metrics`** (#945, #946, #597, #1249 G11) ŌĆö the read-only
  HTTP API now exposes engine-native health surfaces plus per-route HTTP RED metrics
  (request rate, p50/p95 latency, errors) at `GET /metrics` (new `metrics.rs` module),
  in addition to its 6 `/v1/*` routes (doc 25).
- **`weave-loom` CLI command** (`feat(loom)`, issue #870) ŌĆö corpus-scale loom that writes
  the `XTerm` CF plus a between-document kNN AssocGraph into the `graph` CF; `kernel-build`
  now consumes that woven graph.
- **Resident panel runtime service** and `calyxd` restore / VRAM-budget audit metrics
  (configured VRAM ceiling now surfaced on `/metrics`, #1934).
- **Cross-cutting fail-closed / provenance hardening** across search, Lodestar answer
  paths, and the MCP search surface (search now fails closed on unverifiable provenance,
  unbounded multi-sidecars, and missing lens provenance for learned signals).

## How this set was produced
## Current post-57fcd478 additions

### calyx-poly

`crates/calyx-poly` is now a first-class workspace member. It imports the useful Calyx-facing
parts of the Poly forecasting system while preserving a strict local/read-only boundary: it ingests
public market and on-chain evidence, stores local source snapshots and Calyx constellations, derives
forecast features, grounds them against resolved outcomes, writes local forecast artifacts, and gates
admission through policy/risk/sufficiency checks. It explicitly does **not** trade: no order signing,
order submission, cancellation, redemption, bankroll management, stake sizing, Kelly sizing, or PnL
optimization. Public runbooks live at `crates/calyx-poly/runbooks/` with repository-level copies in
`docs/poly-single-workstation-runbook.md` and `docs/poly-daily-jobs-runbook.md`.

### Biomedical blindspot audit

The biomedical discovery surface now has a mandatory post-generation audit command,
`calyx biomedical-blindspot-audit`, documented in `docs/medicalsearch/109_biomedical_blindspot_audit.md`.
It converts the paper's blindspot questions into persisted machine state: ready rows, blocked rows,
pending-evidence rows, benchmark export rows, and metrics. The historical 726-row atlas is now described
as **pre-blindspot ready** until rerun through this audit.

Each document lists the **source files it covers** at the top, uses numbered sections,
puts structured data in tables, and traces behavioral claims to specific files. The
authoring rules are in [`_SPEC.md`](_SPEC.md). Where the code is a stub, a `todo!()`, or
diverges from the design plans, each doc says so in a **Gaps / not covered** section.

| 09 | [09_sextant_search.md](09_sextant_search.md) | calyx-sextant ŌĆö HNSW/DiskANN/SPANN/funnel, BM25, RRF fusion, planner |
| 10 | [10_loom_associations.md](10_loom_associations.md) | calyx-loom ŌĆö cross-terms (agreement/delta/interaction), agreement graph |
| 11 | [11_assay_signal_bits.md](11_assay_signal_bits.md) | calyx-assay ŌĆö KSG mutual information, redundancy contract, panel sufficiency |
| 12 | [12_lodestar_kernel.md](12_lodestar_kernel.md) | calyx-lodestar ŌĆö grounding-kernel discovery, kernel index & answer path |
| 13 | [13_ward_guard.md](13_ward_guard.md) | calyx-ward ŌĆö fail-closed per-slot guard, conformal calibration |
| 14 | [14_ledger_provenance.md](14_ledger_provenance.md) | calyx-ledger ŌĆö hash chain, Merkle checkpoints, ed25519 signing, verification |
| 15 | [15_anneal_optimization.md](15_anneal_optimization.md) | calyx-anneal ŌĆö reversible self-tuning, tripwires, shadow tests, rollback |
| 16 | [16_oracle_prediction.md](16_oracle_prediction.md) | calyx-oracle ŌĆö butterfly consequence tree, reverse walk, honesty gate |
| 17 | [17_graph_mincut_paths.md](17_graph_mincut_paths.md) | calyx-mincut + calyx-paths ŌĆö SCC, betweenness, spectral, traversal |
| 18 | [18_hazard_soak_and_testkit.md](18_hazard_soak_and_testkit.md) | calyx-hazard-soak (25 probes + soak) + calyx-testkit |

- **New to Calyx?** 01 ŌåÆ 23 (intent) ŌåÆ 04 (data) ŌåÆ the subsystem you care about.

- **Assessing maturity / what's left?** 22 ŌåÆ 24.

## Notes on accuracy

- Counts in 22 are static (`git ls-files`/`ripgrep`/`wc`) tallies, not a test-runner
  report; tests were **not executed** while producing these docs.
- Several numbers are pinned-by-test invariants in the code (38 error codes, 31 MCP
  tools, 33 column families) ŌĆö these are exact, not estimates.
- Auxiliary files in this folder: [`_SPEC.md`](_SPEC.md) (authoring rules) and
  `_open_issues.json` (raw GitHub open-issue dump used to build doc 24).

---

# 01 ŌĆö System Overview

**Source files covered (high-level entry points & manifests):**
- `README.md`, `Cargo.toml`, `rust-toolchain.toml`, `LICENSE`
- `crates/calyx-core/src/lib.rs` (types, error catalog, traits)
- `crates/calyx-cli/src/main.rs`, `crates/calyxd/src/main.rs` + `src/lib.rs`, `crates/calyx-mcp/src/main.rs` + `src/lib.rs`
- `crates/calyx-hazard-soak/src/main.rs`
- All 19 crate `src/lib.rs` module headers
- Detailed per-subsystem behavior is documented in docs 04ŌĆō20; this doc is the map.

> This document describes **what the code is**, traced to source. Where the code is a
> stub or diverges from the design plans in `docs/dbprdplans/`, that is noted here and
> in the per-subsystem docs. Calyx is **pre-1.0** software; the README itself flags the
> on-disk format and interfaces as unstable.

---

## 1. What the system is

Calyx is an **embedded, association-native database engine** written in Rust
(workspace, `edition = 2024`, pinned toolchain `1.95.0`, license BSL 1.1). Its native
record is not a row or a single vector but a **constellation**: one input measured
through many independent, frozen embedders ("lenses"), each producing its own typed
slot-vector that is kept separate (never flattened). On top of that record the engine
bakes in: multi-signal search and fusion, derivation of the associations *between*
slots, information-theoretic measurement of which lenses actually add signal, discovery
of the minimal "grounding kernel" that explains a corpus, a fail-closed guard against
out-of-distribution answers, a hash-chained provenance ledger, reversible
self-optimization, and grounded consequence prediction.

It is **not a service mesh.** It is a stack of focused Rust crates compiled together,
with four thin entry points on top: a CLI (`calyx`), a daemon (`calyxd`), an MCP
server (`calyx-mcp`), and a read-only HTTP API (`calyx-web-api`, a loopback Axum service
documented in [25_web_api.md](25_web_api.md)). It builds **CPU-only by default**; a CUDA
GPU backend is an opt-in Cargo feature (`--features cuda`).

### 1.1 The four verbs (organizing model)

The README and `docs/dbprdplans/DOCTRINE.md` describe the engine as a "calculus of
association" with four verbs, each mapped to subsystems implemented in the workspace:

| Verb | Meaning | Subsystem / crate |
|---|---|---|
| **Measure** | Assemble a constellation by viewing one input through a panel of lenses | `calyx-registry`, `calyx-aster` |
| **Count** | Derive the associations between slots (agreement, delta, interaction) | `calyx-loom` |
| **Differentiate** | Quantify the unique information (bits) each lens adds about real outcomes | `calyx-assay` |
| **Compose** | Find the kernel, guard generation, answer with provenance | `calyx-lodestar`, `calyx-ward`, `calyx-ledger` |

### 1.2 Three trust principles (enforced in code)

- **Grounding is mandatory** ŌĆö claims are measured against anchored outcomes; ungrounded
  results are tagged *provisional* (see `CxFlags`/`AnchorKind` in [05_core.md](05_core.md),
  and the Oracle honesty gate in [16_oracle_prediction.md](16_oracle_prediction.md)).
- **No-flatten** ŌĆö slots stay typed and separate end-to-end (`SlotVector` is never
  concatenated into one opaque blob; Ward scores each slot independently).
- **Fail closed** ŌĆö unknown lens, shape mismatch, uncalibrated guard, or missing data
  returns a structured `CalyxError`, never a silent wrong answer. The closed error
  catalog (`CalyxErrorCode`, 38 codes) is the spine of this principle.

---

## 2. Architecture

### 2.1 Layered crate stack

```
Entry points :  calyx (CLI) ┬Ę calyxd (daemon + /metrics) ┬Ę calyx-mcp (agent MCP) ┬Ę calyx-web-api (read-only HTTP /v1)
                       Ōöé                    Ōöé                            Ōöé                        Ōöé
Shared search:   calyx-search (one Sextant recall ŌåÆ fusion ŌåÆ rerank ŌåÆ provenance path; CLI + web-api)
                       Ōöé
Intelligence :   Oracle  ┬Ę  Anneal  ┬Ę  Lodestar
                       Ōöé
Engine       :   Sextant ┬Ę Loom ┬Ę Assay ┬Ę Ward ┬Ę Registry
                       Ōöé
Foundation   :   Aster (LSM storage) ┬Ę Forge (CPU/GPU math) ┬Ę Ledger (provenance)
                       Ōöé
Core         :   calyx-core (ids, error catalog, data model, engine traits)
                 calyx-paths / calyx-mincut (graph primitives)
```

`Surfaces ŌåÆ Intelligence ŌåÆ Engine ŌåÆ Foundation` is the README's flow. The actual
internal dependency graph is in [02_source_code_map.md](02_source_code_map.md); `calyx-core`
is the zero-internal-dep foundation depended on by all other crates. The workspace now
holds **25 crates** ŌĆö `calyx-poly` and `calyx-web-api` were added after `57fcd478`; `calyx-buildinfo`
(issue #1108), `calyx-fsv` (issue #1014), `calyx-search` (issue #573/#900), and
`calyx-web-api` (issue #889) were added earlier after the 2e7b9a2 baseline.

### 2.2 Process / surface map

| Surface | Binary | Crate | Transport / port | Purpose |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| CLI | `calyx` | `calyx-cli` | process invocation; JSON error envelope on stderr | Drive every engine operation from the shell; 46 structured subcommands + legacy/domain command families |
| Daemon | `calyxd` | `calyxd` | HTTP `GET /metrics` (Prometheus 0.0.4) on loopback, default `127.0.0.1:7700`; loopback MCP-over-socket + learner-origin worker API when configured | Long-running service: startup CUDA/VRAM probes, health probe, Prometheus metrics, `verify-restore` tool. **As of `32cc7dea`, server mode wires a production `CalyxMcpServer`** registering all MCP tools (`register_all`) when `mcp_bind_addr` + `mcp_mtls` are configured (loopback bind, mTLS required; issue #959); when unconfigured the daemon serves only `/metrics`. Also hosts the learner-origin worker API (#813). |
| MCP server | `calyx-mcp` | `calyx-mcp` | **stdio only**, line-delimited JSON-RPC 2.0, MCP protocol `2024-11-05` | Agent-facing tool surface: 31 `calyx.*` tools |
| Soak/hazard harness | `calyx-hazard-soak` | `calyx-hazard-soak` | CLI binary | 25 fault-injection probes (H1ŌĆōH25) + a long integrated soak; emits JSON + Prometheus evidence |

### 2.3 Technology stack

| Layer | Technology | Version / constraint (from `Cargo.toml`) |
|---|---|---|
| Language / toolchain | Rust, edition 2024 | toolchain `1.95.0` (pinned in `rust-toolchain.toml`), `rust-version = 1.95` |
| Hashing | `blake3` | `1` ŌĆö content addressing, ledger chain, Bloom filters |
| Crypto (signing) | `ed25519-dalek` | `2` ŌĆö ledger checkpoint signatures |
| Crypto (at-rest) | `aes-gcm`, `hkdf`, `sha2`, `zeroize` | `0.10` / `0.12` / `0.10` / `1` |
| Serialization | `serde`, `serde_json`, `bincode_reloaded` (3.1.6), `ciborium` | `1` / `1` / `3.1.6` / `0.2` |
| Storage | `memmap2` `0.9`, `crc32fast` `1`, `zstd` `0.13`, `filetime` `0.2`, `nix` `0.30` (fs) | mmap tables, CRC, posting-list compression |
| CPU math | `wide` `1` (SIMD), `rayon` `1` (parallelism) | Forge CPU backend |
| GPU math (opt-in) | `cudarc` `0.19.7`, `nvml-wrapper` `0.10` | CUDA 13.2, `sm_120`; feature `cuda`, default off |
| SQLite (import-only) | `rusqlite` `0.40.1` (bundled) | only the `calyx migrate` CLI reads external SQLite |
| IDs / time | `ulid` `1`, `uuid` `1` (dep present; core uses ULID), Unix-ms `Ts` | |
| Randomness | `rand` `0.8`, `rand_chacha` `0.3` | deterministic seeded RNG |
| Observability | `tracing` `0.1`, `prometheus` `0.14` | |
| Errors | `thiserror` `2` | |
| Testing | `proptest` `1`, `criterion` `0.5`, `cargo-fuzz` (6 targets) | see [21_test_suite.md](21_test_suite.md) |

### 2.4 Build profiles

The workspace `Cargo.toml` tunes debug info for a high-churn multi-agent build cadence:
`[profile.dev] debug = "line-tables-only"` (first-party crates keep function names +
file:line for backtraces) and `[profile.dev.package."*"] debug = false` (dependencies get
no debuginfo). This was a deliberate response to dev/test executables reaching ~280 MB
and the shared `target/` dir ballooning to ~190 GB. See
[03_configuration.md](03_configuration.md) and `docs/implementation/02_BUILD_PERFORMANCE.md`.

---

## 3. Public surfaces (APIs / tools / commands)

### 3.1 MCP tools ŌĆö 31 total (`calyx.*`), grouped by domain

Full parameter/return/error tables in [19_mcp_api_tools_reference.md](19_mcp_api_tools_reference.md).
The tool set is pinned by `crates/calyx-mcp/tests/stdio.rs::EXPECTED_TOOLS`.

| Domain | Tools |
|---|---|
| Vault & panel (6) | `create_vault`, `add_lens`, `retire_lens`, `park_lens`, `list_panel`, `profile_lens` |
| Ingest & measure (4) | `ingest`, `ingest_media`, `anchor`, `measure` |
| Search & navigate (10) | `search`, `kernel_answer`, `neighbors`, `agree`, `disagree`, `define`, `guard_generate`, `traverse`, `skills`, `search_skill` |
| Intelligence (6) | `abundance`, `bits`, `kernel`, `guard.calibrate`, `guard.check`, `propose_lens` |
| Provenance & ops (5) | `provenance`, `answer_trace`, `verify_chain`, `reproduce`, `anneal.status` |

### 3.2 CLI commands

`calyx-cli` uses **hand-rolled arg parsing** (no clap), dispatched in layers. ~20
structured subcommands (`create-vault`, `add-lens`, `retire-lens`, `park-lens`,
`list-panel`, `profile-lens`, `ingest`, `anchor`, `measure`, `search`, `kernel-answer`,
`bits`, `kernel`, `guard`, `abundance`, `propose-lens`, `provenance`, `verify-chain`,
`reproduce`, `anneal-status`) plus legacy commands (`readback`, `merkle-root`, FSV/ops
families) and domain command groups (`navigate`, `sextant`, `media`, `lodestar`, `lens`,
`panel`, `intelligence`, `summarize`, `migrate`, `anneal`, `leapable`). Every failure
emits a JSON `{code,message,remediation}` envelope on stderr with exit code 2. Full
tables in [20_cli_and_daemon_reference.md](20_cli_and_daemon_reference.md).

### 3.3 Daemon endpoint

`calyxd` serves exactly one HTTP route, `GET /metrics` (Prometheus text format 0.0.4) on
loopback. Metric families and startup probes are documented in
[20_cli_and_daemon_reference.md](20_cli_and_daemon_reference.md).

## 4. Entry points & invocation

| Binary | Crate | How invoked |
|---|---|---|
| `calyx` | `calyx-cli` | `cargo run -p calyx-cli -- <command>` or the built `calyx` binary |
| `calyxd` | `calyxd` | `calyxd --config <path.toml>` (validate-only without a live serve); `calyxd verify-restore ...` (PH67) |
| `calyx-mcp` | `calyx-mcp` | launched by an MCP client over stdio |
| `calyx-hazard-soak` | `calyx-hazard-soak` | `calyx-hazard-soak --hazards <range>` / `--all-hazards` / soak mode |

Build/test: `cargo build --release --workspace` (CPU), `cargo test --workspace`,
optional `cargo build --release --workspace --features cuda`.

---

## 5. Runtime directory layout & data location

Data lives under a **vault directory** (root resolved via `vault_path` /
`$CALYX_HOME`). The full on-disk tree and per-artifact format table are in
[04_storage_and_schema.md](04_storage_and_schema.md). Summary of what gets created:

| Path (under vault) | Contents | Owner subsystem |
|---|---|---|
| WAL segments | write-ahead log records (`CXW1`) | Aster |
| SSTables | sorted immutable tables (`CXS1` v2) + Bloom filters | Aster |
| `manifest-{seq:020}.json` | versioned manifest (`ManifestVersion{1,0}`), immutable refs verified by BLAKE3 | Aster |
| Arrow column chunks (`CXA1` v1) | column-major f32 slot data | Aster |
| `idx/kernel/<id>/index.json` + `kernel.json` | grounding kernel index/artifact (`FORMAT_VERSION = 1`) | Lodestar |
| `idx/*` | ANN/DiskANN/SPANN indexes (`CLXDA001` graph pages) | Sextant |
| `.anneal/tripwire.toml`, `.anneal/budget.toml` | persisted self-optimization tripwires & budgets | Anneal |

### 5.1 Storage tier classification

From [04_storage_and_schema.md](04_storage_and_schema.md):

| Tier | Examples | Rule |
|---|---|---|
| **Sacred** (never auto-deleted) | WAL, Ledger CF, Base/slot CFs, manifest + immutable refs, Anchors | source of truth |
| **Regenerable** | Kernel/Guard CFs + `idx/kernel/*.json`, B-tree/inverted indexes, ANN `idx/*`, Assay cache, XTerm CFs, compacted SSTs, raw slot sidecars | rebuildable from sacred data |
| **Ephemeral** | memtables, LRU/TTL caches, arenas, reader-lease registry, VRAM blocks | in-memory, lost on restart |

---

## 6. Error hierarchy

The closed error catalog lives in `calyx-core` ([05_core.md](05_core.md)). The base
wire type is **`CalyxError`** (`{ code: &'static str, message: String, remediation:
&'static str }`, `Serialize`-only). The canonical catalog is the `CalyxErrorCode` enum
plus the `CALYX_ERROR_CODES` slice ŌĆö **38 codes** in PRD-18 order, pinned by the test
`catalog_matches_prd_18_exactly`. `type Result<T> = Result<T, CalyxError>`.

Individual subsystems define **module-local `&'static str` codes** that are deliberately
NOT in the closed 38-code catalog (they namespace per crate). Roots observed across the
workspace:

| Subsystem | Error-code roots (prefix family) |
|---|---|
| Core (catalog) | the 38 `CALYX_*` codes; plus module-local `CALYX_RECORD_SCHEMA_VIOLATION`, `CALYX_ALLOC_CAP_EXCEEDED`, `CALYX_AUTHN_REQUIRED`, `CALYX_CONSENT_VIOLATION`, `CALYX_PROVISIONAL_VAULT`, `CALYX_TEMPORAL_*` |
| Aster | `CALYX_ASTER_TORN_WAL`, `CALYX_ASTER_CORRUPT_SHARD`, `CALYX_ASTER_BASE_CORRUPT`, `CALYX_FORMAT_VERSION_UNSUPPORTED` |
| Forge | `CALYX_FORGE_*`, `CALYX_QUANT_INTELLIGENCE_LOSS`, `CALYX_VRAM_BUDGET_EXCEEDED` |
| Registry | `CALYX_LENS_{FROZEN_VIOLATION,DIM_MISMATCH,NUMERICAL_INVARIANT,UNREACHABLE}`, `CALYX_REGISTRY_DUPLICATE`, `CALYX_PANEL_LENS_MISSING`, `CALYX_{RAM,VRAM}_BUDGET_EXCEEDED`, `CALYX_STALE_DERIVED` |
| Loom | `CALYX_LOOM_*`, `CALYX_REACTIVE_*` |
| Assay | `CALYX_ASSAY_{LOW_SIGNAL,REDUNDANT,INSUFFICIENT_SAMPLES}`, `CALYX_TC/TE_*`, `CALYX_BAYES_INVALID_INTERVAL` |
| Lodestar | `CALYX_KERNEL_*`, `CALYX_RECALL_*`, `CALYX_DFVS_*`, `CALYX_PROP_*`, `CALYX_SCOPE_*`, `CALYX_LODESTAR_*` |
| Ward | `CALYX_GUARD_*`, `CALYX_WARD_*` |
| Ledger | `CALYX_LEDGER_*`, `CALYX_REPRODUCE_*` |
| Anneal | `CALYX_ANNEAL_{UNKNOWN_CHANGE_ID,CHANGE_COMMITTED,INVALID_ROLLBACK_STATE}` |
| Oracle | `CALYX_ORACLE_*` |
| Mincut / Paths | `CALYX_SCC_*`, `CALYX_BETWEENNESS_*`, `CALYX_MINCUT_*`, `CALYX_GRAPH_*`, `CALYX_PATHS_*` |
| MCP | JSON-RPC codes + `CALYX_MCP_JSONRPC_INVALID`, `CALYX_MCP_TOOL_DUPLICATE` |
| CLI | `CALYX_CLI_USAGE_ERROR`, `CALYX_CLI_IO_ERROR` |
| Daemon | `CALYX_DAEMON_{BIND_FAILED,CONFIG_INVALID,HEALTH_FAIL,FRAME_INVALID,CONN_PANIC}` |

---

## 7. Subsystem summaries

Each one-paragraph summary points to its deep-dive doc. All behavioral claims are traced
there.

### 7.1 calyx-core ŌĆö types, errors, traits ([05_core.md](05_core.md))
Dependency-free foundation. Provides content-addressed IDs (`VaultId(Ulid)`,
`LensId([u8;16])`, `CxId([u8;16])`, `SlotId(u16)`) where `LensId`/`CxId` are the first
16 bytes of BLAKE3 over length-delimited ordered parts; the closed `CalyxErrorCode`
catalog (38 codes); the data model (`Constellation`, `Slot`, `Panel`, `SlotVector` =
Dense/Sparse/Multi/Absent, `Anchor`, `Signal`, etc.); and the object-safe engine traits
`Lens`, `Index`, `VaultStore`, `Estimator`, plus `Input` and `Clock`. Serialization is
serde/JSON in this crate.

### 7.2 calyx-aster ŌĆö LSM storage engine ([06_aster_storage_engine.md](06_aster_storage_engine.md))
The "schema" layer and largest crate. A write-ahead log (`CXW1`, 20-byte header, CRC32,
group-commit with a 2 ms window) feeds bounded memtables that freeze and flush to
SSTables (`CXS1` v2, sorted index, trailing BLAKE3 Bloom). MVCC snapshots via
`VersionedCfStore`/`Snapshot`/`ReaderLease`; crash recovery via a JSON manifest
(`ManifestVersion{1,0}`, atomic rename, BLAKE3-verified immutable refs); 33 column
families routed by `CfRouter`; compaction + hot/cold tiering. Unknown manifest major ŌåÆ
`CALYX_FORMAT_VERSION_UNSUPPORTED`. The crate header still calls itself a "skeleton" and
compaction cadence is fixed (`FIXME(PH46)`).

### 7.3 calyx-forge ŌĆö math runtime ([07_forge_math_runtime.md](07_forge_math_runtime.md))
One numeric backend implemented twice: `CpuBackend` (SIMD via `wide`) and `CudaBackend`
(`cudarc`), both implementing the `Backend` trait (7 ops: gemm, cosine, dot, l2,
normalize, topk, device_info). No runtime auto-dispatch ŌĆö callers pick a `dyn Backend`;
an `AutotuneCache` records but does not auto-apply winning configs. 7 quantization levels
(`QuantLevel`): F32, Bits8 (ScalarInt8), Bits8Fp (MXFP8), Bits4Fp (MXFP4), Bits3p5,
Bits2p5 (TurboQuant + QJL residual), Bits1 (sign bits). The `cuda` feature (off by
default) compiles 3 `.cu` kernels to PTX+cubin with `--fmad=false` for bit-near CPU/GPU
parity; **fail-closed, no silent CPU fallback**. Default VRAM soft cap 12 GiB.

### 7.4 calyx-registry ŌĆö lens registry ([08_registry_lenses.md](08_registry_lenses.md))
Holds frozen, content-addressed embedders implementing the `Lens` trait. Runtimes:
`AlgorithmicLens`, `TeiHttpLens` (HF TEI HTTP), `CandleLens` (BERT via candle),
`OnnxLens` (fastembed/ort), `StaticLookupLens` (mmap model2vec, `CXLKUP1`),
`MultimodalAdapterLens` (hash-derived projection), `ExternalCmdLens`, temporal lenses
(`E2RecencyLens`, `E3PeriodicLens`, `E4PositionalLens`), and `CommissionedLens`.
`LensId = content_address([name, weights_sha256, corpus_hash, output_shape_fingerprint])`.
Registration always fails closed (the frozen contract is mandatory). Hot-swap via
`SwapController` + durable `BackfillScheduler`. Multimodal/commissioned lenses currently
emit deterministic hash projections, not learned embeddings.

### 7.5 calyx-sextant ŌĆö search & navigation ([09_sextant_search.md](09_sextant_search.md))
In-RAM HNSW (M=32, deterministic BLAKE3 levels), on-disk DiskANN/Vamana (`CLXDA001`,
4 KiB pages, RobustPrune, beam search), DualDiskANN, SPANN (RAM centroid HNSW + zstd-3
on-disk posting lists, k-means++), and a kernel-first 3-hop funnel search. BM25 inverted
index (k1=1.2, b=0.75, Lucene-style idf). Multi-vector MaxSim (late interaction). Fusion
is Reciprocal Rank Fusion with `RRF_K = 60.0`; a deterministic keyword classifier picks
the strategy and a planner enforces caps (kŌēż100, efŌēż512, slotsŌēż16, 20M cost cap).
Temporal post-retrieval boosts (50/35/15) and causal gating.

### 7.6 calyx-loom ŌĆö associations ([10_loom_associations.md](10_loom_associations.md))
Computes cross-terms between slot vectors: **agreement** = cosine (scalar), **delta** =
elementwise `aßĄóŌłÆbßĄó`, **interaction** = elementwise Hadamard `aßĄó┬ĘbßĄó`, **concat** = `[aŌĆ¢b]`.
`LoomStore::agreement_graph()` returns an undirected weighted edge list
(`Vec<AgreementEdge>`) recomputed from an in-memory cross-term map; a 0.05-bit
`PairGainGate` controls materialization. Also lead/lag series analysis (`LLAG1` wire
format). Persists to Aster `XTerm`/`Reactive` CFs.

### 7.7 calyx-assay ŌĆö signal bits ([11_assay_signal_bits.md](11_assay_signal_bits.md))
Measures mutual information (bits) each lens adds about an anchor using a **KSG estimator
(k-NN, Chebyshev distance, brute-force O(n┬▓))**, natsŌåÆbits, with a deterministic ChaCha8
bootstrap CI. Enforces a redundancy contract (`MIN_SIGNAL_BITS = 0.05`,
`MAX_PAIRWISE_CORR = 0.6`, min 50 samples). Panel sufficiency: `panel_bits Ōēź
anchor_entropy_bits` (no slack). Persists to Aster `Assay` CF.

### 7.8 calyx-lodestar ŌĆö grounding kernel ([12_lodestar_kernel.md](12_lodestar_kernel.md))
Discovers the minimal record set (the ~1% MFVS) explaining a corpus via a staged
approximate directed-MFVS pipeline: Tarjan SCC ŌåÆ Brandes betweenness ŌåÆ greedy top-fraction
candidate selection (score = `0.40┬Ędegree + 0.40┬Ębetweenness + 0.20┬Ęgroundedness`) ŌåÆ
heuristic candidate graph ŌåÆ `dfvs_approx`. The kernel doubles as an HNSW index and an
answer path (BFS reach with `hop_score = edge_weight┬Ę0.9^hop`). Recall gate default 0.95;
kernel artifact `FORMAT_VERSION = 1`. The LP relaxation is not wired to a solver and the
build pipeline does not measure recall (defaults to 0).

### 7.9 calyx-ward ŌĆö fail-closed guard ([13_ward_guard.md](13_ward_guard.md))
Scores each required slot independently with `dense_cosine` against a per-slot threshold
`tau` (INVARIANT A3 ŌĆö no flattened/averaged gate). Combination rule: `AllRequired` (AND
of all slots) or `KofN{k}`. Conformal calibration sets `tau` to the smallest candidate
cosine where empirical bad-FAR Ōēż target_far AND a binomial CDF bound holds (estimator
`conformal_quantile_v1`, needs Ōēź50 bad scores). Default per-`SlotKind` FAR: Identity 0.01,
Content 0.03, Stylistic 0.05; cold-start `tau = 0.7`. Verdicts ŌåÆ accept / new-region(learn)
/ quarantine / refuse(OOD). Persists verdicts to the Ledger.

### 7.10 calyx-ledger ŌĆö provenance ([14_ledger_provenance.md](14_ledger_provenance.md))
Append-only, hash-chained log. Entry hash = BLAKE3 over length-framed
`(seq, prev_hash, kind, subject, payload, actor, ts)`; each entry's `prev_hash` seals the
previous (genesis = zeros). 10 entry kinds (wire codes 0ŌĆō9). Every
`DEFAULT_CHECKPOINT_INTERVAL = 1000` entries an Admin row carries a Merkle
`CheckpointPayload`, optionally ed25519-signed (message `b"calyx-ledger-root-v1" ŌĆ¢ ŌĆ”`).
Verification (`VerifyResult` = Intact/Broken/Corrupt) re-walks and re-hashes the chain.
Persists to Aster `Ledger` CF. No key management in-crate.

### 7.11 calyx-anneal ŌĆö self-optimization ([15_anneal_optimization.md](15_anneal_optimization.md))
Reversible tuning of index params (hnsw_ef=64, hnsw_m=16, diskann_beamwidth=32, ŌĆ”),
Forge tiling/dtype, Loom eager pairs, and storage knobs, plus online heads (Ōēż1024 params)
and Ward Žä. Loop: prepare(reserve rollback) ŌåÆ budget ŌåÆ shadow-test on held-out replay ŌåÆ
gate (tripwire + per-metric non-regression) ŌåÆ promote(pointer swap + Ledger) or rollback.
Tripwires (`.anneal/tripwire.toml`): RecallAtK<0.90, GuardFAR>0.01, GuardFRR>0.05,
SearchP99>200ms, IngestP95>500ms, 5% hysteresis. Rollback state machine: Prepared ŌåÆ
Promoted ŌåÆ Reverted/Committed. Audited via 28 `AnnealLedgerAction` variants (tag
`anneal_event_v1`); persisted to Aster `AnnealRollback` CF.

### 7.12 calyx-oracle ŌĆö consequence prediction ([16_oracle_prediction.md](16_oracle_prediction.md))
Builds a recursive "butterfly" `ConsequenceTree` (DFS, `MAX_DEPTH = 4`, `HOP_ATTENUATION
= 0.7`, prune below `MIN_CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD = 0.05`, cycle-guarded), a reverse
outcomeŌåÆcause walk (`MAX_REVERSE_DEPTH = 3`, `grounded_confidence(n)=n/(n+1)`), and an
**honesty gate**: `sufficient = panel_bits Ōēź anchor_entropy_bits`; otherwise returns
`OracleError::Insufficient` carrying a `SufficiencyBound` with per-sensor deficits. Ledger
tags `oracle_predict_v1`, etc. The intelligence-objective `J`/growth-curve APIs from the
plans are not implemented here.

### 7.13 calyx-mincut + calyx-paths ŌĆö graph primitives ([17_graph_mincut_paths.md](17_graph_mincut_paths.md))
`calyx-mincut`: Tarjan SCC + condensation, Brandes betweenness, eigenvector centrality,
Laplacian eigenmaps / GFT, spectral gap. Despite the name, there is **no min-cut/max-flow
or feedback-vertex-set solver** ŌĆö only an LP scaffold that formulates (no cycle
constraints, no solver), so Lodestar fails closed for LP-round requests unless a valid
external `LpSolution` is injected. `calyx-paths`:
`AssocGraph` (CSR adjacency), `reach` (bidirectional BFS), `reach_scored` (weighted
best-first, `score┬Ę0.9^hops`).

### 7.14 calyx-hazard-soak + calyx-testkit ([18_hazard_soak_and_testkit.md](18_hazard_soak_and_testkit.md))
`calyx-hazard-soak`: a fault-injection binary (PH59 suite) with 25 hazard probes (write
amplification, memtable stall, tombstone buildup, fsync spikes, VRAM-OOM, clock skew,
secret leakage, DR drill, ŌĆ”) plus a long integrated soak (`DEFAULT_SOAK_OPS =
10_000_000`, seed `0xCA1A_0059`) asserting bounded RSS/VRAM growth. `calyx-testkit`:
deterministic scaffolding ŌĆö `DEFAULT_TEST_SEED = 0xCA1A_CAFE_D15C_1A11`, `DEFAULT_TEST_TS
= 1_785_500_000`, `seeded_rng`, `fixed_clock`, proptest strategies.

### 7.15 Entry points ŌĆö calyx-cli, calyxd, calyx-mcp, calyx-web-api ([19](19_mcp_api_tools_reference.md), [20](20_cli_and_daemon_reference.md), [25](25_web_api.md))
Thin surfaces over the engine. The CLI hand-parses args and returns JSON error envelopes;
`calyxd` runs startup probes (T02 CUDA preflight, T03 NVML VRAM budget Ōēż30000 MiB, T04
health, T05 loopback MCP transport) and serves `/metrics`; `calyx-mcp` exposes 31 tools
over stdio JSON-RPC with no auth/consent gate (vault resolution via `CALYX_HOME`);
`calyx-web-api` (issue #889) serves 6 read-only `/v1/*` routes on loopback `127.0.0.1:8121`
behind a fail-closed shared-secret bearer auth, per-request body/rate/timeout guardrails,
and a bounded TTL response cache (doc 25). Both the CLI and `calyx-web-api` route searches
through the shared `calyx-search` crate (issue #573).

---

## 8. Versions & invariants snapshot

| Item | Value |
|---|---|
| Workspace version | `0.1.0` (all crates) |
| Rust edition / toolchain | 2024 / `1.95.0` (pinned) |
| License | BSL 1.1 (auto-converts to Apache-2.0 four years post-release) |
| WAL format | `CXW1`, 20-byte header, CRC32, group-commit window 2 ms |
| SSTable format | `CXS1`, VERSION 2 (legacy 1) |
| Arrow column format | `CXA1`, VERSION 1 |
| Manifest format | JSON, `ManifestVersion{major=1, minor=0}` |
| Lodestar kernel artifact | `FORMAT_VERSION = 1` |
| DiskANN graph | `CLXDA001`, 4 KiB pages |
| Column families | 33 static (+ parameterized slot CFs) |
| Core error catalog | 38 codes (`CalyxErrorCode`, pinned by test) |
| MCP tools | 31 (pinned by test) |
| Crates | 24 (adds `calyx-poly`, `calyx-buildinfo`, `calyx-fsv`, `calyx-search`, `calyx-web-api`) |
| HTTP API bind | `127.0.0.1:8121` (`calyx-web-api`, loopback only) |
| Default daemon bind | `127.0.0.1:7700` (loopback only) |
| Default VRAM soft cap | 12 GiB (Forge); daemon `vram_budget_mib` 1..=30000 |

---

## 9. Gaps / not covered (system-level)

- **Skeleton/stub markers in shipped code**: Aster `lib.rs` self-describes as a
  "skeleton"; compaction cadence is a fixed `FIXME(PH46)`.
- **GPU is opt-in and fail-loud**: default builds are CPU-only; in server mode CUDA
  absence fails loudly rather than falling back.
- **Unwired/partial paths**: the MCP-over-socket transport in `calyxd` is library-complete
  but not served by the live daemon; the LP solver for kernel DFVS is not wired
  (LP requests fail closed unless a valid external solution is supplied); multimodal/commissioned
  lenses emit hash projections, not learned vectors; `AnnealHook` is an interim pre-PH48
  shim. (The CLI/MCP-vs-web-API search split has since been resolved: the CLI and
  `calyx-web-api` now share one ranking path via the extracted `calyx-search` crate, issue
  #573/#900; vector fusion itself remains fail-closed until `PlanStep::VectorFusion` is
  wired to real slot indexes.)
- **No code-coverage tooling** exists in the repo (see [21_test_suite.md](21_test_suite.md)).
- **Design-vs-code divergences** (e.g. column-family numbering in the PRD vs implemented
  tags, Loom interaction being Hadamard-only) are captured in the relevant per-subsystem
  docs and in [24_roadmap.md](24_roadmap.md).
- Detailed remaining work and open issues: see [24_roadmap.md](24_roadmap.md). Design
  intent vs implementation: see [23_planning_docs_summary.md](23_planning_docs_summary.md).

<!-- ===== END 01_system_overview.md ===== -->

# 02 ŌĆö Source Code Map

This document is the **map** of the Calyx Rust workspace at `C:\code\Calyx-Dev`: the
top-level directory layout, the complete per-crate source-file tree with a one-line
description for every `.rs` file under `crates/*/src/`, the inter-crate dependency
graph, entry-point traces, and the build/package configuration.

Per-crate internals (algorithms, struct fields, error taxonomies) are documented in
docs 05ŌĆō20; this document cross-references them rather than re-describing logic. See
[01_system_overview.md](01_system_overview.md) for the architecture narrative and
[00_INDEX.md](00_INDEX.md) for the full index.

**Source files covered:** every `.rs` file under `crates/*/src/` (877 files across 19
crates), plus `Cargo.toml` (workspace + per-crate), `rust-toolchain.toml`,
`fuzz/Cargo.toml` + `fuzz/fuzz_targets/*.rs`, and `infra/aiwonder/**`.

> **Baseline note (refresh through `57fcd478`, 2026-07-07).** The detailed per-crate file
> tree (┬¦3), the file totals (877), and the dependency-edge count (103) below reflect the
> original `2e7b9a2` snapshot and have **not** been re-enumerated. Since that baseline the
> workspace has grown to **23 crates / 1,577 in-`src/` `.rs` files** (tracked count at
> `57fcd478`, up from ~1,460 at `ab86c430`): four crates were added ŌĆö `calyx-search` (issue
> #573/#900, the shared CLI+web-API search path), `calyx-web-api` (issue #889, the
> read-only HTTP `/v1/*` surface, see [25_web_api.md](25_web_api.md)), `calyx-buildinfo`
> (issue #1108, embedded build identity), and `calyx-fsv` (issue #1014, canonical FSV
> evidence-root resolution) ŌĆö and existing crates gained source. The largest growth since
> `ab86c430` is in **`calyx-cli`** (now ~593 `.rs` files), which absorbed the biomedical
> **discovery pipeline** (typed association mining, hypothesis assembly / falsification /
> evaluation, ledger-sealed discovery-run manifests, external drug-combination source
> mining) and the **database-native association state** migration (A37 admission, partitioned
> RRF truth/plans/reports, `stream-fbin`, i8bin label anchors, and the lens catalog all moved
> into Aster CFs). `calyx-aster`, `calyx-registry`, `calyx-assay`, and `calyx-forge` also
> gained source (graph-CSR binary persistence, ONNX/CUDA-13.3/FP16 embedder runtime, KSG
> estimator fixes, GDELT lenses). Treat the tables below as the `2e7b9a2` map; the newer
> crates and their interfaces are documented in docs 01, 17, 20, and 25.
>
> **Current-count correction (0d4fa6f1):** the workspace now has **25 crates** and **1,869**
> tracked `.rs` files under `crates/*/src/`. The extra current crates beyond the older snapshot include `calyx-poly` and `calyx-web-api`; current
> interfaces are summarized in the current-state patch, `docs/poly-import.md`, and
> `docs/medicalsearch/109_biomedical_blindspot_audit.md`.

> **Method note.** The per-file descriptions in ┬¦3 were generated mechanically by
> extracting the first module-doc comment (`//!`) from each file; where absent, the
> first top-of-file item-doc (`///`, marked `(item-doc)`) was used; where neither
> exists the line is derived from the file/module name and marked `(no doc comment)`.
> Of the 877 files, 293 carry a module `//!` doc, 14 a top item `///` doc, and 570
> have no top-of-file doc comment. The map reports WHAT IS present, not intent.

> **Count note.** The dispatch brief cites ~1174 `.rs` files; that count includes
> `tests/`, `benches/`, `examples/`, `build.rs`, and `fuzz/` files outside `src/`.
> This map enumerates the **877** files under `crates/*/src/` (the in-crate source
> tree). The fuzz targets are listed separately in ┬¦6.3.

---

## 1. Workspace layout

The repository root (`C:\code\Calyx-Dev`) is a Cargo workspace (`resolver = "2"`,
`members = ["crates/*"]`, edition 2024, rust-version 1.95). Top-level entries:

| Path | Purpose (as observed in the tree) |
|------|------------------------------------|
| `crates/` | The 19 workspace member crates (all source code). See ┬¦3. |
| `docs/` | Original design/planning material: `dbprdplans/` (PRD plans), `implementation/` (build/impl notes incl. `02_BUILD_PERFORMANCE.md`), `systemspecs/`. |
| `docs2/` | Loose prose/PDF design essays and operator guides (`releaseguide.md`, `infisical-secrets-guide.md`, prompt docs, `*.pdf`). Not part of the numbered reference. |
| `scripts/` | Shell scripts: dataset acquisition (`acquire_*.sh`), build setup (`aiwonder-build-setup.sh`), CI/gate helpers (`check.sh`, `check_manifest_coverage.sh`, `fsv_*.sh`), `dataset_acquire_lib.sh`. |
| `tools/` | Auxiliary tooling; currently `tools/lensforge/` (lens-conversion tooling). |
| `infra/` | Deployment/ops for the `aiwonder` host: systemd units, Prometheus/Grafana/Alertmanager config, restic backup units, ZFS provisioning/scrub scripts, secrets-loader map. See ┬¦6.4. |
| `fuzz/` | `cargo-fuzz` package (`calyx-fuzz`, separate `[workspace]`) with 6 libFuzzer targets. See ┬¦6.3. |
| `datasets/` | Dataset manifest (`MANIFEST.md`); actual data acquired via `scripts/acquire_*.sh`. |
| `assets/` | PNG marketing/diagram images (`hero.png`, `ledger.png`, `oracle.png`, `ward-guard.png`, etc.). |
| `.github/` | `workflows/` ŌĆö CI definitions. |
| `.githooks/` | `pre-push` git hook. |
| `.cargo/` | `config.toml` ŌĆö cargo config (kept machine-agnostic per the workspace `Cargo.toml` comment; linker/incremental are machine-local). |
| `.config/` | `nextest.toml` ŌĆö cargo-nextest test-runner config. |
| `target/` | Build output (shared workspace target dir). |
| `Cargo.toml`, `Cargo.lock` | Workspace manifest + lockfile. See ┬¦6.1. |
| `rust-toolchain.toml` | Pins toolchain `1.95.0`, `profile = minimal`, components `clippy` + `rustfmt`. |
| `env.sh` | Environment bootstrap script. |
| `README.md`, `CONTRIBUTING.md`, `LICENSE` | Standard repo docs. |

### 1.1 Binaries produced

Four executables are built from the workspace. Each is declared with an explicit
`[[bin]]` name and a `src/main.rs` in its crate:

| Binary name | Producing crate | `main.rs` | Role |
|-------------|-----------------|-----------|------|
| `calyx` | `calyx-cli` | `crates/calyx-cli/src/main.rs` | The command-line tool: ingest, search, readbacks, ops, migrate, verify-restore. See [20_cli_and_daemon_reference.md](20_cli_and_daemon_reference.md). |
| `calyxd` | `calyxd` | `crates/calyxd/src/main.rs` | The daemon: loopback `/metrics` Prometheus endpoint driven by a periodic Ledger chain-verify loop. See [20_cli_and_daemon_reference.md](20_cli_and_daemon_reference.md). |
| `calyx-mcp` | `calyx-mcp` | `crates/calyx-mcp/src/main.rs` | The MCP stdio server: newline-delimited JSON-RPC over stdin/stdout. See [19_mcp_api_tools_reference.md](19_mcp_api_tools_reference.md). |
| `calyx-hazard-soak` | `calyx-hazard-soak` | `crates/calyx-hazard-soak/src/main.rs` | The 25-hazard soak harness driver. See [18_hazard_soak_and_testkit.md](18_hazard_soak_and_testkit.md). |

- `novelty.rs` ŌĆö Novelty routing for failed Ward verdicts.
- `polis.rs` ŌĆö Polis civic-panel guard validation over deterministic synthetic personas.
- `profile.rs` ŌĆö Guard profile configuration shared by Ward guard calls.
- `query.rs` ŌĆö Incoming-query Ward guard over trusted regions.
- `required.rs` ŌĆö Assay-bit derived required-slot selection for Ward profiles.
- `speaker_lens.rs` ŌĆö WavLM speaker lens adapter for PH39 identity slots.
- `style_lens.rs` ŌĆö RoBERTa style lens adapter for PH39 identity slots.
- `verdict.rs` ŌĆö Structured verdicts emitted by Ward guard calls.

#### calyxd

- `config.rs` ŌĆö CalyxConfig ŌĆö the single authoritative runtime configuration for calyxd.
- `cuda_probe.rs` ŌĆö CUDA device preflight for calyxd (PH65 ┬Ę T02).
- `error.rs` ŌĆö Daemon error taxonomy mapping to stable CALYX_* codes (PH65).
- `health.rs` ŌĆö PH65 ┬Ę T04 ŌĆö calyxd daemon-readiness healthcheck.
- `lib.rs` ŌĆö calyxd library surface.
- `main.rs` ŌĆö Calyx daemon: Ledger chain-verify metrics on a loopback /metrics endpoint.
- `mcp_server.rs` ŌĆö Loopback-only MCP-over-socket transport for calyxd (PH65 ┬Ę T05).
- `metrics.rs` ŌĆö Prometheus registry for the Ledger chain-verify gauge family (PH66, issue #602).
- `metrics/calyx.rs` ŌĆö CalyxMetrics: the full daemon /metrics surface (PH66 T03, issue #538).
- `metrics/hazards.rs` ŌĆö The PH59 25-hazard register exposed as one gauge per hazard (PH66 T03).
- `metrics/zfs.rs` ŌĆö ZFS integrity metric collector for calyxd (issue #729).
- `server.rs` ŌĆö Loopback-only HTTP listener serving GET /metrics (PH65 bind rules).
- `startup.rs` ŌĆö startup module (no doc comment)
- `verify.rs` ŌĆö calyx verify-restore ŌĆö byte-level read-back verification of a restored vault.
- `verify_loop.rs` ŌĆö Periodic Ledger chain-verify cycle feeding the chain-verify gauge family.

> `calyx-cli` is the largest crate (183 src files) and is enumerated in full at ┬¦3
> above under the **calyx-cli** heading.

<!-- END GENERATED TREE -->

| **calyx-core** | **0** | **18** |

### 4.3 Foundation crates and leaf entry points

- **Foundation crates** (depended on by the most crates, lowest layer):
  - `calyx-core` ŌĆö **0 internal deps**, depended on by **18** of the other 18 crates
    (every crate). It is the universal foundation: ids, error catalog, data model,
    shared traits/enums. See [05_core.md](05_core.md).
  - `calyx-paths` ŌĆö only depends on `calyx-core`; depended on by 8 crates. With
    `calyx-core` it forms the second foundation layer (graph/path primitives). See
    [17_graph_mincut_paths.md](17_graph_mincut_paths.md).
  - `calyx-ledger` (in-deg 13) and `calyx-forge` (in-deg 11) are also near-foundational:
    each depends only on `calyx-core` and is pulled in by most engine crates.
- **Leaf entry points** (out-deg high, in-deg 0 ŌĆö nothing depends on them):
  - `calyx-cli` (out-deg 13), `calyxd` (out-deg 5), `calyx-hazard-soak` (out-deg 7).
    `calyx-mcp` is a near-leaf: its only consumer is `calyxd` (in-deg 1), which embeds
    the MCP server over a loopback socket.
- **Cycle note.** No `calyx-*` build cycle exists in `[dependencies]` (Cargo would
  reject it). `calyx-assay -> calyx-oracle`/`calyx-sextant`/`calyx-lodestar` and the
  reverse `calyx-oracle -> calyx-assay`, `calyx-sextant -> calyx-oracle`,
  `calyx-lodestar -> calyx-sextant` appear in the edge list because some of these are
  **dev-dependencies** (test-only), not normal build dependencies. The normal-build
  layering remains acyclic; the apparent back-edges are test wiring.

## 5. Entry-point traces

High-level traces from each binary's `main` through its top modules to the crates it
pulls in. Detailed command/tool surfaces are in
[19_mcp_api_tools_reference.md](19_mcp_api_tools_reference.md) and
[20_cli_and_daemon_reference.md](20_cli_and_daemon_reference.md).

### 5.1 `calyx` ŌĆö `crates/calyx-cli/src/main.rs`

```
main()  ŌåÆ  entry::main()           (crates/calyx-cli/src/entry.rs)
  Ōö£ŌöĆ verify_restore::try_run       ŌĆö short-circuits `verify-restore` (PH67 T03)
  Ōö£ŌöĆ healthcheck_daemon::try_run   ŌĆö short-circuits `healthcheck --config` (PH65 T04)
  Ōö£ŌöĆ cmd::try_run                  ŌĆö structured subcommand table (crates/calyx-cli/src/cmd/)
  Ōöé      Ōö£ŌöĆ cmd/ingest             ŌåÆ calyx-aster, calyx-registry, calyx-loom, calyx-ledger
  Ōöé      Ōö£ŌöĆ cmd/search             ŌåÆ calyx-sextant, calyx-ward, calyx-oracle
  Ōöé      Ōö£ŌöĆ cmd/intelligence       ŌåÆ calyx-assay, calyx-anneal, calyx-lodestar, calyx-oracle
  Ōöé      Ōö£ŌöĆ cmd/provenance         ŌåÆ calyx-ledger
  Ōöé      ŌööŌöĆ cmd/readback, vault, healthcheck
  ŌööŌöĆ dispatch::run                 ŌĆö legacy/flat dispatch for remaining readbacks
         (anneal_*, oracle_*, sextant_*, lodestar_*, media_*, temporal_*, ph42_*, ŌĆ”)
```

`main.rs` declares ~110 sibling modules (anneal readbacks, oracle readbacks, sextant
validation harnesses, leapable dual-write/shadow harnesses, migrate, ops, navigate,
merkle, etc.). Error handling routes through `error.rs` (`CliError::emit()` ŌåÆ stable
`ExitCode`). The crate links all 13 engine crates (see ┬¦4.1) ŌĆö it is the broadest
consumer in the workspace.

### 5.2 `calyxd` ŌĆö `crates/calyxd/src/main.rs`

```
#[tokio::main] main()             (crates/calyxd/src/main.rs)
  Ōö£ŌöĆ parse_args                    ŌĆö --vault/--ledger/--bind/--interval-secs/--once/--config/--validate-config/--audit-vram
  Ōö£ŌöĆ startup::validate_config      (crates/calyxd/src/startup.rs)  ŌåÆ calyxd::config::CalyxConfig
  Ōö£ŌöĆ verify_loop::run_cycle        ŌĆö synchronous first Ledger chain-verify before bind
  Ōöé      ŌööŌöĆ uses calyx_aster::ledger_view  ŌåÆ calyx-aster, calyx-ledger
  Ōö£ŌöĆ calyxd::metrics::CalyxMetrics ŌĆö Prometheus registry (chain-verify + 25-hazard + ZFS)
  Ōö£ŌöĆ calyxd::server::MetricsServer ŌĆö loopback-only GET /metrics
  ŌööŌöĆ verify_loop::spawn_loop       ŌĆö periodic re-verify, fed by CancellationToken
```

Library modules consumed (single source of truth, also reused by `calyx-cli` and the
healthcheck): `config`, `cuda_probe` (ŌåÆ uses Forge/CUDA preflight), `error`, `health`,
`mcp_server` (embeds `calyx-mcp`), `metrics` (+`metrics/calyx.rs`, `metrics/hazards.rs`,
`metrics/zfs.rs`), `server`, `verify`, `vram`. Crates pulled in: `calyx-core`,
`calyx-aster`, `calyx-forge`, `calyx-ledger`, `calyx-mcp`.

### 5.3 `calyx-mcp` ŌĆö `crates/calyx-mcp/src/main.rs`

```
main()                            (crates/calyx-mcp/src/main.rs)
  Ōö£ŌöĆ McpServer::new                (crates/calyx-mcp/src/server.rs)
  Ōö£ŌöĆ tools::register_all           (crates/calyx-mcp/src/tools/mod.rs)
  Ōöé      Ōö£ŌöĆ tools/vault            ŌåÆ calyx-aster, calyx-registry  (PH63 T02)
  Ōöé      Ōö£ŌöĆ tools/ingest           ŌåÆ calyx-aster, calyx-loom      (PH63 T03)
  Ōöé      Ōö£ŌöĆ tools/search           ŌåÆ calyx-sextant, calyx-ward    (PH63 T04)
  Ōöé      Ōö£ŌöĆ tools/intelligence     ŌåÆ calyx-anneal, calyx-assay*   (PH63 T06)
  Ōöé      ŌööŌöĆ tools/provenance       ŌåÆ calyx-ledger                 (PH63 T07)
  ŌööŌöĆ stdin loop:
         decode_jsonrpc_request  (jsonrpc.rs)  ŌåÆ  server.dispatch  ŌåÆ  serde_json ŌåÆ stdout
```

stdout is reserved for JSON-RPC responses; all diagnostics go to stderr. Notifications
(no `id`) receive no reply. Crates pulled in: `calyx-core`, `calyx-aster`,
`calyx-ledger`, `calyx-loom`, `calyx-paths`, `calyx-registry`, `calyx-sextant`,
`calyx-ward`, `calyx-anneal`.

## 6. Build / package configuration

### 6.1 Workspace `Cargo.toml`

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| `[workspace] resolver` | `"2"` |
| `members` | `["crates/*"]` (globs all 19 crates) |
| `[workspace.package] version` | `0.1.0` |
| `edition` | `2024` |
| `rust-version` | `1.95` |
| `repository` | `https://github.com/ChrisRoyse/Calyx` |
| `publish` | `false` |

`[workspace.dependencies]` pins the shared third-party stack (versions as written):
`aes-gcm 0.10`, `blake3 1`, `bincode` (= `bincode_reloaded 3.1.6`, serde feature),
`ciborium 0.2`, `crc32fast 1`, `criterion 0.5`, `cudarc 0.19.7` (no default features),
`ed25519-dalek 2`, `filetime 0.2`, `hkdf 0.12`, `memmap2 0.9`, `nix 0.30` (fs only),
`prometheus 0.14` (no defaults), `proptest 1`, `rand 0.8`, `rand_chacha 0.3`,
`rayon 1`, `nvml-wrapper 0.10`, `rusqlite 0.40.1` (bundled), `serde 1` (derive),
`serde_json 1`, `sha2 0.10`, `thiserror 2`, `tokio 1`, `tokio-util 0.7`, `toml 0.8`,
`tracing 0.1`, `tracing-subscriber 0.3`, `ulid 1` (serde), `uuid 1` (serde), `wide 1`,
`zeroize 1`, `zstd 0.13`.

**Build profiles** (tuned to shrink the shared `target/` dir for the multi-agent build
cadence; per the in-file comment, the cargo default `debug = 2` ballooned `target/` to
~190 GB):

| Profile | Setting | Effect |
|---------|---------|--------|
| `[profile.dev]` | `debug = "line-tables-only"` | First-party crates keep function names + file:line in backtraces; no full DWARF. |
| `[profile.dev.package."*"]` | `debug = false` | Dependencies get no debuginfo (largest `target/` size reduction). |

No custom `[profile.release]` is set in the workspace `Cargo.toml` (cargo defaults
apply). Linker (mold) and incremental policy are machine-local (see
`docs/implementation/02_BUILD_PERFORMANCE.md`, referenced in the manifest comment).

### 6.2 `rust-toolchain.toml`

```toml
[toolchain]
channel = "1.95.0"
profile = "minimal"
components = ["clippy", "rustfmt"]
```

### 6.3 Fuzz targets (`fuzz/`)

`fuzz/Cargo.toml` is a standalone `cargo-fuzz` package (`name = "calyx-fuzz"`,
`edition = 2024`, `publish = false`, its own `[workspace]` so it is excluded from the
main workspace; `[package.metadata] cargo-fuzz = true`). It depends on path crates
`calyx-aster`, `calyx-core`, `calyx-mcp`, `calyx-sextant`, plus `libfuzzer-sys 0.4` and
`serde_json 1`. Six libFuzzer targets (each `[[bin]]` with `test/doc/bench = false`):

| Target | Path | Exercises |
|--------|------|-----------|
| `aster_sst_decode` | `fuzz_targets/aster_sst_decode.rs` | Aster SST block decode. |
| `aster_wal_replay` | `fuzz_targets/aster_wal_replay.rs` | WAL record framing / replay. |
| `aster_manifest_decode` | `fuzz_targets/aster_manifest_decode.rs` | Manifest decode/recovery. |
| `query_parse` | `fuzz_targets/query_parse.rs` | Sextant query parsing. |
| `lens_output_decode` | `fuzz_targets/lens_output_decode.rs` | Lens runtime output decode. |
| `mcp_jsonrpc_decode` | `fuzz_targets/mcp_jsonrpc_decode.rs` | MCP JSON-RPC wire decode. |

### 6.4 `infra/` (operations for the `aiwonder` host)

All units are repo-owned and operator-installed (non-root, loopback-bound). Contents:

| Path | What it is |
|------|------------|
| `infra/aiwonder/systemd/calyxd.service` | systemd unit for `calyxd` (PH66 T01, #536). Runs `User=croyse`, loads `/run/leapable/secrets/calyx.env`, `ExecStart=ŌĆ”/calyxd --config ŌĆ”/calyx.toml`, `ExecStartPost=ŌĆ”/calyx healthcheck --wait 30`, `Restart=on-failure`, `LimitNOFILE=1048576`. After `network-online.target` + `leapable-secrets-load.service`. |
| `infra/aiwonder/backup/calyx-backup.service` | restic backup unit (PH67 T02). |
| `infra/aiwonder/backup/calyx-backup.timer` | Hourly restic backup timer (#542): `OnCalendar=hourly`, `Persistent=true`, `RandomizedDelaySec=300`. RPO = 1h. Requires the `.service`. |
| `infra/aiwonder/backup/restic-backup.sh`, `restic-restore.sh`, `zfs-snapshot.sh` | Backup/restore + ZFS snapshot scripts. |
| `infra/aiwonder/backup/dr-drill-runbook.md`, `README.md` | DR drill runbook (PH67 T04) + backup README. |
| `infra/aiwonder/calyx.toml` | The deployed runtime config consumed by `calyxd --config` (parsed by `calyxd::config::CalyxConfig`). See [03_configuration.md](03_configuration.md). |
| `infra/aiwonder/prometheus/calyx-scrape.yml` | Prometheus scrape config for the `calyxd` `/metrics` endpoint. |
| `infra/aiwonder/grafana/calyx-dashboard.json` | Grafana dashboard. |
| `infra/aiwonder/alertmanager/calyx-alerts.yml`, `calyx-alerts.test.yml` | Alertmanager rules + test. |
| `infra/aiwonder/bin/*.sh` | Healthcheck (`calyx-aiwonder-healthcheck.sh`), deploy-wiring installer, ZFS integrity verifier. |
| `infra/aiwonder/ops/*.sh` | Service install, ZFS provisioning/scrub, bitrot FSV, data relocation. |
| `infra/aiwonder/secrets-loader/calyx.env.map.json` | Secrets-loader env mapping (Infisical ŌåÆ `calyx.env`). |

There are **no `*.service`/`*.timer` files outside `infra/aiwonder/`**, and the systemd
units target the `aiwonder` host only.

## 7. Gaps / not covered

- This is a **map**, not a behavioral spec: it does not enumerate struct fields,
  function signatures, error variants, or algorithm steps. Those live in docs 04ŌĆō20.
- 570 of 877 source files have no top-of-file doc comment; their one-liners are
  **derived from the file/module name** and explicitly marked `(no doc comment)`. They
  describe the file's likely role from naming only, not from reading the body.
- The `~1174 .rs` figure in the dispatch brief includes files outside `crates/*/src/`
  (`tests/`, `benches/`, `examples/`, `build.rs`, and the 6 `fuzz_targets/`). This map
  covers the **877** in-`src/` files plus the fuzz targets (┬¦6.3). The full external
  test inventory is in [21_test_suite.md](21_test_suite.md).
- Stub/aspirational markers (`todo!()`, unimplemented paths) are noted in the
  per-subsystem docs, not here. One naming signal visible in the tree:
  `calyx-sextant/src/query/ask.rs` advertises "PH33/PH49-compatible **stubs**".
