## 1. Crate layout and public surface

`lib.rs` declares 13 public modules (`alloc`, `cache`, `cold_start`, `consent`, `cosine`,
`enums`, `error`, `ids`, `model`, `security`, `temporal`, `time`, `traits`) and re-exports
their main types at the crate root. The only test in `lib.rs` asserts
`env!("CARGO_PKG_NAME") == "calyx-core"`.

### 1.1 Cargo.toml ŌĆö dependencies and features

Source: `crates/calyx-core/Cargo.toml`. Package version/edition/rust-version inherited from
the workspace (edition 2024, toolchain 1.95 per `_SPEC.md`).

| Dependency | Workspace version | Used for |
|---|---|---|
| `blake3` | "1" | content-addressing (`content_address`), FSV checksums |
| `rand` | "0.8" | TTL jitter RNG (`Rng`) |
| `rand_chacha` | "0.3" | `ChaCha8Rng` seeded jitter |
| `serde` | "1" (derive) | all (de)serialization |
| `thiserror` | "2" | `CalyxError` derive |
| `tracing` | ŌĆö | `CALYX_CACHE_EVICTED` debug events |
| `ulid` | "1" (serde) | `VaultId` |

Dev-dependencies: `proptest`, `serde_json`.

**Feature flags: none.** `calyx-core/Cargo.toml` declares no `[features]` table. Note the
workspace exposes `bincode`/`uuid`, but `calyx-core` itself does **not** depend on them ŌĆö its
serialization is serde-driven and the on-the-wire encodings exercised in tests are JSON. No
`bincode`/`ciborium` usage appears in this crate.

---

## 2. Identifiers and content-addressing (`ids.rs`)

Constant `ID_BYTES = 16`; hex display width `HEX_CHARS = 32`.

### 2.1 ID types

| Type | Underlying | Display form | Generation / format |
|---|---|---|---|
| `VaultId(pub Ulid)` | 128-bit ULID | ULID Crockford-base32 string | Wraps an externally-minted `Ulid`; stable for the life of a vault. `from_ulid`, `as_ulid`. |
| `LensId(pub [u8;16])` | 16 raw bytes | 32-char lowercase hex | Content-addressed (BLAKE3) from lens spec; see 2.2. |
| `CxId(pub [u8;16])` | 16 raw bytes | 32-char lowercase hex | Content-addressed (BLAKE3) from input + panel version + vault salt; see 2.3. |
| `SlotId(pub u16)` | `u16` | decimal | Compact stable panel index. `serde(transparent)`. `new`, `get`, `with_key`. |
| `SlotKey { id: SlotId, key: String }` | ŌĆö | ŌĆö | Pairs a `SlotId` with a stable human-readable key. Accessors `id()`, `key()`. |

`LensId` and `CxId` are generated by the `hex_id!` macro, which provides `from_bytes`,
`to_bytes`, `as_bytes`, `Debug` (tuple of lowercase hex), `Display` (lowercase hex),
`FromStr` (via `parse_hex_16`), and serde as a hex **string**. `VaultId` serializes via its
ULID string; `SlotId` is a transparent `u16`. All ID types derive
`Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, PartialOrd, Ord, Hash` (`SlotKey` is not `Copy` and lacks
`Ord`/`PartialOrd`).

### 2.2 `LensId::from_parts`

```
LensId = content_address([ name.as_bytes(), weights_sha256, corpus_hash, output_shape ])
```

Identical lens specs (name + weights hash + corpus hash + output shape) yield the same id
across vaults. Test `lens_id_is_deterministic_on_raw_bytes` confirms determinism and that
changing `output_shape` changes the id.

### 2.3 `CxId::from_input`

```
CxId = content_address([ input_bytes, panel_version.to_be_bytes(), vault_salt ])
```

`panel_version: u32` is encoded big-endian. Determinism and panel-version sensitivity are
pinned by `cx_id_is_deterministic_on_raw_bytes`.

### 2.4 `content_address` ŌĆö the hash formula

`pub fn content_address<I,P>(parts) -> [u8;16]`. Steps:

1. `blake3::Hasher::new()`.
2. For each part in order: update with `(part.len() as u64).to_be_bytes()` (8-byte big-endian
   length prefix), then update with the part bytes. This **length-delimits** each part so
   `["ab","c"]` and `["a","bc"]` hash differently (`content_address_is_length_delimited`).
3. Take the first 16 bytes of the 32-byte BLAKE3 digest.

So all Calyx content addresses are a **128-bit BLAKE3 prefix over length-delimited ordered
byte parts**.

### 2.5 `ParseIdError`

| Variant | Raised when |
|---|---|
| `InvalidLength { expected, actual }` | hex string length != 32 |
| `InvalidHex { index }` | non-hex byte at the given byte index |
| `InvalidUlid` | `VaultId::from_str` got a non-ULID string |
| `InvalidSlotId` | `SlotId::from_str` got a non-`u16` |

Implements `Display` + `std::error::Error`. Helper `parse_hex_16` accepts both upper- and
lowercase hex; `hex_lower` emits lowercase. Proptests round-trip every ID through
DisplayŌåöFromStr and serde-JSON.

---

## 3. Error taxonomy ŌĆö the closed `CALYX_*` catalog (`error.rs`)

### 3.1 Root types

- **`CalyxError`** ŌĆö the error-taxonomy **root type**. Fields:

  | Field | Type | Meaning |
  |---|---|---|
  | `code` | `&'static str` | stable `CALYX_*` wire code |
  | `message` | `String` | concrete failure detail |
  | `remediation` | `&'static str` | stable remediation text |

  Derives `Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize` and `thiserror::Error` with
  `#[error("{code}: {message}")]`. It is **not `Deserialize`** (the `remediation`/`code` are
  static). Wire JSON shape is exactly
  `{"code":...,"message":...,"remediation":...}` (`error_serializes_to_wire_shape`).

- **`type Result<T> = std::result::Result<T, CalyxError>`** ŌĆö crate-wide result alias.

- **`CalyxErrorCode`** ŌĆö closed `enum` of the PRD-18 codes (derives
  `Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Hash`). Methods: `code() -> &'static str`,
  `meaning() -> &'static str`, `remediation() -> &'static str`, `error(msg) -> CalyxError`.

- **`CALYX_ERROR_CODES: &[CalyxErrorCode]`** ŌĆö every catalog code in PRD-18 order.

- **`CalyxWarning`** ŌĆö non-fatal warning enum, `#[serde(tag="code", rename_all="snake_case")]`,
  one variant `Unprovenanced { surface: String }` (constructor `unprovenanced`). Derives
  `Serialize` **and** `Deserialize`.

The `error_catalog!` macro generates the enum, the `CALYX_ERROR_CODES` slice, the three
`const fn` lookups, an `error(msg)` builder per code, and a snake_case constructor on
`CalyxError` per code (e.g. `CalyxError::lens_dim_mismatch("...")`). `CalyxError::from_code`
attaches the catalog remediation automatically.

### 3.2 The closed catalog (PRD-18, in order)

The unit test `catalog_matches_prd_18_exactly` pins this exact list and order. Each row:
wire code, constructor, PRD meaning, PRD remediation.

| # | Wire code | Constructor | Meaning (when raised) | Remediation |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | `CALYX_LENS_FROZEN_VIOLATION` | `lens_frozen_violation` | weights hash != registered | re-register as new LensId |
| 2 | `CALYX_LENS_DIM_MISMATCH` | `lens_dim_mismatch` | output dim != Slot.shape | fix lens or slot shape |
| 3 | `CALYX_LENS_NUMERICAL_INVARIANT` | `lens_numerical_invariant` | NaN/Inf/non-unit output | check lens runtime/normalize |
| 4 | `CALYX_LENS_UNREACHABLE` | `lens_unreachable` | runtime endpoint down | restore lens service |
| 5 | `CALYX_REGISTRY_DUPLICATE` | `registry_duplicate` | lens id already registered | reuse existing LensId or register a distinct frozen spec |
| 6 | `CALYX_REGISTRY_UNAVAILABLE` | `registry_unavailable` | lens registry unavailable | restore registry before guarded anneal update |
| 7 | `CALYX_ASSAY_INSUFFICIENT_SAMPLES` | `assay_insufficient_samples` | < quorum (50) anchors | anchor more outcomes |
| 8 | `CALYX_ASSAY_LOW_SIGNAL` | `assay_low_signal` | lens < 0.05 bits | park/retire lens |
| 9 | `CALYX_ASSAY_REDUNDANT` | `assay_redundant` | pair corr > 0.6 | drop duplicate lens |
| 10 | `CALYX_KERNEL_UNGROUNDED` | `kernel_ungrounded` | kernel over ungrounded graph | add anchors (grounding_gaps) |
| 11 | `CALYX_GUARD_PROVISIONAL` | `guard_provisional` | tau not calibrated | calibrate before high-stakes use |
| 12 | `CALYX_GUARD_OOD` | `guard_ood` | query/output outside trusted region | new-region or reject per policy |
| 13 | `CALYX_FORGE_NUMERICAL_INVARIANT` | `forge_numerical_invariant` | kernel NaN/Inf | numerical fail-closed |
| 14 | `CALYX_FORGE_DEVICE_UNAVAILABLE` | `forge_device_unavailable` | CUDA init failed (server mode) | fix driver (reboot per gotcha) |
| 15 | `CALYX_ASTER_CORRUPT_SHARD` | `aster_corrupt_shard` | base shard hash mismatch | restore from restic/snapshot |
| 16 | `CALYX_ASTER_TORN_WAL` | `aster_torn_wal` | torn tail on recovery | auto-discarded; logged |
| 17 | `CALYX_LEDGER_CHAIN_BROKEN` | `ledger_chain_broken` | hash-chain verify failed | quarantine range, investigate |
| 18 | `CALYX_LEDGER_CORRUPT` | `ledger_corrupt` | ledger CF integrity violation | ledger CF integrity violation ŌĆö run verify_chain to identify range |
| 19 | `CALYX_LEDGER_APPEND_ONLY_VIOLATION` | `ledger_append_only_violation` | ledger CF append-only invariant violated | ledger CF is append-only; deletes and tombstones are forbidden |
| 20 | `CALYX_LEDGER_SECRET_IN_PAYLOAD` | `ledger_secret_in_payload` | ledger payload contains secret-like material | ledger payload must store hashes/ids only ŌĆö redact before writing |
| 21 | `CALYX_LEDGER_ACTOR_TOO_LONG` | `ledger_actor_too_long` | ledger actor id exceeds 64 UTF-8 bytes | actor id must be <= 64 bytes UTF-8 |
| 22 | `CALYX_LEDGER_GROUP_COMMIT_FAILED` | `ledger_group_commit_failed` | ledger hook failed during group commit | ledger hook failed ŌĆö group-commit rolled back; retry the write |
| 23 | `CALYX_REPRODUCE_NONDETERMINISTIC` | `reproduce_nondeterministic` | reproduce ledger entry lacks determinism seed | no determinism seed in ledger entry - cannot guarantee reproduce fidelity |
| 24 | `CALYX_REPRODUCE_DRIFT_EXCEEDED` | `reproduce_drift_exceeded` | reproduce max_drift exceeded tolerance | reproduce max_drift exceeded 1e-3 - possible lens drift or fusion parameter change |
| 25 | `CALYX_VAULT_ACCESS_DENIED` | `vault_access_denied` | cross-vault read without grant | request grant |
| 26 | `CALYX_ERASE_ALREADY_TOMBSTONED` | `erase_already_tombstoned` | erase scope already has an erasure tombstone | treat as idempotent erasure or inspect ledger tombstone |
| 27 | `CALYX_STALE_DERIVED` | `stale_derived` | fresh required, rebuild pending | retry or accept StaleOk |
| 28 | `CALYX_ORACLE_INSUFFICIENT` | `oracle_insufficient` | I(panel;oracle) < H(Y) - panel can't predict | add outcome/execution lens (propose_lens) |
| 29 | `CALYX_FORGE_VRAM_BUDGET` | `forge_vram_budget` | dispatch exceeds VRAM budget | split batch / raise budget / wait |
| 30 | `CALYX_BACKPRESSURE` | `backpressure` | write/query queue at high-water | retry with backoff |
| 31 | `CALYX_DISK_PRESSURE` | `disk_pressure` | hotpool near full | free/spill to archive; writes fail-closed |
| 32 | `CALYX_QUANT_INTELLIGENCE_LOSS` | `quant_intelligence_loss` | quant level would drop bits/cosine/FAR beyond bound | use a gentler level (A25) |
| 33 | `CALYX_READER_LEASE_EXPIRED` | `reader_lease_expired` | long reader aborted to release MVCC version | re-issue with bounded-staleness snapshot |
| 34 | `CALYX_DATASET_NOT_FOUND` | `dataset_not_found` | dataset dir or MANIFEST row missing | acquire + register via scripts/acquire_datasets.sh |
| 35 | `CALYX_DATASET_CHECKSUM_MISMATCH` | `dataset_checksum_mismatch` | recomputed sha256 != recorded value | re-acquire at the pinned revision; never edit dataset bytes in place |
| 36 | `CALYX_DATASET_ROWCOUNT_MISMATCH` | `dataset_rowcount_mismatch` | recomputed row count != recorded value | re-acquire at the pinned revision; check split/decoder drift |
| 37 | `CALYX_DATASET_MANIFEST_INVALID` | `dataset_manifest_invalid` | MANIFEST.md/manifest.json missing/malformed/drifted | re-register via scripts/verify_dataset.sh register |
| 38 | `CALYX_DATASET_SCHEMA_MISMATCH` | `dataset_schema_mismatch` | dataset columns/fields missing or malformed vs pinned upstream | re-acquire at the pinned revision; check upstream schema drift |

### 3.3 Module-local error codes (NOT in the closed catalog)

The doc-comment in `error.rs` states subsystem-local `CALYX_*` strings live beside their
owning type and build `CalyxError` directly. They are `pub const &str` (not catalog
members); `module_local_codes_are_not_prd_18_catalog_entries` asserts they are absent from
`CALYX_ERROR_CODES`. Those defined inside `calyx-core`:

| Const | Module | Built where | Remediation (in source) |
|---|---|---|---|
| `CALYX_RECORD_SCHEMA_VIOLATION` | `model/validation.rs` | `record_schema_error` | submit a constellation matching the record schema with finite values |
| `CALYX_PROVISIONAL_VAULT` | `cold_start.rs` | `ColdStartGuard::assert_grounded` | record at least one grounded anchor before returning non-provisional high-stakes output |
| `CALYX_CONSENT_VIOLATION` | `consent.rs` | `check_consent` | request only permitted purposes or refresh consent before processing |
| `CALYX_AUTHN_REQUIRED` | `security.rs` | `no_anonymous_write` | present a valid mTLS, Cloudflare Access, or in-process identity before writing |
| `CALYX_TLS_CONFIG_INVALID` | `security.rs` | `TlsConfig::validate` | point cert_pem_path/key_pem_path/ca_pem_path at existing, readable PEM files |
| `CALYX_ALLOC_CAP_EXCEEDED` | `alloc/mod.rs` | `alloc_cap_exceeded` | raise the cap or shrink the working set; allocations fail closed (A26) |
| `CALYX_CACHE_EVICTED` | `cache/lru_ttl.rs` | `tracing::debug!` event (not an error) | n/a ŌĆö structured log event, never a panic/error |
| `CALYX_TEMPORAL_AP60_VIOLATION` | `temporal.rs` | `temporal_error` | keep temporal signals post-retrieval only and never dominant |
| `CALYX_TEMPORAL_INVALID_BOOST_CONFIG` | `temporal.rs` | `temporal_error` | set post-retrieval alpha and causal multipliers within their valid ranges |
| `CALYX_TEMPORAL_INVALID_PERIOD` | `temporal.rs` | `temporal_error` | set target_hour 0..=23 and day_of_week 0..=6 |
| `CALYX_TEMPORAL_INVALID_WINDOW` | `temporal.rs` | (declared; remediation defined, not raised within this crate) | set a non-empty temporal window within i64 bounds |
| `CALYX_TEMPORAL_NEGATIVE_WEIGHT` | `temporal.rs` | `FusionWeights::validate` | use a convex temporal fusion blend with every component >= 0.0 |
| `CALYX_TEMPORAL_WEIGHT_SUM` | `temporal.rs` | `FusionWeights::validate` | normalize recency + sequence + periodic to exactly 1.0 |

The test also lists additional module-local codes owned by **other** crates and not defined
here (`CALYX_MCP_JSONRPC_INVALID`, `CALYX_PII_REDACTION_REQUIRED`, `CALYX_SBOM_PARSE_ERROR`,
`CALYX_SUPPLY_CHAIN_VULN`, `CALYX_LENS_WEIGHT_TAMPERED`, `CALYX_EXTERNAL_CMD_NOT_ALLOWED`).

---

## 4. Shared enum vocabulary (`enums.rs`)

All enums derive serde with `#[serde(rename_all = "snake_case")]`; struct-like variants
serialize as `{"variant_snake": {fields}}`. Round-trip bytes are pinned by
`enum_serialization_bytes_are_stable`.

| Enum | Variants | Notes |
|---|---|---|
| `Modality` | `Text, Code, Image, Audio, Video, Protein, Dna, Molecule, Structured, Mixed` | Variant set locked by `modality_variant_set_is_locked` (snake_case wire names). |
| `SlotShape` | `Dense(u32)`, `Sparse(u32)`, `Multi { token_dim: u32 }` | Physical vector shape a lens slot emits. JSON e.g. `{"dense":768}`, `{"multi":{"token_dim":128}}`. |
| `Asymmetry` | `None`, `Dual { a: SlotId, b: SlotId }` | Directional relation for asymmetric slot pairings. |
| `QuantPolicy` | `None`, `TurboQuant { bits_per_channel_x2: u8 }`, `MxFp4`, `Pq { m: u8, nbits: u8 }`, `Float8`, `Binary` | `bits_per_channel_x2 = 7` means 3.5 bpc. `MxFp4` = Blackwell microscaling FP4 (MXFP8 fallback). `turboquant_default()` returns `TurboQuant{bits_per_channel_x2:7}`. |
| `AnchorKind` | `TestPass, TieFormed, Thumbs, Label(String), Reward, SpeakerMatch, StyleHold, Recurrence` | Grounded outcome axis. Derives `Ord` (used as `BTreeMap` key). |
| `SlotState` | `Active, Parked, Retired` | Slot lifecycle. |
| `AbsentReason` | `NotApplicable, Redacted, LensUnavailable, Deferred, LensInactive, Error(String)` | Explicit reason a slot vector is absent. |

---

## 5. The data model (`model/`)

`model/mod.rs` re-exports all model types and `Ts`. Constellation JSON round-trips are
byte-exact (proptest `constellation_json_roundtrip_is_byte_exact`).

### 5.1 `Constellation` ŌĆö the atomic record (`model/constellation.rs`)

One input measured by one panel of frozen lenses. Derives `Clone, Debug, PartialEq,
Serialize, Deserialize` (no `Eq` ŌĆö contains floats).

| Field | Type | Meaning |
|---|---|---|
| `cx_id` | `CxId` | Content-addressed constellation id. |
| `vault_id` | `VaultId` | Owning vault. |
| `panel_version` | `u32` | Panel version used for this measurement (must be > 0). |
| `created_at` | `Ts` (`u64` ms) | Server-stamped creation timestamp. |
| `input_ref` | `InputRef` | Input hash + optional pointer + redaction flag. |
| `modality` | `Modality` | Input modality. |
| `slots` | `BTreeMap<SlotId, SlotVector>` | Per-slot vectors; absent slots are explicit `SlotVector::Absent`. |
| `scalars` | `BTreeMap<String, f64>` | Scalar measurements derived at ingest. |
| `metadata` | `BTreeMap<String, String>` | Verbatim string identifiers / source metadata. `#[serde(default)]`. |
| `anchors` | `Vec<Anchor>` | Grounded outcomes observed for this input. |
| `provenance` | `LedgerRef` | Ledger entry proving inputŌåÆlensŌåÆconstellation lineage. |
| `flags` | `CxFlags` | Trust / degradation flags. |

Two metadata contract keys (Leapable Vault integration):
`METADATA_CHUNK_ID = "chunk_id"`, `METADATA_DATABASE_NAME = "database_name"`. Accessors:
`metadata_value(key)`, `chunk_id()`, `database_name()`.

`validate_schema()` enforces: `panel_version != 0`; every slot vector valid (delegates to
`SlotVector::validate_schema`, error prefixed `slot {id}: ŌĆ”`); non-empty scalar keys and
finite scalar values; non-empty metadata keys; every anchor valid. All failures use
`CALYX_RECORD_SCHEMA_VIOLATION`.

### 5.2 `SlotVector` and `SparseEntry` (`model/vector.rs`)

`SlotVector` (`snake_case` tagged enum) ŌĆö per-slot payload. Derives `Clone, Debug,
PartialEq, Serialize, Deserialize`.

| Variant | Fields | Meaning |
|---|---|---|
| `Dense` | `dim: u32, data: Vec<f32>` | Dense f32 payload. |
| `Sparse` | `dim: u32, entries: Vec<SparseEntry>` | Sparse payload. |
| `Multi` | `token_dim: u32, tokens: Vec<Vec<f32>>` | Multi-vector token payload. |
| `Absent` | `reason: AbsentReason` | Explicit absence ŌĆö "must never be interpreted as a zero vector". |

`SparseEntry { idx: u32, val: f32 }`. Helpers: `is_absent()`, `as_dense() -> Option<&[f32]>`
(only for `Dense`). `validate_schema()` rules:
- Dense: `dim > 0`, `data.len() == dim`, all finite.
- Sparse: `dim > 0`, each `idx < dim`, no duplicate `idx`, each `val` finite.
- Multi: `token_dim > 0`, Ōēź1 token, each token length == `token_dim`, all finite.
- Absent: always Ok.

### 5.3 `Anchor` / `AnchorValue` (`model/anchor.rs`)

`Anchor` ŌĆö a grounded real-outcome observation.

| Field | Type | Meaning |
|---|---|---|
| `kind` | `AnchorKind` | Outcome axis. |
| `value` | `AnchorValue` | Observed value. |
| `source` | `String` | Oracle / human labeler / reward / reality source. |
| `observed_at` | `Ts` | Server-observed timestamp. |
| `confidence` | `f32` | In `[0,1]`; deterministic oracles use `1.0`. |

`AnchorValue` (`snake_case` tagged): `Bool(bool)`, `Enum(String)`, `Number(f64)`,
`OneHot(Vec<String>)`, `Text(String)`, `Vector(Vec<f32>)`.

Validation: `confidence` must be finite and within `[0,1]`; `Number` must be finite;
`Vector` must be non-empty and all finite. Failures use `CALYX_RECORD_SCHEMA_VIOLATION`.

### 5.4 `Slot`, `Panel`, `LensCost`, `SlotResource`, `Placement` (`model/slot.rs`)

`Slot` ŌĆö a frozen lens slot in a panel.

| Field | Type | Meaning |
|---|---|---|
| `slot_id` | `SlotId` | Compact panel slot id. |
| `slot_key` | `SlotKey` | Human-readable key paired with the id. |
| `lens_id` | `LensId` | Frozen lens content id. |
| `shape` | `SlotShape` | Physical vector shape. |
| `modality` | `Modality` | Measured modality. |
| `asymmetry` | `Asymmetry` | Directional relation. |
| `quant` | `QuantPolicy` | Quantization policy. |
| `resource` | `SlotResource` | Cost + placement; `#[serde(default, skip_serializing_if = "SlotResource::is_default")]`. |
| `axis` | `Option<String>` | Optional semantic axis tag. |
| `retrieval_only` | `bool` | Post-retrieval signal only, not primary recall. `#[serde(default)]`. |
| `excluded_from_dedup` | `bool` | Must not drive dedup. `#[serde(default)]`. |
| `bits_about` | `BTreeMap<AnchorKind, Signal>` | Assay signal per outcome axis; custom `anchor_signal_map` serde (see 5.7). |
| `state` | `SlotState` | Lifecycle state. |
| `added_at_panel_version` | `u32` | Panel version that introduced the slot. |

`Panel`:

| Field | Type | Meaning |
|---|---|---|
| `version` | `u32` | Panel version. |
| `slots` | `Vec<Slot>` | Active or historically interpretable slots. |
| `created_at` | `Ts` | Server-stamped creation time. |
| `kernel_ref` | `Option<LedgerRef>` | Ledger ref for the grounding kernel used with this panel. |
| `guard_ref` | `Option<LedgerRef>` | Ledger ref for the guard calibration used with this panel. |

`LensCost` (all fields `#[serde(default)]`): `total_ms: f32`, `ms_per_input: f32`,
`vram_bytes: u64`, `ram_bytes: u64`, `batch_ceiling: u32`. `zero()` sets
`batch_ceiling = u32::MAX` and all else 0 (also the `Default`); `is_zero_cost()` ignores
`batch_ceiling`.

`SlotResource { cost: LensCost, placement: Placement }` (both `#[serde(default)]`),
`is_default()`. `Placement` enum: `Cpu` (default) | `Gpu` (`snake_case`).

### 5.5 `Signal`, `ConfidenceInterval`, `InputRef`, `LedgerRef`, `CxFlags` (`model/signal.rs`)

| Type | Fields |
|---|---|
| `ConfidenceInterval` | `low: f32`, `high: f32` |
| `Signal` | `bits: f32`, `ci: ConfidenceInterval`, `n: usize`, `estimator: String`, `ts: Ts` |
| `InputRef` | `hash: [u8;32]`, `pointer: Option<String>`, `redacted: bool` (derives `Eq`) |
| `LedgerRef` | `seq: u64`, `hash: [u8;32]` (derives `Eq`) |
| `CxFlags` | `ungrounded: bool`, `degraded: bool`, `novel_region: bool`, `redacted_input: bool` (derives `Default, Eq, Hash`) |

### 5.6 Record-schema validation (`model/validation.rs`)

`pub const CALYX_RECORD_SCHEMA_VIOLATION = "CALYX_RECORD_SCHEMA_VIOLATION"`. The
`pub(crate) fn record_schema_error(msg)` builds a `CalyxError` with that code and remediation
"submit a constellation matching the record schema with finite values". This is the single
error surface for all model `validate_schema` methods.

### 5.7 `bits_about` key encoding

`Slot.bits_about` uses module `anchor_signal_map`: it serializes the `BTreeMap<AnchorKind,
Signal>` as a `BTreeMap<String, Signal>`, encoding keys as the snake_case name except
`Label(v) ŌåÆ "label:{v}"` (e.g. `"label:gold"`). Decoding rejects unknown keys and duplicate
anchor kinds. Pinned by `panel_bits_about_supports_label_anchor_kind`.

---

## 6. Engine traits (`traits.rs`)

All four traits are `Send + Sync` and object-safe (`engine_traits_are_object_safe`). The
shared input type:

`Input { modality: Modality, bytes: Vec<u8>, pointer: Option<String> }` ŌĆö derives
`Clone, Debug, PartialEq, Eq, Serialize, Deserialize`; builders `new(modality, bytes)` and
`with_pointer(p)`.

### 6.1 `Lens` (implemented by Registry lens runtimes)

| Method | Signature | Implementor must provide |
|---|---|---|
| `id` | `fn id(&self) -> LensId` | stable frozen lens id |
| `shape` | `fn shape(&self) -> SlotShape` | emitted vector shape |
| `modality` | `fn modality(&self) -> Modality` | accepted modality |
| `measure` | `fn measure(&self, input: &Input) -> Result<SlotVector>` | deterministic per-input measurement |
| `measure_batch` | `fn measure_batch(&self, inputs: &[Input]) -> Result<Vec<SlotVector>>` | **default** maps `measure` over inputs (deterministic) |

### 6.2 `Index` (per-slot ANN / inverted index)

| Method | Signature |
|---|---|
| `insert` | `fn insert(&mut self, cx: CxId, vector: &SlotVector) -> Result<()>` |
| `search` | `fn search(&self, query: &SlotVector, k: usize, ef: Option<usize>) -> Result<Vec<(CxId, f32)>>` |
| `rebuild` | `fn rebuild(&mut self) -> Result<()>` |

### 6.3 `VaultStore` (Aster vault storage)

| Method | Signature |
|---|---|
| `put` | `fn put(&self, constellation: Constellation) -> Result<CxId>` (group-commit path) |
| `get` | `fn get(&self, id: CxId, snapshot: Seq) -> Result<Constellation>` (MVCC snapshot read) |
| `anchor` | `fn anchor(&self, id: CxId, anchor: Anchor) -> Result<()>` |
| `snapshot` | `fn snapshot(&self) -> Seq` (latest readable sequence) |

### 6.4 `Estimator` (Assay signal estimators)

| Method | Signature |
|---|---|
| `mi` | `fn mi(&self, x: &[SlotVector], y: &[Anchor]) -> Result<Signal>` |
| `redundancy` | `fn redundancy(&self, a: &[SlotVector], b: &[SlotVector]) -> Result<f32>` |

---

## 7. Time, clock injection (`time.rs`)

- `type Seq = u64` ŌĆö monotonic store sequence number.
- `type Ts = u64` ŌĆö server timestamp in **Unix milliseconds**.
- `trait Clock: Send + Sync { fn now(&self) -> Ts; }` ŌĆö injected clock; deterministic logic
  must use this rather than `SystemTime::now()`.
- `SystemClock` ŌĆö wall clock; `now()` = ms since Unix epoch (saturates to `Ts::MAX` on
  overflow; **panics** if before the epoch).
- `FixedClock { ts }` ŌĆö deterministic clock for tests/FSV; `new(ts)`, `now()` returns `ts`.

---

## 8. Cosine helper (`cosine.rs`)

- `trait GuardTauProfile { fn tau_for(&self, slot: &SlotId) -> Option<f32>; }` with a blanket
  impl for `BTreeMap<SlotId, f32>`. Lets guard-like policies look up per-slot tau without a
  crate dependency.
- `fn dense_cosine(left: &[f32], right: &[f32]) -> Option<f32>` ŌĆö fails **closed** (returns
  `None`) when lengths differ, either is empty, any element is non-finite, or the denominator
  is non-positive/non-finite. Otherwise returns `dot / (||l|| ┬Ę ||r||)` if finite.

---

## 9. Cold-start trust guard (`cold_start.rs`)

Enforces that a brand-new vault may search but must not label high-stakes answers grounded
until Ōēź1 real anchor exists.

- `VaultTrustState`: `Provisional` | `Grounded { anchor_count: usize }`.
- `ColdStartGuard { state }`: `new()`/`Default` start `Provisional`; `state()`,
  `anchor_count()`, `record_anchor()` (saturating +1, transitions to `Grounded`),
  `assert_grounded(operation) -> Result<()>` (fails with `CALYX_PROVISIONAL_VAULT` until
  `anchor_count >= 1`), `search_always_ok()` always `true`.

---

## 10. Consent / purpose gating (`consent.rs`)

- `type Timestamp = Ts` (Unix ms).
- `LawfulBasis` (snake_case, `Display` impl): `Consent, LegitimateInterest,
  ContractPerformance, LegalObligation, VitalInterests, PublicTask`.
- `Purpose` (snake_case): `Search, Intelligence, Reranking, Analytics, Export, AuditOnly`.
- `ConsentTag { lawful_basis: LawfulBasis, permitted_purposes: Vec<Purpose>, expires_at:
  Option<Timestamp> }`.
- `consent_expired(tag, now) -> bool` ŌĆö true iff `expires_at.is_some_and(now >= expires_at)`.
- `check_consent(tag, requested_purpose, now) -> Result<()>` ŌĆö fail-closed:
  `AuditOnly` is always allowed; otherwise rejects with `CALYX_CONSENT_VIOLATION` if expired
  or if the purpose is not in `permitted_purposes`.

---

## 11. Transport security / authN (`security.rs`)

Lives in core so `calyx-aster` and `calyxd` share it without a cycle (PRD 30 ┬¦2). Module-local
codes `CALYX_AUTHN_REQUIRED`, `CALYX_TLS_CONFIG_INVALID` (not in the closed catalog).

- `TlsConfig { cert_pem_path: PathBuf, key_pem_path: PathBuf, ca_pem_path: Option<PathBuf> }`.
  `validate()` checks each configured path exists and is a regular readable **file** (metadata
  only, no PEM parse); first offender ŌåÆ `CALYX_TLS_CONFIG_INVALID`. `ca_pem_path = Some`
  enables mTLS.
- `MtlsConfig { tls: TlsConfig, require_client_cert: bool }`.
- `AuthN` enum (3 identity modes): `InProcess { host_app_id: String }`,
  `MtlsToken { fingerprint: [u8;32] }`, `CloudflareAccess { service_token_id: String }`.
  `is_server_mode()` is true only for the latter two.
- `no_anonymous_write(authn: Option<&AuthN>) -> Result<()>` ŌĆö the only presence gate: `Some` ŌåÆ
  Ok, `None` ŌåÆ `CALYX_AUTHN_REQUIRED` (fail-closed, A16). Validating identity *contents* is the
  caller's job.

---

## 12. Temporal policy contracts (`temporal.rs`)

Post-retrieval boosting contracts (AP-60: temporal signals stay post-retrieval and never
dominant). Constants: `WEIGHT_SUM_EPSILON = 1e-6`, `DEFAULT_HALF_LIFE_SECS = 3600`,
`DEFAULT_POST_RETRIEVAL_ALPHA = 0.10`, `MAX_POST_RETRIEVAL_ALPHA = 0.10`,
`MAX_CAUSAL_MULTIPLIER = 10.0`, `DEFAULT_RECURRENCE_WEIGHT = 0.05`,
`DEFAULT_MAX_RECURRENCE_BOOST = 0.10`. Six module-local `CALYX_TEMPORAL_*` codes (see 3.3).

Most of these types have **hand-written `Deserialize`** impls that run `validate()` on the
wire payload (fail-closed on load); only their `Serialize` is derived.

| Type | Fields / variants | Validation |
|---|---|---|
| `DecayFunction` | `Linear { max_age_secs: u64 }`, `Exponential { half_life_secs: u64 }`, `Step` | Default `Exponential{half_life_secs:3600}`. |
| `PeriodicOptions` | `target_hour: Option<u8>`, `target_day_of_week: Option<u8>`, `use_now: bool` | `target_hour Ōēż 23`, `day_of_week Ōēż 6` else `CALYX_TEMPORAL_INVALID_PERIOD`. Default `use_now=true`. |
| `SequenceDirection` | `Forward`, `Backward` | ŌĆö |
| `MultiAnchorMode` | `First`, `Last`, `All` | ŌĆö |
| `SequenceOptions` | `direction: SequenceDirection`, `multi_anchor_mode: MultiAnchorMode` | Default `Forward`/`First`. |
| `FusionWeights` | `recency: f32`, `sequence: f32`, `periodic: f32` | all finite (else `CALYX_TEMPORAL_WEIGHT_SUM`), all Ōēź0 (else `CALYX_TEMPORAL_NEGATIVE_WEIGHT`), `|sum-1| < 1e-6` (else `CALYX_TEMPORAL_WEIGHT_SUM`). Default `0.50/0.35/0.15`. |
| `BoostConfig` | `post_retrieval_alpha: f32`, `causal_high_mult: f32`, `causal_low_mult: f32` | `alpha` finite in `0..=0.10` (else `CALYX_TEMPORAL_AP60_VIOLATION`); `high_mult` finite in `(1.0, 10.0]`; `low_mult` finite in `[0.0,1.0)`; `low_mult < high_mult` (else `CALYX_TEMPORAL_INVALID_BOOST_CONFIG`). Default `0.10/1.10/0.85`. `alpha` defaults to `0.10` if missing on the wire. |
| `RecurrenceBoostConfig` | `frequency_weight: f32`, `recency_weight: f32`, `max_recurrence_boost: f32` | all finite, Ōēź0, `max Ōēż 0.10` (else `CALYX_TEMPORAL_INVALID_BOOST_CONFIG`). Default `0.05/0.05/0.10`. |
| `TemporalPolicy` | `enabled: bool`, `decay`, `periodic`, `sequence`, `fusion_weights`, `boost`, `recurrence_boost: Option<RecurrenceBoostConfig>`, `never_dominant: bool` | `never_dominant` must be `true` (else `CALYX_TEMPORAL_AP60_VIOLATION`); then validates periodic, fusion_weights, recurrence_boost (if present), boost. `recurrence_boost` defaults to `Some(default)`. |

`FusionWeights` validation is the subject of the integration FSV
(`tests/fusion_weights_validation_fsv.rs`): 8 named cases + 2 proptests confirm valid convex
blends pass and that negative components ŌåÆ `CALYX_TEMPORAL_NEGATIVE_WEIGHT`, NaN/Inf and
sumŌēĀ1 ŌåÆ `CALYX_TEMPORAL_WEIGHT_SUM`. The test writes a JSON readback artifact + BLAKE3SUMS to
a temp root (kept if `CALYX_FUSION_WEIGHTS_FSV_ROOT` is set).

`temporal_error(code, msg)` maps each code to its remediation string (see 3.3).

---

## 13. Bounded allocation primitives (`alloc/`)

PH56 / Stage S13. Every cap violation surfaces `CALYX_ALLOC_CAP_EXCEEDED` (built by
`alloc_cap_exceeded`, remediation "raise the cap or shrink the working set; allocations fail
closed (A26)"). Constant `CALYX_ALLOC_CAP_EXCEEDED` is `pub`.

`AllocStats { arena_high_water_bytes: usize, arena_resets: u64 }` ŌĆö metrics snapshot.

### 13.1 `Arena` / `ArenaVec` (`alloc/arena.rs`)

Bump allocator over one pre-allocated, `ARENA_BASE_ALIGN = 4096`-byte-aligned block.

- `Arena::new(cap)` ŌĆö `cap==0` ŌåÆ `CALYX_ALLOC_CAP_EXCEEDED`.
- `alloc(size, align) -> Result<*mut u8>` ŌĆö `align` must be a power of two (asserted);
  `size==0` returns an aligned dangling pointer consuming nothing; pads cursor to `align`,
  checked-arithmetic throughout; if padded request would cross `cap`, fails **without**
  advancing the cursor; tracks high-water.
- `alloc_vec::<T>(capacity) -> Result<ArenaVec<T>>` ŌĆö reserves bytes for `capacity` `T`s
  (ZST/zero-cap returns a dangling vec); borrows the arena for the vec's lifetime.
- `reset()` ŌĆö O(1) cursor rewind to 0, no `free`, increments `resets`.
- Accessors: `used()`, `capacity()`, `high_water()`, `stats()`.
- `ArenaVec<'a, T>`: `push(value)` fails closed at reserved capacity; `len`, `is_empty`,
  `capacity`, `as_slice`, `as_mut_slice`; `Drop` drops initialized elements in place.

### 13.2 `SlabPool` / `PageAlignedSlabPool` (`alloc/slab.rs`)

Fixed-size object pools with a free list; RAII guards release slots on drop. Exhaustion ŌåÆ
`CALYX_ALLOC_CAP_EXCEEDED`. Constants: `PAGE_SIZE = 4096`, `DEFAULT_EMBED_DIM = 768`,
`VEC_BLOCK_SIZE = 768*4 = 3072`, `ANN_NODE_SIZE = size_of::<AnnNode>()`.

- `AnnNode` `#[repr(C)]`: `id: u64`, `neighbors: [u32; 32]`, `level: u16`, `pad: [u8; 6]`.
- `SlabPool<const SLOT_SIZE: usize>`: `new(cap_slots)` (`0` rejected), `acquire() ->
  SlabGuard`, `cap_slots()`, `held()`, `utilization()`. Slots in `UnsafeCell`; free
  list/state behind `RefCell` so `acquire` needs only `&self`. A double-release
  `debug_assert!`s (panics in debug; refuses the push in release).
- Aliases: `VecBlockPool = SlabPool<3072>`, `AnnNodePool = SlabPool<ANN_NODE_SIZE>`.
- `SlabGuard<'_, SLOT_SIZE>`: `Deref/DerefMut` to `[u8; SLOT_SIZE]`, `slot_index()`.
- `PageAlignedSlabPool`: 4 KiB-aligned for pinned-host CUDA staging. `new(slot_size,
  cap_slots)` ŌĆö `slot_size` must be a non-zero multiple of `PAGE_SIZE` (**panics**
  otherwise); `cap_slots==0` rejected. `acquire() -> PageSlabGuard`, `slot_size()`,
  `cap_slots()`, `held()`, `utilization()`. Manually `unsafe impl Send` (not `Sync`).
- `PageSlabGuard<'_>`: `slot_index()`, `as_mut_ptr()` (page-aligned), `as_mut_slice()`.

---

## 14. Bounded LRU+TTL cache (`cache/`)

PH56 / Stage S13. `LruTtlCache<K, V>` ŌĆö byte-capped, LRU-evicting, per-entry-TTL cache over an
intrusive doubly-linked node arena (O(1) get/insert/evict; no external map crate). Constant
`CALYX_CACHE_EVICTED = "CALYX_CACHE_EVICTED"` is emitted as a `tracing::debug!` event (never a
panic). Jitter RNG is `ChaCha8Rng` seeded with fixed `JITTER_SEED = 0xCA178C0FFEE51D0F` for
reproducibility.

- `InsertResult { evicted: usize }`.
- `new(byte_cap, ttl: Duration, clock: Arc<dyn Clock>)` and `with_jitter(byte_cap, ttl,
  jitter, clock)` ŌĆö `byte_cap==0` ŌåÆ `CALYX_ALLOC_CAP_EXCEEDED`. TTL/jitter stored as ms.
- `get(&mut, key) -> Option<&V>` ŌĆö entries past TTL are evicted and counted as a miss; a live
  hit is promoted to MRU.
- `insert(key, value, size_bytes) -> Result<InsertResult>` ŌĆö a single entry larger than the
  whole cap ŌåÆ `CALYX_ALLOC_CAP_EXCEEDED`; first sweeps expired entries, replaces an existing
  key (not counted as eviction), then evicts LRU tail entries until `used_bytes + size_bytes
  <= byte_cap`.
- `evict_expired() -> usize`; `len`, `is_empty`, `used_bytes`, `byte_cap`, `hit_rate`,
  `evictions`, `expired_total`.
- Expiry = `now + ttl_ms` with `┬▒jitter/2` offset (saturating). The clock is injected
  (`Arc<dyn Clock>`), never `SystemTime::now()` in logic.

---

## 15. Serialization & determinism summary

- **Format**: serde-driven; tested wire format is JSON (`serde_json`). No `bincode`/`ciborium`
  in this crate. Maps use `BTreeMap` for stable key ordering; many round-trip tests assert
  **byte-exact** re-serialization.
- **IDs**: `LensId`/`CxId` serialize as lowercase hex strings; `VaultId` as a ULID string;
  `SlotId` transparently as a `u16`.
- **Enums**: `#[serde(rename_all = "snake_case")]`; struct variants nest under the snake_case
  tag.
- **Content addresses**: 128-bit BLAKE3 prefix over length-delimited (8-byte BE length +
  bytes) ordered parts.
- **Validating deserializers**: temporal policy types validate on load and fail closed.
- **`CalyxError`**: `Serialize`-only (the `&'static str` code/remediation are not
  round-trippable); wire shape `{"code","message","remediation"}`.

---

## 16. Gaps / not covered

- `CALYX_TEMPORAL_INVALID_WINDOW` is declared and given a remediation in `temporal_error`,
  but no code path in `calyx-core` raises it (its window type, if any, lives elsewhere).
- `calyx-core` defines the engine **traits** only; concrete `Lens`/`Index`/`VaultStore`/
  `Estimator` implementations live in their owning crates (see the cross-references above).
  Tests here use in-file dummy impls only.
- `SystemClock::now()` panics if the system clock predates the Unix epoch ŌĆö the only panic on
  a non-misuse path in this crate (alloc-pool misuse such as a non-page-multiple slot size or
  a debug double-release also panics).
- The data-model structs deliberately omit `Eq`/`Hash` where they carry floats
  (`Constellation`, `Signal`, `Slot`, `Panel`, `SlotVector`, `Anchor`, etc.).
- Module-local error codes are intentionally outside the closed PRD-18 catalog; the source
  comments flag this as a pending governance follow-up.

<!-- ===== END 05_core.md ===== -->


<!-- ===== BEGIN 06_aster_storage_engine.md ===== -->

---

# 06 ŌĆö Aster Storage Engine (calyx-aster)

`calyx-aster` is the storage substrate of Calyx: an ordered, transactional, MVCC
keyspace built as an LSM tree (memtable + immutable SSTables + WAL) with column
families, hot/cold tiering, atomic manifest/versioning, crash recovery, and a set
of FoundationDB-style key-encoding "layers" (relational, document, KV,
time-series, blob, graph) plus the native constellation/slot/anchor families.
Largest crate in the workspace (232 `.rs` files).

This doc documents WHAT THE CODE DOES. Where the planning doc
`docs/dbprdplans/04_ASTER_STORAGE_FORMAT.md` describes intent that is not (yet)
matched by code (DiskANN, SPANN, PQ/Float8 quantization, zstd compression), it is
flagged in [┬¦11 Gaps](#11-gaps--not-covered). On-disk magic/version constants here
also feed [04_storage_and_schema.md](04_storage_and_schema.md).

**Source files covered:**
- `crates/calyx-aster/src/lib.rs`
- `crates/calyx-aster/src/wal/mod.rs`, `wal/record.rs`, `wal/batch.rs`, `wal/segment.rs`
- `crates/calyx-aster/src/memtable/bounded.rs`, `memtable/mod.rs`
- `crates/calyx-aster/src/sst/mod.rs`, `sst/bloom.rs`, `sst/level.rs`, `sst/arrow.rs`
- `crates/calyx-aster/src/mmap_col.rs`
- `crates/calyx-aster/src/mvcc/store.rs`, `mvcc/mod.rs`, `mvcc/lease.rs`, `mvcc/read_barrier.rs`
- `crates/calyx-aster/src/manifest/mod.rs`, `manifest/quarantine.rs`
- `crates/calyx-aster/src/compaction/mod.rs`, `compaction/tiering.rs`, `compaction/scan.rs`
- `crates/calyx-aster/src/cf/family.rs`, `cf/key.rs`, `cf/router.rs`, `cf/mod.rs`
- `crates/calyx-aster/src/storage_names.rs`
- `crates/calyx-aster/src/vault.rs`, `vault/encode.rs`, `vault/durable.rs`
- `crates/calyx-aster/src/gc/*`, `timetravel/*`, `txn/*`, `dedup/*`, `index/*`, `layers/*`, `collection/*`, `resource/*`, `pressure.rs`, `residency.rs`, `retention.rs`, `security/*`, `redaction.rs`, `erase.rs`

---

## 1. Storage architecture

### 1.1 Module tree (top-level `pub mod` from `src/lib.rs`)

`cf`, `collection`, `compaction`, `dedup`, `erase`, `gc`, `index`, `layers`,
`ledger_view`, `manifest`, `memtable`, `mmap_col`, `mvcc`, `olap`, `plain_column`,
`plain_graph`, `pressure`, `recurrence`, `redaction`, `residency`, `resource`,
`retention`, `security`, `sst`, `storage_names`, `stream`, `stride_fsv`,
`supply_chain`, `timetravel`, `txn`, `vault`, `wal`. Private: `file_lock`.
`lib.rs` re-exports only the dedup compression helpers
(`CompressionRatio`, `Domain`, `DomainCompressionStats`, `compression_ratio`,
`domain_compression_stats`). The `lib.rs` doc-comment calls the crate a
"skeleton".

### 1.2 LSM design

Aster is a leveled LSM keyspace. Per column family the write/read components are:

| Component | Type | File |
|---|---|---|
| Mutable in-memory table | `BoundedMemtable` (alias `Memtable`), `BTreeMap<Vec<u8>,Vec<u8>>` with byte cap | `memtable/bounded.rs` |
| Frozen handoff | `FrozenMemtable` (immutable `BTreeMap`) | `memtable/bounded.rs` |
| On-disk sorted table | SSTable (`write_sst` / `SstReader`), mmap-backed | `sst/mod.rs` |
| Per-CF newest-first stack | `SstLevel` (single level) | `sst/level.rs` |
| Router | `CfRouter` ŌĆö owns one memtable + one `SstLevel` per CF | `cf/router.rs` |
| Compaction view | `CompactionCatalog` / `CompactionSnapshot` with atomic swap | `compaction/mod.rs` |

Note: `SstLevel` models a single per-CF level (`files: Vec<PathBuf>`, newest at
index 0 via `push` inserting at front). There is no multi-level (L0/L1/ŌĆ”)
fan-out implemented inside `SstLevel`; the `level: u8` on `SstShard` only
increments on compaction for naming/debt purposes.

### 1.3 Write path (`AsterVault` / `CfRouter` / `DurableVault`)

`AsterVault<C>` (`vault.rs`) is the single-vault store. A durable write group
(`write_cf_batch` / `commit_rows` ŌåÆ `stage_constellation_rows`):

1. Build `Vec<WriteRow{cf,key,value}>`.
2. `ensure_memtable_admission` / `CfRouter::ensure_batch_admitted` ŌĆö fail closed
   with `CALYX_BACKPRESSURE` if any single row exceeds the memtable byte cap
   (a row that can never fit), BEFORE the WAL append (`cf/router.rs`).
3. `DurableVault::append_batch` (`vault/durable.rs`): `encode_write_batch(rows)`
   ŌåÆ `GroupCommitBatcher::submit(payload)` ŌåÆ WAL append + fsync; returns the
   allocated seq. (Test-only failpoint `fail_next_wal_append`.)
4. `VersionedCfStore::commit_batch` applies rows to the CF router memtables and
   pushes versioned values at the allocated MVCC seq (`mvcc/store.rs`).
5. Memtable high-water ŌåÆ `CfRouter::flush_cf` writes an SSTable and pushes it on
   the CF's `SstLevel`. Backpressure on a full memtable triggers an inline flush
   and retry (`record_memtable_absorbed` / `record_memtable_rejected`).

`CfRouter::put` flow: write to memtable; on `CALYX_BACKPRESSURE` flush the CF and
retry once; if `ack.flush_triggered` (high-water), flush after the write.

### 1.4 Read path

`AsterVault::read_cf_at(seq, cf, key)` ŌåÆ `VersionedCfStore::read_at` resolves the
visible version for the pinned seq (MVCC, ┬¦4). For the non-MVCC raw LSM path,
`CfRouter::get` checks the memtable first, then `SstLevel::get` which opens each
SST newest-first and returns the first hit (Bloom-gated). `range`/`iter_cf` merge
memtable + level into a `BTreeMap` (newest wins). `CompactionSnapshot::get`
iterates shards in reverse, newest first.

### 1.5 Column families

`ColumnFamily` (`cf/family.rs`) is the CF enum. Static (non-slot) families are in
`ColumnFamily::STATIC` (an array of 33; recovery/manifest order). Slot CFs are
parameterized: `Slot { slot: SlotId, kind: SlotFamilyKind }` where
`SlotFamilyKind Ōłł {Quantized, Raw}`. Directory names from `ColumnFamily::name()`:

| CF | dir name | key (logical) |
|---|---|---|
| `Base` | `base` | `CxId` ŌåÆ ConstellationHeader |
| `Collections` | `collections` | `b"coll\0" ŌĆ¢ name` ŌåÆ collection metadata |
| `Relational` | `relational` | `0x01 ŌĆ¢ collection_id ŌĆ¢ pk` |
| `Document` | `document` | `0x02 ŌĆ¢ collection_id ŌĆ¢ doc_id ŌĆ¢ path` |
| `Kv` | `kv` | `0x03 ŌĆ¢ collection_id ŌĆ¢ ns ŌĆ¢ key` |
| `TimeSeries` | `timeseries` | `0x04 ŌĆ¢ ŌĆ” ŌĆ¢ ts/window` |
| `Blob` | `blob` | `0x05 ŌĆ¢ ŌĆ” ŌĆ¢ blob_id ŌĆ¢ chunk` |
| `Slot{Quantized}` | `slot_NN` | `CxId` ŌåÆ quantized SlotVector |
| `Slot{Raw}` | `slot_NN.raw` | `CxId` ŌåÆ raw f32 sidecar |
| `XTerm` | `xterm` | `(CxId, SlotId_a, SlotId_b, XTermKind)` |
| `TemporalXTerm` | `temporal_xterm` | `(CxId_a, CxId_b)` |
| `Scalars` | `scalars` | `(ScalarId, CxId)` ŌåÆ f64 |
| `Anchors` | `anchors` | `(CxId, AnchorKind)` ŌåÆ AnchorValue |
| `Assay` | `assay` | `(panel_version, corpus_shard, subject)` |
| `Ledger` | `ledger` | `seq` ŌåÆ hash-chained entry |
| `Kernel` | `kernel` | Lodestar kernel reports/indexes |
| `Guard` | `guard` | Ward calibration profiles |
| `Recurrence` | `recurrence` | `(CxId, OccurrenceId)` |
| `Graph` | `graph` | nodes/edges/reverse/CSR |
| `Online` | `online` | typed online state |
| `Reactive` | `reactive` | reactive trigger audit |
| `AnnealRollbackŌĆ”AnnealOperators` (14 CFs) | `anneal_*` | Anneal state |
| `TimeIndex` | `time_index` | `be(millis) ŌĆ¢ be(seqno)` ŌåÆ sentinel |
| `IndexBtree` | `index_btree` | `0x10 ŌĆ¢ collection_id ŌĆ¢ index_id ŌĆ¢ field_val ŌĆ¢ pk` |
| `IndexInverted` | `index_inverted` | `0x11 ŌĆ¢ collection_id ŌĆ¢ index_id ŌĆ¢ term_hash ŌĆ¢ pk` ŌåÆ f32 |

`ColumnFamily::keyspace_tag()` / `parse_keyspace_tag()` give a reversible CF tag
for vault-scoped composite keys: non-slot CFs encode to their single-byte index
in `STATIC`; slot CFs encode to `SLOT_KEYSPACE_TAG (0xF0) ŌĆ¢ slot_id_be(2) ŌĆ¢ kind_byte`
(`Quantized=0`, `Raw=1`). `STATIC.len()` stays below `0xF0` so there is no
collision. `is_slot`, `is_raw_slot`, `slot_id`, `slot(SlotId)`, `slot_raw(SlotId)`
are the accessors/constructors.

Key codecs (`cf/key.rs`) are all big-endian for range-scan ordering. `CxId` is a
16-byte BLAKE3 prefix (`CX_ID_BYTES = 16`, `FULL_HASH_BYTES = 32`). Functions:
`base_key`, `slot_key`, `xterm_key`, `temporal_xterm_key`, `scalar_key`,
`anchor_key`, `ledger_key`, `recurrence_key`, `online_key`, the matching
`*_prefix_range`/`*_range` builders, `prefix_range`, `full_content_hash` (BLAKE3
over length-delimited parts: each part prefixed with `be_u64(len)`),
`cx_id_from_full_hash` (first 16 bytes), `verify_cx_hash_prefix`.
`XTermKind Ōłł {Concat=0, Interaction=1, Agreement=2, Delta=3}`;
`OnlineKeyKind Ōłł {MistakeLog=0, ReplayBuffer=1, HeadState=2, DeltaJQueue=3}`;
`ScalarId(u32)`; `KeyRange{start, end:Option}` (`contains`: `start Ōēż key < end`).
`anchor_key` encodes `AnchorKind` as a `be_u16` tag (`TestPass=0 ŌĆ” Recurrence=6`,
`Label=7` followed by `be_u64(len) ŌĆ¢ utf8`).

---

## 2. Write-ahead log (`wal/`)

### 2.1 Record format ŌĆö "CXW1" (`wal/record.rs`)

`MAGIC = "CXW1"` as little-endian `u32` (`u32::from_le_bytes(*b"CXW1")`).
`HEADER_LEN = 20`, `MAX_RECORD_BYTES = 64 MiB`.

```
WAL record (all little-endian):
  +0   u32   magic   = "CXW1"
  +4   u64   seq             (1-based vault WAL sequence)
  +12  u32   len             (payload length, Ōēż 64 MiB)
  +16  u32   crc             (crc32fast over seq_le ŌĆ¢ len_le ŌĆ¢ payload)
  +20  [u8; len]  payload    (encode_write_batch output)
```

CRC: `crc32fast::Hasher` over `seq.to_le_bytes()`, `len.to_le_bytes()`, then the
payload. `decode_at` returns `DecodeStatus::{Complete, Eof, Torn{offset,message}}`.
A record is **Torn** (and the tail truncated) on: partial header (`<20` bytes,
non-zero), bad magic, `len > MAX_RECORD_BYTES`, partial payload (UnexpectedEof),
or CRC mismatch. `Eof` is a clean 0-byte read at a record boundary.

The WAL payload is a `WriteRow` batch (`vault/encode.rs` `encode_write_batch`):
`be_u32(row_count)` then per row `cf_tag(u8) ŌĆ¢ be_u32(key_len) ŌĆ¢ key ŌĆ¢ be_u32(value_len) ŌĆ¢ value`.

### 2.2 Segments (`wal/segment.rs`)

Segment files are named `{index:020}.wal` (20-digit zero-padded). `list_segments`
sorts by index and **fails closed** (`CALYX_ASTER_CORRUPT_SHARD`) if indexes are
non-contiguous (a missing segment would silently drop committed writes) or if a
`*.wal` file has a non-canonical name (`storage_names::wal_segment_index`).

### 2.3 Writer & group-commit (`wal/mod.rs`, `wal/batch.rs`)

`Wal` holds the active segment file in append mode. `WalOptions`:
`max_segment_bytes` (default 64 MiB), `group_commit_window` (default
`DEFAULT_GROUP_COMMIT_WINDOW = 2 ms`). `Wal::open` acquires a `.append.lock`
file lock, replays/truncates a torn tail, and sets `next_seq` to last seq + 1
(or 1). `append_batch` re-checks for external appends, encodes each record, rotates
the segment if `offset + bytes > max_segment_bytes` (fsync-before-rotate via
`sync_all`), writes all records, then a single `sync_data()` (fsync) before
returning `AppendAck{seq, segment_path, start_offset, end_offset}`. One fsync per
batch is the group-commit unit.

`GroupCommitBatcher` (`wal/batch.rs`) is the fsync-backed coalescing wrapper: a
dedicated thread receives `BatchOp::{Append,Flush,TipSeq}` over an mpsc channel.
On the first `Append` it opens a deadline of `group_commit_window` and drains
further requests until the deadline/timeout/disconnect, then calls
`Wal::append_batch` once for all coalesced payloads (one fsync). `validate_window`
**rejects any window > 2 ms** with `CALYX_DISK_PRESSURE` ("group_commit_window
exceeds 2 ms limit"). Public API: `submit(payload)->AppendAck`, `flush_sync()`,
`tip_seq()->u64`.

### 2.4 fsync policy

Every batch append issues `sync_data()`; segment rotation issues `sync_all()`;
newly created segments fsync the parent directory on Unix (`sync_parent`, no-op on
non-Unix). The torn-tail truncation path also `set_len` + `sync_data`. WAL is the
source of truth for un-checkpointed writes.

### 2.5 Replay & recycling

`replay_dir` / `replay_dir_locked` decode every segment in order; on the first
torn record it truncates that segment to the torn offset, removes all later
segments, and returns `ReplayOutcome{records, torn_tail: Some(TornTail)}`.
`TornTail{segment_path, offset, code, message}` carries `code =
CalyxErrorCode::AsterTornWal.code()`; `TornTail::error()` builds the catalogued
`AsterTornWal` error. `WalSegmentStatus`, `segment_inventory`,
`total_segment_bytes`, `durable_tip_seq`, and `recycle_durable_segments`
(`WalRecycleReport`) support the GC WAL recycler: a non-active segment whose
`last_seq Ōēż newest_durable_seq` is recyclable; recycling truncates it to 0 and
fsyncs, bounded by `min(max_segments, fsync_budget)` per pass.

---

## 3. Memtable, SSTable, columnar & mmap formats

### 3.1 Memtable (`memtable/bounded.rs`)

`BoundedMemtable` (aliased `Memtable`): `Mutex<BTreeMap<Vec<u8>,Vec<u8>>>` with a
hard `cap_bytes` and a `high_water_bytes` (default 80% of cap,
`high_water_for = cap*4/5`). `ENTRY_OVERHEAD_BYTES = 4`; `entry_size = key.len +
value.len + 4`. `write(key,value,seq)->WriteAck` fails closed with
`CALYX_BACKPRESSURE` if the row alone exceeds cap, or if projected used bytes
exceed cap (replacing an existing key reclaims its bytes first). `WriteAck{seq,
accepted_bytes, used_bytes, cap_bytes, high_water_bytes, flush_triggered}`;
`flush_triggered` is true at/above high-water (and always true when cap==0).
`MemtableUsage` mirrors the byte accounting. `freeze()` ŌåÆ `FrozenMemtable`;
`flush_to_sst(path)` writes a sorted SSTable; `reset_after_flush(bytes)`
decrements the atomic usage counter. Iteration is key-ordered (BTreeMap).

### 3.2 SSTable format ŌĆö "CXS1" v2 (`sst/mod.rs`)

`MAGIC = b"CXS1"`, current `VERSION = 2`, `LEGACY_VERSION = 1` (still readable),
`HEADER_LEN = 32`, `RECORD_HEADER_LEN = 12`, `INDEX_ENTRY_FIXED_LEN = 12`.
All multi-byte fields little-endian. Layout:

```
SSTable (CXS1):
  HEADER (32 B):
    +0  [u8;4] magic = "CXS1"
    +4  u32    version = 2
    +8  u32    entries
    +12 u64    index_offset
    +20 u64    bloom_offset
    +28 u32    body_crc   (crc32 over bytes[32..]; v2 only)
  RECORDS  (offset 32 .. index_offset), each:
    +0  u32    key_len
    +4  u32    value_len
    +8  u32    record_crc  (crc32 over key ŌĆ¢ value)
    +12 key bytes ŌĆ¢ value bytes
  INDEX  (index_offset .. bloom_offset), one per entry, key-sorted:
    +0  u32    key_len
    +4  u64    record_offset
    +12 key bytes
  BLOOM  (bloom_offset .. EOF): encoded BloomFilter
```

`write_sst(path, entries)` requires strictly sorted, unique keys
(`ensure_sorted`, else `CALYX_ASTER_CORRUPT_SHARD`); writes to `path.sst.tmp`,
`sync_all`, then atomic `rename` + parent fsync. `SstReader::open` mmaps the file
(`MmapColumn`), validates header magic/version, bounds-checks offsets, verifies
the v2 body CRC, and decodes the index and Bloom filter ŌĆö every failure path is a
fail-closed `CALYX_ASTER_CORRUPT_SHARD`. `get(key)` consults the Bloom filter,
then binary-searches the index and reads + CRC-verifies the record. `range`,
`iter`, `bloom_may_contain` round out the API. `SstSummary{path, entries, bytes,
index_offset, bloom_offset}`; `SstEntry{key, value}`.

### 3.3 Bloom filter (`sst/bloom.rs`)

Deterministic per-SST filter: `bit_count = max(64,
next_power_of_two(max(1,n)*16))`, `hash_count = 3`. Hashing is BLAKE3 over
`key ŌĆ¢ round_le_u32`, first 8 bytes mod `bit_count`. Encoded as
`le_u64(bit_count) ŌĆ¢ le_u32(hash_count) ŌĆ¢ le_u32(byte_len) ŌĆ¢ bits`. Tested
false-positive rate < 1% at 10k keys; no false negatives by construction.

### 3.4 SstLevel (`sst/level.rs`)

Per-CF newest-first `Vec<PathBuf>` (`push` inserts at front). `get` returns the
first (newest) SST hit. `range`/`iter` merge across files into a `BTreeMap` where
the **oldest** value is kept (`or_insert`) because files are iterated newest-first
and `or_insert` does not overwrite ŌĆö so the first-seen (newest) value wins.

### 3.5 Arrow column chunk ŌĆö "CXA1" v1 (`sst/arrow.rs`)

Column-major f32 chunk for SIMD-friendly slot scans:

```
Arrow chunk (CXA1, little-endian):
  +0  [u8;4] magic = "CXA1"
  +4  u32    version = 1
  +8  u32    n_rows
  +12 u32    dim
  +16 ...    f32 values, COLUMN-MAJOR: for col in 0..dim { for row in 0..n_rows { f32_le } }
```

`HEADER_LEN = 16`. `encode_column_chunk(rows)` (all rows same non-zero dim);
`decode_column_shape` ŌåÆ `ArrowColumnView` (zero-copy column slices,
`column_bytes`/`column_values`/`value(col,row)`); `decode_column_chunk` ŌåÆ
`ArrowChunkView` (row-major materialized, `row(i)`). Length and shape are
validated exactly (`bytes.len() == HEADER_LEN + n_rows*dim*4`).

### 3.6 mmap (`mmap_col.rs`)

`MmapColumn` is a read-only `memmap2::Mmap` over an immutable file (backs every
`SstReader`). `open` rejects missing/empty files (`CALYX_NOT_FOUND`). Accessors:
`read_slice(offset,len)` (bounds-checked), `read_f32_slice(offset,count)`
(checks f32 alignment of both offset and base pointer, returns `&[f32]` via
`from_raw_parts`), `as_bytes`, `file_len`, `path`, plus `prefetch`/`drop_pages`
(`madvise WILL_NEED`/`DONT_NEED`, Unix-only, best-effort). Error codes:
`CALYX_NOT_FOUND`, `CALYX_IO_ERROR`, `CALYX_BOUNDS_EXCEEDED`. Doc note: file must
not be truncated while mapped (SIGBUS risk); ZFS columns should use
`primarycache=metadata`.

### 3.7 Constellation base value encoding (`vault/encode.rs`)

The `base` CF value is the constellation header + body. `HEADER_LEN = 102`,
`IDENTITY_HASH_LEN = 32`. `ConstellationHeader` fields:
`cx_id(16) ŌĆ¢ vault_id ULID(16) ŌĆ¢ be_u32 panel_version ŌĆ¢ be_u64 created_at ŌĆ¢
u8 modality_tag ŌĆ¢ u8 flags_bits ŌĆ¢ be_u16 n_slots ŌĆ¢ be_u16 n_anchors ŌĆ¢
be_u64 ledger_seq ŌĆ¢ input_hash(32) ŌĆ¢ 12 zero bytes` (= 102 bytes).
`encode_constellation_base` appends: BLAKE3 identity hash (32 B), input-ref tail
(`u8 redacted ŌĆ¢ pointer tag/string`), slot list (`be_u16 count`, then per slot
`be_u16 slot_id ŌĆ¢ blake3(encode_slot_vector)`), scalars (`be_u32 count`, then
`len-prefixed key ŌĆ¢ be_u64 f64.to_bits`), anchors (`be_u32 count`, len-prefixed
`encode_anchor`), provenance hash (32 B), then string metadata. Modality tags
`Text=0 ŌĆ” Molecule=9`; flags bitfield `ungrounded|degraded<<1|novel_region<<2|redacted_input<<3`.

`encode_slot_vector` tag byte: `Dense=0 (be_u32 dim ŌĆ¢ be_u32 f32.to_bitsŌĆ”)`,
`Absent=1 (reason tag 0..5)`, `Sparse=2 (be_u32 dim ŌĆ¢ be_u32 n ŌĆ¢ {be_u32 idx ŌĆ¢
be_u32 val}ŌĆ”)`, `Multi=3 (be_u32 token_dim ŌĆ¢ be_u32 n_tokens ŌĆ¢ tokensŌĆ”)`. Floats
are stored as big-endian IEEE-754 bit patterns (`f32::to_bits`/`f64::to_bits`),
not raw f32 LE ŌĆö i.e. the slot CF value is NOT the Arrow CXA1 layout.

---

## 4. MVCC snapshots (`mvcc/`)

### 4.1 Sequence allocator (`mvcc/lease.rs`)

`SeqAllocator{current:AtomicU64, allocated:AtomicBool}`: `new(start)` makes the
next write `start+1`. `allocate()` does `fetch_add(1)+1` and marks allocated;
`current()` reads the latest committed seq; `set_start_seq(seq)` is permitted only
before the first allocation (else `CALYX_BACKPRESSURE` "cannot reset MVCC start
seq after allocation") ŌĆö used during recovery; `advance_to_at_least(seq)` CAS-bumps
the seq after reading externally committed durable rows. The vault sequence is a
single vault-wide monotonic counter; a write advances it and all CFs share it.

### 4.2 Versioned store & visibility (`mvcc/store.rs`)

`VersionedCfStore` keys a `BTreeMap<(ColumnFamily, Vec<u8>), Vec<VersionedValue{seq,value}>>`
(append-only per-key version chain) plus a `SeqAllocator`, an optional `CfRouter`,
read barriers, a `LeaseRegistry`, `ResourceCounters`, and a `SnapshotGcReclaimer`.
`commit_batch(rows)` writes rows to the router and pushes a `VersionedValue` per
row at one freshly-allocated seq (atomic across any number of CFs).
`restore_batch(seq, rows)` re-inserts durable rows at their original seq during
recovery before live writes begin.

Visibility (`visible_version`): scan the version chain **in reverse** and return
the first version with `seq Ōēż snapshot.seq`, unless it is a tombstone.
Tombstones: `TOMBSTONE_VALUE = b"\0CALYX_ASTER_TOMBSTONE_V1"`,
`tombstone_value()` / `is_tombstone_value()`. A visible tombstone reads as
absent. This is snapshot isolation: a reader pinned at seq S sees exactly the
latest committed version Ōēż S of every key across every CF.

Read API (all take a `Snapshot` + `&dyn Clock`, enforce lease liveness, and check
read barriers): `read_at`, `seq_for_key_at`, `read_batch(&[CfRead])`, `scan_cf_at`,
`scan_cf_range_at`, `scan_cf_range_page_at(after_key, limit)`. `CfRead{cf,key}`.

### 4.3 Reader leases & freshness (`mvcc/lease.rs`, `mvcc/store.rs`)

`ReaderLease{id, pinned_seq, issued_at, max_age_ms}` with
`expires_at = issued_at + max_age_ms`, `is_expired_at`, `ensure_live_at`
(`CALYX_READER_LEASE_EXPIRED` on expiry). `Snapshot{seq, freshness, lease}`.
`pin_snapshot(freshness, clock, max_age_ms)` pins at `current_seq` and registers
the lease for oldest-pinned-seq accounting; `pin_snapshot_at(seq, ŌĆ”)` pins at an
explicit historical seq (time-travel) so version GC cannot reclaim Ōēż seq while
held; `release_lease(id)`; `lease_view(now)`. `AsterVault` exposes `pin_reader`,
`pin_reader_at`, `release_reader`. Internal vault reads use a transient lease id 0
with `DEFAULT_LEASE_MS = 5_000` and `Freshness::FreshDerived`.

`Freshness` governs DERIVED structures (ANN/xterm/kernel/guard) carrying a build
seq: `FreshDerived` requires `derived_seq Ōēź pinned_seq`; `StaleOk{max_lag}` allows
lag up to `max_lag`. `ensure(pinned, derived)` returns `CALYX_STALE_DERIVED` on
violation.

`snapshot_gc_tick(clock, max_gap_seqs)` aborts expired readers, checks the
pinned-seq gap, and returns `SnapshotGcTick{aborted_readers, gap_alert, metrics}`.

### 4.4 Read barriers (`mvcc/read_barrier.rs`)

`ReadBarrier` blocks reads over a `(ColumnFamily, KeyRange)`. `base_corrupt(id,
range)` constructs one for `ColumnFamily::Base` with code
`CALYX_ASTER_BASE_CORRUPT` and remediation "restore from restic/snapshot"
(A16: a corrupt base shard fails reads closed rather than returning wrong data).
`first_blocking(barriers, cf, key)` returns the blocking error if any.
`AsterVault::install_read_barrier`/`remove_read_barrier`/`read_barriers`.

---

## 5. Crash recovery, manifest & versioning (`manifest/`, `vault/durable.rs`)

### 5.1 Manifest format & format version (`manifest/mod.rs`)

The manifest is **JSON** (`serde_json::to_vec_pretty`), not a binary format.
Files in the vault root: `CURRENT` (text pointer), `MANIFEST` (mirror copy of the
current manifest bytes), and immutable `manifest-{seq:020}.json` files
(`MANIFEST_PREFIX="manifest-"`, `MANIFEST_SUFFIX=".json"`).

Format version constant: `ManifestVersion{major:u16, minor:u16}` with
`SUPPORTED_MANIFEST_MAJOR = 1`, `SUPPORTED_MANIFEST_MINOR = 0`
(`ManifestVersion::current()` = `1.0`). `validate()` refuses any **unknown major**
with error code `CALYX_FORMAT_VERSION_UNSUPPORTED` (remediation: "refuse unknown
format major; migrate through a compatible reader"). This is the Aster
format-version gate referenced by [04_storage_and_schema.md](04_storage_and_schema.md).

`VaultManifest` fields: `version`, `manifest_seq:u64` (must be Ōēź 1),
`durable_seq:u64` (highest seq durably checkpointed to SSTs), `panel_ref:ImmutableRef`,
`registry_ref:Option<ImmutableRef>`, `codebook_refs:Vec<ImmutableRef>`,
`temporal_policy:Option`, `dedup_policy:Option`, `retention_horizon`,
`degraded_rebuildable:bool`, `quarantines:Vec<QuarantineRecord>`. `ImmutableRef{
logical_path, blake3_hex}` is content-addressed: path must be vault-relative,
not escape the vault (no `..`/root/prefix), not point at a control file, and the
hash must be 64 lowercase hex chars (32-byte BLAKE3). `panel_ref` must be under
`panel/`, `registry_ref` under `registry/`, codebooks under `codebooks/`
(deduplicated).

### 5.2 Atomic manifest swap (`ManifestStore`)

`write_current(manifest)`: validate, then `write_atomic` (write `*.tmp`,
`sync_all`, `rename`, parent fsync) for the `manifest-NNNN.json`, the `MANIFEST`
mirror, and finally `CURRENT` ŌåÆ the pointer filename. `load_current` reads
`CURRENT`, validates the pointer filename shape, reads the pointed manifest,
decodes + validates, and **verifies every immutable ref's BLAKE3 hash against the
on-disk bytes** (`verify_immutable_refs`) ŌĆö a mismatch is
`CALYX_ASTER_CORRUPT_SHARD`. `append_quarantine` bumps `manifest_seq` and rewrites.
`ManifestWrite{manifest_path, mirror_path, current_path, pointer}`.

### 5.3 Recovery algorithm (`recover_vault` + `DurableVault::recover_batches`)

`recover_vault(vault_dir)`:
1. `ManifestStore::load_current()` ŌĆö load + validate manifest, verify immutable
   refs (panel/registry/codebooks) by hash. If `CURRENT` is absent, recovery
   falls through to a WAL-only path (`DurableVault::recover_batches`).
2. `replay_dir(vault_dir/"wal")` ŌĆö replay all WAL segments, truncating any torn
   tail (┬¦2.5).
3. Keep only WAL records with `seq > manifest.durable_seq` (records already
   checkpointed into SSTs are not replayed).
4. `last_recovered_seq` = last surviving WAL record seq, else `manifest.durable_seq`.
5. Return `RecoveryOutcome{manifest, wal_records, torn_tail, last_recovered_seq,
   degraded_rebuildable}`.

`DurableVault::recover_batches` then materializes batches:
- With a manifest: `read_manifested_batches` reads SSTs across all tier roots,
  classifying names via `storage_names::classify_sst`. `DurableBatch{seq,index}`
  and `Compacted{seq}` files with `seq Ōēż durable_seq` are loaded (router-flush
  `Router{seq}` SSTs are recovered separately by `CfRouter::load_existing`),
  ordered by `(seq, index+row_offset)`. WAL records (seq > durable_seq) are decoded
  via `decode_write_batch` and appended.
- Without a manifest: replay the WAL directly into batches.

On open (`AsterVault::open_with_clock`): recover batches, recover the ledger hook,
open the `CfRouter` (loads existing SSTs), build `VersionedCfStore` at
`last_recovered_seq`, `restore_batch` every recovered batch at its original seq,
`set_start_seq(last_recovered_seq)`, then open `DurableVault`. `VaultRecoveryReport{
last_recovered_seq, torn_tail}` is exposed via `recovery_report()` ŌĆö the torn-tail
diagnostic surfaces on normal open.

### 5.4 Canonical file names (`storage_names.rs`)

Single fail-closed authority for `*.sst`/`*.wal` names in Aster-owned dirs. SST
name classes (`SstName`): `Router{seq}` = `{seq:020}.sst` (router memtable flush);
`DurableBatch{seq,index}` = `{seq:020}-{index:04}.sst` (group-commit batch);
`Compacted{seq}` = `compacted-{seq:020}.sst`. `classify_sst` returns `Ok(None)`
for non-`.sst` files, `Ok(Some)` for canonical names, and a typed
`CALYX_ASTER_CORRUPT_SHARD` error for any `*.sst` that matches no canonical shape
(refusing to silently skip it). `sst_order_key`/`SstOrderKey{seq, class_rank,
index}` give chronological order (`Router=1 < DurableBatch=2 < Compacted=3` within
a seq). `wal_segment_index` parses `{index:020}.wal`. `parse_cf_dir_name` maps a
`cf/<name>` dir back to a `ColumnFamily`, round-tripping through `name()` so a
mis-padded slot dir is rejected.

### 5.5 Quarantine (`manifest/quarantine.rs`)

`QuarantineRecord` ranges of seqs poisoned by corruption; `is_quarantined`,
`is_vault_seq_quarantined`, `manifest.quarantines`. `read_base_shard(path,key)`
reads a base SST through the fail-closed `SstReader`.

---

## 6. Compaction & hot/cold tiering (`compaction/`)

### 6.1 Catalog & snapshot-safe compaction (`compaction/mod.rs`)

`SstShard{cf, path, level:u8, bytes}`. `CompactionCatalog{active:RwLock<Arc<Vec<SstShard>>>}`
with `pin_snapshot()->CompactionSnapshot` (an `Arc` clone; old pinned views
survive a swap ŌåÆ concurrent reads during rebuild). `compact_cf(cf, output_path,
throttle)`:
1. Pin a snapshot, collect input shards for `cf`.
2. `compact_shards(cf, inputs, output_path, throttle)`.
3. On success build the output `SstShard` at `level = max(input levels)+1`, swap
   the active list (drop old `cf` shards, add the compacted one) atomically.

`compact_shards`:
1. `CompactionDebt::measure` over inputs.
2. **Skip** if `< 2` input files, or if `throttle.max_input_bytes` is set and
   pending bytes exceed it (`CompactionResult::Skipped{debt}`).
3. Merge all input SSTs into a `BTreeMap` (later files overwrite ŌĆö newest wins),
   write a single output SST (`write_sst`).
4. Compute `write_amp_milli = output_bytes*1000 / logical_bytes` and return
   `CompactionResult::Compacted(CompactionReport{ŌĆ”})`.

`CompactionReport` fields: `cf, input_files, input_paths, input_bytes,
output_bytes, logical_bytes, write_amp_milli, reclaimed_input_files(=0),
debt_before, debt_after, output_path, staging_parent`.

### 6.2 Debt & scheduler

`CompactionDebt{pending_bytes, target_bytes, score_milli}` where
`score_milli = pending_bytes*WRITE_AMP_SCALE / target_bytes`,
`WRITE_AMP_SCALE = 1_000`, `DEFAULT_COMPACTION_TARGET_BYTES = 64 MiB`.
`CompactionThrottle{max_input_bytes:Option<u64>}` (`unlimited` / `max_input_bytes`).

`CompactionScheduler::start(catalog, options)` runs a background thread:
`CompactionSchedulerOptions{interval_ms=10_000, debt_trigger_score_milli=1_000,
max_write_amp_milli=2_000, backoff_factor=2, max_interval_ms=60_000, output_root,
tiering_policy}`. Each tick: sleep `interval_ms`; for each CF, if `debt.score_milli
Ōēź debt_trigger_score_milli` compact it; if the resulting `write_amp_milli >
max_write_amp_milli`, multiply the interval by `backoff_factor` (capped at
`max_interval_ms`) ŌĆö anti-storm backoff. Output path is placed via the tiering
policy or `output_root/<cf>/compacted-{id:020}.sst`. The cadence is fixed; a
`FIXME(PH46)` notes the intended Anneal adaptive hook is not yet wired.

### 6.3 Hot/cold tiering (`compaction/tiering.rs`)

`StorageTier Ōłł {Hot, Cold}`. `TieringPolicy{hot_root, archive_root, active_slots,
current_panel_version}`; `TieringPolicy::aiwonder(...)` defaults to
`/zfs/hot/calyx` and `/zfs/archive/calyx` (falling back to `$CALYX_HOME/<hot|archive>`
or `/home/croyse/calyx/...` when the ZFS path is absent). `place_cf(cf,
panel_version)->TierPlacement{tier, root, cf_dir=cf/<name>}`;
`absolute_dir() = root.join(cf_dir)`. `place_current_cf` uses
`current_panel_version`.

Cold-vs-hot rule (`is_cold`):
- Always **Hot**: `Base`, `Ledger`, `Anchors`, `Graph`, `Reactive`, and all
  `Anneal*` CFs.
- Always **Cold**: any raw slot CF (`is_raw_slot`).
- A quantized slot CF is **Cold** iff `panel_version < current_panel_version`
  (retired version) OR its slot is not in `active_slots`.
- Everything else: Hot.

`write_tiered_sst(cf, panel_version, file_name, entries)` refuses a non-canonical
SST file name (would be invisible to fail-closed recovery scans), creates the tier
dir, writes the SST, returns `TierWrite{placement, path, bytes, staging_parent}`.
`tier_roots()` returns one root when hot==archive, else both.
`scan.rs`: `catalog_from_vault_dir`, `catalog_from_vault_tiers` build a
`CompactionCatalog` by scanning canonical SSTs across tier roots.

---

## 7. Garbage collection (`gc/`)

Six GC subsystems (public types only; thresholds in parentheses). All are
incremental/bounded with anti-storm controls.

| GC | Reclaims | Key public types / defaults |
|---|---|---|
| `snapshot_gc` | abandoned/expired reader leases, oldest-pinned-seq gap | `SnapshotGcReclaimer`, `SnapshotGcTick`, `SnapshotGcCounters`; `DEFAULT_READER_LEASE_MS=5_000`, `DEFAULT_MAX_PINNED_SEQ_GAP=1_000_000` |
| `wal_recycler` | durable, non-active WAL segments (truncate to 0) | `WalRecycleReport`; `DEFAULT_MAX_RECYCLE_PER_TICK=8`, `DEFAULT_FSYNC_BUDGET_PER_TICK=8`, `DEFAULT_FSYNC_P99_ALERT_US=10_000` |
| `compaction_gc` | tombstone-heavy SSTs (drive compaction) | `TombstoneInventory`, `CompactionGcResult`, `CompactionCadence`; tombstone-ratio trigger Ōēł `0.50` |
| `panel_version_gc` | retired panel versions (hotŌåÆcold, prune) | `PanelVersionRecord`, `RetentionPolicy` (keep 2 hot, cold-tier first) |
| `orphan_reconciler` | dangling slot/indexŌåöbase mismatches | `OrphanReport`, `OrphanRepairResult` |
| `ann_gc` | tombstoned ANN graph nodes (copy-on-write rebuild) | `SharedAnnIndex<T>`, `AnnGcResult`; rebuild interval Ōēł `600_000` ms, max tombstone ratio Ōēł `0.25` |

(Exact constant values live in `gc/<sub>.rs`; the snapshot-GC hook is invoked from
`VersionedCfStore::snapshot_gc_tick`.)

---

## 8. Key-encoding layers & secondary indexes

### 8.1 FoundationDB-style layers (`layers/`)

Each paradigm is a key-encoding layer over the ordered keyspace, with a leading
discriminant byte:

| Layer | Discriminant | Key | Value |
|---|---|---|---|
| Relational (`relational.rs`) | `0x01` | `0x01 ŌĆ¢ collection_id(8) ŌĆ¢ pk` | `be_u16 ROW_SCHEMA_VERSION ŌĆ¢ bincode(Row)` |
| Document (`document.rs`) | `0x02` | `0x02 ŌĆ¢ collection_id(8) ŌĆ¢ doc_id(16) ŌĆ¢ path` | Leaf / Tombstone / Branch cell |
| KV (`kv.rs`) | `0x03` | `0x03 ŌĆ¢ collection_id(8) ŌĆ¢ ns(8) ŌĆ¢ user_key` | `KV_VALUE_VERSION(0x01) ŌĆ¢ be_u64 expires_at_ms ŌĆ¢ payload` (TTL checked on read) |
| TimeSeries (`timeseries.rs`) | `0x04` | `0x04 ŌĆ¢ kind(point=0x00/rollup=0x01) ŌĆ¢ collection_id(8) ŌĆ¢ series(8) ŌĆ¢ be ts/window` | point `be f64`; rollup `count(8) ŌĆ¢ sum(f64) ŌĆ¢ min(f64) ŌĆ¢ max(f64)` |
| Blob (`blob.rs`) | `0x05` | chunk `0x05 ŌĆ¢ 0x00 ŌĆ¢ blob_id(16) ŌĆ¢ be_u32 chunk_idx`; manifest `0x05 ŌĆ¢ 0x01 ŌĆ¢ blob_id(16)` | chunk bytes; manifest `total_bytes(8) ŌĆ¢ chunk_count(4) ŌĆ¢ blake3(32) ŌĆ¢ cold_tier(1) ŌĆ¢ created_at_ms(8)` |

Blob: `BLOB_CHUNK_SIZE = 262_144` (256 KiB), `MAX_BLOB_BYTES = 1 GiB`; chunks
committed before the manifest (content-addressed durability). Time-series rollup
windows are minute/hour/day (`NANOS_PER_MINUTE` etc.), updated atomically per write.

### 8.2 Secondary indexes (`index/`)

`IndexId(u32)` (4-byte BE in keys). `IndexSpec{index_id, name, kind, on_field,
field_type}`.
- **B-tree** (`index_btree`, discriminant `0x10`): key
  `0x10 ŌĆ¢ collection_id(8) ŌĆ¢ index_id(4) ŌĆ¢ memcomparable(field_val) ŌĆ¢ pk`, empty
  value. Field encodings are order-preserving: `I64` sign-flipped then BE; `U64`
  plain BE; `F64` IEEE total-order transform then BE; `Bool` one byte; `Text`/`Bytes`
  first 64 bytes (`MAX_INDEXED_BYTES = 64`) escape-terminated memcomparable.
- **Inverted** (`index_inverted`, discriminant `0x11`): posting key
  `0x11 ŌĆ¢ collection_id(8) ŌĆ¢ index_id(4) ŌĆ¢ term_hash(8) ŌĆ¢ pk`, value `f32 BE`
  (BM25 tf-weight). A reserved all-ones (`u64::MAX`) term hash stores stats
  (`doc_count(8) ŌĆ¢ avgdl(f32)`). `BM25_K1=1.2`, `BM25_B=0.75`.

`btree.rs`, `inverted.rs`, `inverted_maintenance.rs`, `maintenance.rs`,
`rebuild/*`, `terms.rs` provide build/maintain/rebuild logic.

---

## 9. Dedup, time-travel, transactions

### 9.1 Dedup / idempotency (`dedup/`)

`DedupPolicy Ōłł {Off, Exact, TctCosine(TctCosineConfig)}` (re-validated against the
panel on vault open). `DedupResult Ōłł {New(CxId), DedupMerge{into,occurrence},
ExactDuplicate(CxId)}`. Content addressing: `CxId::from_input(bytes,
panel_version, salt)` and `full_content_hash` (BLAKE3 over length-delimited parts).
Recurrence signature detection (`signature.rs`) compares temporal-slot cosine and
event time. Compression aggregates (re-exported in `lib.rs`): `CompressionRatio`,
`Domain`, `DomainCompressionStats`, `compression_ratio`,
`domain_compression_stats`. Anchor-conflict threshold `ANCHOR_VECTOR_TAU = 0.70`.
Error codes include `CALYX_DEDUP_DPI_EXCEEDED`, `CALYX_DEDUP_ANCHOR_CONFLICT`,
`CALYX_RECURRENCE_SLOT_MISSING`.

### 9.2 Time-travel (`timetravel/`)

`TimeIndex` CF rows are `be_u64(millis_utc) ŌĆ¢ be_u64(seqno)` ŌåÆ 1-byte sentinel.
`AsterVault::as_of(t_millis)` ŌåÆ `TimeTravelSnapshot` resolves the greatest seqno
with `millis Ōēż t`, pins a reader lease there, releases on drop. `RetentionHorizon
Ōłł {Rolling{min_age}, Absolute{horizon_millis}, None}` lower-bounds `as_of`
(`CALYX_TIMETRAVEL_BEFORE_HORIZON` when violated); `safe_to_gc_before_millis`
feeds version GC. `TimeIndexEntry{millis, seqno}`.

### 9.3 Transactions (`txn/`)

`TxnHandle` is a vault-scoped serial transaction manager (one active txn per
vault, condvar-gated) with state `Idle | Active{started_at, cost_cap_ms}`.
`CrossModelTxn` batches writes across paradigm layers (`put_record`, `put_doc`,
`kv_set`, `ts_write`, `blob_put`, ŌĆ”); validation enforces schema, dedup policy,
and index maintenance (`validation.rs`). All layer writes for one logical change
commit in one MVCC batch (data key + index key in one transaction). Error codes:
`CALYX_TXN_TIMEOUT`, `CALYX_TXN_COST_CAP`.

---

## 10. Resource accounting, pressure, residency, redaction, erase

- `resource/` ŌĆö `ResourceCounters` (atomic `memtable_absorbed_total`,
  `memtable_rejected_total`, `disk_pressure_events_total`), `BackpressureStatus`,
  `LeaseRegistry`/`LeaseView`, `MemtableStatus`/`MemtableCfStatus`,
  `collect_resource_status`/`ResourceStatus`/`VramBudgetStatus`.
- `pressure.rs` ŌĆö `DiskPressureGuard` (high-water ratio default 0.85),
  `DiskSample`; `CALYX_DISK_PRESSURE` admission gate with spill request.
- `residency.rs` ŌĆö immutable data-residency pin (`Residency{dataset_root,
  allow_off_dataset}`, sidecar `residency.json`); `authorize(target)` fails closed
  with `CALYX_RESIDENCY_VIOLATION` and writes a path-digest-only Ledger audit
  entry (no raw paths in the ledger).
- `retention.rs` ŌĆö per-collection TTL/rollup sweep (`RetentionPolicy`,
  `RetentionStore`).
- `security/` ŌĆö `LensStoreGuard` (cross-vault vector guard), ZFS encryption probe.
- `redaction.rs` ŌĆö input PII modes (`InputMode Ōłł {Full, HashOnly([u8;32]),
  Redacted}`, `redact_to_hash` = BLAKE3, `CALYX_PII_REDACTION_REQUIRED`). Per
  product policy, local-only/opt-in redaction is intentional, not a defect.
- `erase.rs` ŌĆö lawful erasure (`EraseScope Ōłł {Vault, Cx(CxId), Subject(SubjectId)}`,
  `EraseResult`, `EraseRegistry`); distinct from compaction.

### 10.1 Error taxonomy (codes surfaced by this crate)

`CALYX_ASTER_TORN_WAL`, `CALYX_ASTER_CORRUPT_SHARD`, `CALYX_ASTER_BASE_CORRUPT`,
`CALYX_FORMAT_VERSION_UNSUPPORTED`, `CALYX_BACKPRESSURE`, `CALYX_DISK_PRESSURE`,
`CALYX_STALE_DERIVED`, `CALYX_READER_LEASE_EXPIRED`, `CALYX_NOT_FOUND`,
`CALYX_IO_ERROR`, `CALYX_BOUNDS_EXCEEDED`, `CALYX_VAULT_KEYSPACE_MISMATCH`,
`CALYX_QUOTA_EXCEEDED`, `CALYX_ENCRYPTION_FAILED`, `CALYX_DECRYPTION_FAILED`,
`CALYX_VAULT_KEY_MISSING`, `CALYX_RESIDENCY_VIOLATION`,
`CALYX_TIMETRAVEL_BEFORE_HORIZON`, `CALYX_TXN_TIMEOUT`, `CALYX_TXN_COST_CAP`,
`CALYX_PII_REDACTION_REQUIRED`, plus the dedup codes above. (Many are constructed
via `calyx-core::CalyxError`; see [05_core.md](05_core.md).)

---

## 11. Gaps / not covered

- **Quantization / compression are not implemented in this crate.** Slot CF
  values are stored as big-endian IEEE bit patterns (`vault/encode.rs`); the PRD's
  PQ-8 / Float8 / binary quantization and zstd raw-sidecar compression are not
  present here. "Quantized" vs "Raw" slot CFs differ only by directory/tier
  policy, not by an encoding in this code.
- **ANN / DiskANN / SPANN indexes are not in calyx-aster.** The `idx/` directory
  tree, HNSW/DiskANN graphs, and sparse posting lists from the PRD live in
  `calyx-sextant` ([09_sextant_search.md](09_sextant_search.md)); aster only holds
  the `Kernel`/`Guard` CFs and the secondary B-tree/inverted indexes (┬¦8.2). ANN
  GC here operates on a `SharedAnnIndex<T>` abstraction, not an on-disk ANN format.
- **Single-level SstLevel.** `SstLevel` is one newest-first stack per CF; multi-
  level LSM fan-out (L0/L1/ŌĆ”) is not implemented; `level:u8` is metadata only.
- **Manifest is JSON, not binary.** No binary manifest magic; the format gate is
  the `ManifestVersion` major/minor (1.0).
- **Compaction cadence is fixed.** `FIXME(PH46)` ŌĆö the Anneal adaptive cadence
  hook is not wired; the scheduler uses fixed interval + write-amp backoff.
- `lib.rs` self-describes as a "skeleton"; several modules (`olap`, `plain_column`,
  `plain_graph`, `stream`, `stride_fsv`, `supply_chain`, `ledger_view`) were not
  deep-read for this doc and may contain partial implementations.

See also [04_storage_and_schema.md](04_storage_and_schema.md) (consolidated
on-disk format), [05_core.md](05_core.md) (CxId/SlotVector/error types),
[09_sextant_search.md](09_sextant_search.md) (ANN), and
[01_system_overview.md](01_system_overview.md).

<!-- ===== END 06_aster_storage_engine.md ===== -->

# 07 ŌĆö Forge Math Runtime (calyx-forge)

`calyx-forge` is Calyx's owned numeric runtime: one math backend implemented
twice ŌĆö a CPU SIMD path (via the `wide` crate) and a CUDA path (via `cudarc`,
gated behind the `cuda` feature) ŌĆö engineered for bit-near parity, plus a
quantization stack from full precision (fp32) down to 1-bit. It also contains a
VRAM budgeter/admission subsystem, an autotune cache, and a compression report
generator.

**Source files covered:**

- `crates/calyx-forge/src/lib.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/Cargo.toml`
- `crates/calyx-forge/build.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/backend.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/error.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/cpu/mod.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/cpu/distance.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/cpu/gemm.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/cpu/normalize.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/cpu/topk.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/cpu/guard.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/cuda/mod.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/cuda/context.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/cuda/kernels.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/cuda/distance.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/cuda/gemm.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/cuda/gemm/mxfp4_path.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/cuda/gemm/mxfp8_path.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/cuda/topk.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/cuda/grouped_gemm.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/cuda/ragged_gemm.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/cuda/kernels/distance.cu`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/cuda/kernels/topk.cu`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/cuda/kernels/mxfp4_gemm.cu`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/cuda/mxfp4.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/cuda/mxfp8.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/quant/mod.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/quant/binary.rs`
- `crates/calyx-forge/src/quant/turboquant.rs`

- `crates/calyx-forge/src/quant/rotation.rs`

- `crates/calyx-forge/src/vram/mod.rs`
