---

# Planning Docs Summary ŌĆö `docs/dbprdplans/` + `docs/implementation/`

**Source files covered:**
- `docs/dbprdplans/00_INDEX.md`, `docs/dbprdplans/DOCTRINE.md`, and the 32 numbered PRD plans `docs/dbprdplans/01_*.md` ŌĆ” `docs/dbprdplans/31_*.md`
- `docs/implementation/00_README.md`, `docs/implementation/02_WORKING_AGREEMENT.md`, `docs/implementation/03_PHASE_MAP.md`, and the stage docs `10_STAGE0_*` ŌĆ” `30_STAGE20_*`, plus `01_AIWONDER_ENVIRONMENT.md`, `02_BUILD_PERFORMANCE.md`, `FSV_NOTES.md`, `STAGE1_5_EVIDENCE_MANIFEST.md`
- `docs2/` reference files

> **What this doc is.** A NAVIGATION/INTENT map of the *original design plans* for Calyx ŌĆö the PRD (`docs/dbprdplans/`) and the build plan (`docs/implementation/`). These are markdown design documents, **not code**. They state design *intent*: what Calyx is meant to be and in what order it is meant to be built. Where the shipped code diverges from a plan, that divergence is documented in the per-subsystem reference docs `05_*.md`ŌĆō`20_*.md` (cross-referenced by subsystem below). Per the spec's iron rule (`_SPEC.md ┬¦11`): document WHAT IS in those docs; this doc summarizes the PLANS. Do not read a plan statement as a claim that the code does it.

---

## 1. The two doc sets

| Set | Path | Role | Count |
|---|---|---|---|
| **PRD plans** | `docs/dbprdplans/` | *What* and *why* ŌĆö the product requirements, vision, axioms, per-subsystem design | 32 numbered docs (`00`ŌĆō`31`) + `DOCTRINE.md` (33 files total) |
| **Implementation plan** | `docs/implementation/` | *In what order, on what machine, proven how* ŌĆö phases/stages mapped to crates with FSV exit gates | 21 stage docs (`10_STAGE0` ŌĆ” `30_STAGE20`) + `00_README`, `02_WORKING_AGREEMENT`, `03_PHASE_MAP`, `01_AIWONDER_ENVIRONMENT`, `02_BUILD_PERFORMANCE`, `FSV_NOTES`, `STAGE1_5_EVIDENCE_MANIFEST`, + 60+ per-phase `PHnn-*/` task-card subdirs |

`DOCTRINE.md` is the canonical binding charter ŌĆö it overrides every other doc. The PRD's master index is `00_INDEX.md`. The implementation read order is: `DOCTRINE.md` ŌåÆ `00_README.md` ŌåÆ `01_AIWONDER_ENVIRONMENT.md` ŌåÆ `02_WORKING_AGREEMENT.md` ŌåÆ `03_PHASE_MAP.md` ŌåÆ the stage files in order.

---

## 2. DOCTRINE ŌĆö the binding principles (verbatim where short)

`DOCTRINE.md` is "the canonical, binding charter" and "overrides every other doc in this project." Core principles, stated verbatim:

### 2.1 The cardinal rule (┬¦0)
> **A return value is a claim. The source of truth is the bytes. Read the bytes.**

This is **FSV** (Full State Verification): "No FSV script/harness can satisfy FSV; a human or agent reads the bytes." Inherited from Leapable doctrine, non-negotiable.

### 2.2 The thesis (┬¦1)
> **Calyx is the heart of the formula for intelligence, implemented as a database.**

Three-in-one: (1) the engine of the **Calculus of Association** ŌĆö the four native verbs **measure ┬Ę count ┬Ę differentiate ┬Ę compose**; (2) the **universal database** serving every paradigm's root purpose on one ordered transactional core; (3) the **AGI / Oracle / kernel substrate**.

### 2.3 Living intelligence (┬¦1b, A31)
Every life-like property maps to a concrete engine (the Living System Map: perception=lenses, memory=store, cognition=Loom/Sextant, differentiation=Assay, homeostasis=Anneal, foresight=Oracle, immune boundary=Ward). The bound (binding, honesty): claims **operational intelligence + life-like behavior**, **never consciousness/sentience/qualia**.

### 2.4 The drive (┬¦1c, A32)
> maximize the growth of grounded intelligence/understanding, as fast as safely possible.

Measurable objective `J`; fastest-first; "recode itself" means **online re-parameterization** (fusion weights, quant levels, `Žä`, heads), **never engine-source rewriting**. Compression & retrieval are **facets, not trade-offs**.

### 2.5 Zero-cost & self-built (┬¦1d, A34)
> **Everything is free, and we build it ourselves in Rust.**

No paid services/SaaS/cloud DB/CI/scanners. Every engine hand-built in Rust. Only conceivable paid item: a great embedder (doubted to exist).

### 2.6 Strict source-of-theory (┬¦2, A24)
Theory is **strictly and only** the Royse corpus (papers *Calculus of Association*, *The Oracle and the Kernel*, *The Symmetry of Knowing*; proven systems ContextGraph/Polis/ClipCannon/Leapable; the video transcripts). No external theory of intelligence imported. External technique is frozen to founder-requested/platform-reality scaffolding only (TurboQuant, grouped GEMM / Blackwell / CUDA / ZFS, FoundationDB-style key-encoding pattern).

### 2.7 Other binding rules
- **┬¦3 Universality mandate** ŌĆö serve the root purpose of every paradigm (relational/document/KV/columnar/graph/time-series/full-text/vector/blob) from first principles, not by bolting on engines. Full-text search = a sparse lens; a vector DB = a 1-lens Calyx.
- **┬¦4 AGI/Oracle/kernel mandate** ŌĆö bake in the Oracle, the kernel at any scope, automatic intelligence extraction.
- **┬¦5 The backbone rule** ŌĆö *plug-in lenses is THE key*: a new lens is one call (`add_lens`), its value one number (`bits`), the kernel one call at any scope. Reject any change that makes this harder.
- **┬¦6 The 34 axioms (A1ŌĆōA34)** ŌĆö full text in `02_VISION_AND_AXIOMS.md`. Key ones: A1 record=constellation ┬Ę A2 grounding mandatory ┬Ę **A3 no-flatten** ┬Ę A4 frozen lenses ┬Ę A5 hot-swap ┬Ę A7 differentiation contract (**Ōēź0.05 bits, Ōēż0.6 corr**) ┬Ę A8 DPI ceiling ┬Ę A10 kernel at any scope ┬Ę A12 `GŽä` everywhere generation touches the store ┬Ę A13 Rust + baked-in GPU math ┬Ę A15 source-of-truth verification ┬Ę **A16 fail closed** ┬Ę A19 universality ┬Ę A20 the Oracle ┬Ę A24 strict Royse theory ┬Ę A25 measured compression ┬Ę A33 security/privacy by construction ┬Ę A34 zero-cost.
- **┬¦7 Bake the formulas in** ŌĆö every Royse formula is a callable, self-tuning backend primitive.
- **┬¦8 Engineering rules** ŌĆö **fail closed** (unknown lens, dim mismatch, ungrounded result, corrupt shard ŌåÆ structured `CALYX_*` error, never a silent fallback); provenance always (Ledger); FSV (harnesses banned); **code/test files Ōēż 500 lines (HARD)**, docs unlimited; one change at a time.
- **┬¦8b/┬¦8c/┬¦8d/┬¦8e** ŌĆö protocols (`AICodingAgentSuperPrompt.md`, `modulateprompt.md`, `compressionprompt.md`); **no CI ŌĆö FSV is CI**; everything runs on **aiwonder** (WSL authors only); secrets via Infisical (`hf_hub_token`); dev state in GitHub Issues; **Synapse is the computer-use & orchestration runtime** (preferred over the subagent tool).
- **┬¦9 Anti-patterns (refuse)** ŌĆö flattening the panel; selling `C(N,2)` past the DPI ceiling; labeling ungrounded results "trusted"; mutating a frozen lens; substituting an external theory; making lens plug-in harder; a green-checkmark harness standing in for FSV; >500-line file without a tracking issue; bolting on a separate search/graph/vector DB.

The **`BUILD_DONE` predicate** (`00_INDEX.md`, full def in `19_ROADMAP_FSV_BUILD_DONE.md`) is a mechanical conjunction of ~30 clauses (CORE Ōł¦ LENS Ōł¦ DDA Ōł¦ BITS Ōł¦ KERNEL Ōł¦ GUARD Ōł¦ SEARCH Ōł¦ UNIVERSAL Ōł¦ ORACLE Ōł¦ ŌĆ” Ōł¦ FSV); Calyx is "complete" only when all are true.

---

## 3. PRD plan docs ŌĆö `docs/dbprdplans/` (table, grouped by theme)

Filename ŌåÆ title ŌåÆ what it specifies (design intent). Cross-references point to the per-subsystem reference doc that documents the shipped code.

### 3.1 Foundation & vision
| Doc | Title | What it specifies | Reference doc |
|---|---|---|---|
| `00_INDEX.md` | Master PRD Index | Product framing, reading order, the canonical glossary (Lens/Slot/Panel/Constellation/Cross-term/DDA/`GŽä`/kernel/Oracle), hardware ground truth, the `BUILD_DONE` predicate. | ŌĆö |
| `01_BRAND_AND_NAMING.md` | Brand & naming | Establishes the name *Calyx* and the celestial-instrument subsystem codenames (Aster, Loom, Assay, Lodestar, Ward, Sextant, Ledger, Anneal, Forge, Registry); controlled vocabulary, one term per concept. | ŌĆö |
| `02_VISION_AND_AXIOMS.md` | Vision & 34 axioms | The four verbs (measure/count/differentiate/compose) as first-class DB operations; "why not a vector DB"; the binding axioms A1ŌĆōA34 every later doc is checked against. | `01_system_overview.md` |
| `03_DATA_MODEL.md` | Data model | The logical hierarchy Vault ŌåÆ Collection ŌåÆ Panel ŌåÆ Slot ŌåÆ Lens ŌåÆ Constellation/TCT; slot-vectors, cross-terms, scalars, anchors, provenance; content-addressed IDs for idempotency. | `05_core.md`, `04_storage_and_schema.md` |

### 3.2 Engine (storage, math, lenses, search)
| Doc | Title | What it specifies | Reference doc |
|---|---|---|---|
| `04_ASTER_STORAGE_FORMAT.md` | Aster on-disk format | A custom columnar transactional LSM (`.aster`): one ordered keyspace, association-native column families (base/slot/anchors/cross-term/kernel/bits/guard/ledger), tiering, ZFS layout, crash safety. | `06_aster_storage_engine.md`, `04_storage_and_schema.md` |
| `13_FORGE_MATH_RUNTIME.md` | Forge math runtime | Baked-in matmul/BLAS/SIMD/GPU (CUDA sm_120 + AVX-512 + ONNX), quantization, autotuned kernels, CPUŌåöGPU bit-parity contract; no external math service on the hot path. | `07_forge_math_runtime.md` |
| `05_EMBEDDER_REGISTRY.md` | Registry / lenses | Lenses as designable, frozen, content-addressed instruments; hot-swap add/retire with lazy backfill; the frozen contract; capability assay. | `08_registry_lenses.md` |
| `10_SEXTANT_SEARCH_NAV.md` | Sextant search/nav | Multi-lens search, RRF/WeightedRRF/SingleLens fusion, per-slot ANN, sparse lexical lens, query planner/explain, navigation modes; the universal query surface. | `09_sextant_search.md` |

### 3.3 Intelligence (associations, bits, kernel, guard, oracle, math)
| Doc | Title | What it specifies | Reference doc |
|---|---|---|---|
| `06_LOOM_DDA_ENGINE.md` | Loom / DDA | Derived Data Abundance: cross-term weaving (`C(N,2)` associations-between-associations), lazy/eager materialization, effective-rank cap, DPI bound. | `10_loom_associations.md` |
| `07_ASSAY_SIGNAL_BITS.md` | Assay / signal bits | MI estimation (KSG / partitioned-NMI), the differentiation contract (Ōēź0.05 bits, Ōēż0.6 corr), `n_eff`, sufficiency, oracle self-consistency. | `11_assay_signal_bits.md` |
| `08_LODESTAR_KERNEL.md` | Lodestar / kernel | Grounding-kernel discovery via directed MFVS (~1% feedback-vertex-set), kernel-as-index + kernel-based answering, kernel at ANY scope. | `12_lodestar_kernel.md`, `17_graph_mincut_paths.md` |
| `09_WARD_TCT_GUARD.md` | Ward / `GŽä` guard | Per-output cosine guard `GŽä`, per-slot conformal `Žä` calibration, noveltyŌåÆnew-region, injection defense, identity-locked generation. | `13_ward_guard.md` |
| `21_ORACLE_AND_AGI.md` | Oracle & AGI | Consequence prediction (world model / butterfly effect), oracle self-consistency ceiling, panel sufficiency `I(panel;oracle)`, falsifiable per-domain super-intelligence predicate, epistemic symmetry (QŌåöA). | `16_oracle_prediction.md` |

---

## 4. Implementation stage docs ŌĆö `docs/implementation/`

The implementation plan reorganizes the PRD into **phases PH00ŌĆōPH72** grouped into **stages S0ŌĆōS20**, each mapped to crate(s) with a single byte-level FSV exit gate. Phase IDs are stable handles used in GitHub issues/commits. The dependency spine (critical path): `S0 ŌåÆ S1 Aster ŌåÆ S2 Forge ŌåÆ S3 Registry ŌåÆ S4 Sextant ŌåÆ S5 Loom/Assay`, with Lodestar/Ward/Ledger/universal/resource branching off.

### 4.1 Working-agreement rules (`02_WORKING_AGREEMENT.md`)
A phase is DONE only when **all** hold:
1. `cargo check` + `cargo clippy -D warnings` + `cargo test` green **on aiwonder**.
2. **Ōēż500-line file-size gate** passes (`scripts/linecount.sh`); over-limit ŌåÆ `type:task` issue + modularize first.
3. **CPUŌåöGPU bit-parity** holds for Forge-touching code (Ōēż1e-3 rel tol).
4. **FSV exit gate met** ŌĆö proven by reading persisted bytes on aiwonder, not a return value, not a harness; evidence attached to the GitHub issue.
5. **Provenance + fail-closed** wired: Ledger entry on every mutation; every error path returns a structured `CALYX_*` code, never a silent fallback (A16).
6. **Context issues updated** (`[CONTEXT] You are here`).

Other binding rules carried into every phase:
- **FSV protocol (5 steps, via Synapse):** identify bytes ŌåÆ read before ŌåÆ execute ŌåÆ read after ŌåÆ inspect delta. **FSV harnesses are banned.**
- **Tests support FSV, don't replace it:** two questions (fails-when-wrong, passes-when-right); FIRST + properties; seed all RNG, inject the clock (never `SystemTime::now()` in logic); proptest/cargo-fuzz/cargo-mutants/criterion (all free OSS). Zero tolerance for flakiness.
- **No CI ŌĆö FSV is our CI** (`scripts/check.sh` run on aiwonder, agent-invoked).
- **Code reuse:** lift proven ContextGraph (`mincut`/`paths`/`solver`/`witness`) + `mejepa` (Assay/kernel/guard) seeds by **copying source** into Calyx crates, never linking the live project.
- **Dev-state on GitHub Issues** (`chrisroyse/calyx-dev`): pinned `type:context` issues; edit to truth, never append contradictions; prune every phase.
- **Orchestration via Synapse:** open real terminals, command Claude (`cldy`)/Codex (`codex --yolo`) workers ŌĆö preferred over the subagent tool. Humans direct + approve outward/destructive actions only.
- **Doctrine compliance checklist** before closing any phase: no panel flattening (A3); no `C(N,2)` past DPI (A8); nothing "trusted" without grounding (A2 ŌåÆ say `provisional`); no frozen-lens mutation; no external theory (A24); lens plug-in/bits/kernel never made harder; no harness for FSV; no >500-line file without an issue; no bolt-on search/graph/vector DB.

### 4.2 Stage docs (table)
Stage doc ŌåÆ stage name ŌåÆ what it covers ŌåÆ crate(s). (Status as of `03_PHASE_MAP.md` dated 2026-06-10: S0ŌĆōS8 Ō£ģ DONE/FSV-signed-off; S9 Ō¢Č ACTIVE; S10ŌĆōS20 pending.)

| Stage doc | Stage | What it covers (phases) | Crate(s) |

| `11_STAGE1_ASTER.md` | S1 Aster | WAL + group-commit, memtable + LSM SSTable, column families + key codecs, MVCC snapshots, constellation CRUD + idempotent ingest, manifest + crash recovery, compaction + hot/cold tiering. PH05ŌĆōPH11. | `calyx-aster` (+ `calyx-cli`, `calyx-testkit`) |
| `12_STAGE2_FORGE.md` | S2 Forge | CPU SIMD backend (gemm/cosine/l2/normalize/topk, AVX-512), CUDA sm_120 + bit-parity, TurboQuant, MXFP4/grouped GEMM, per-shape autotune cache. PH12ŌĆōPH16. | `calyx-forge` |
| `13_STAGE3_REGISTRY.md` | S3 Registry | Uniform `Registry.measure` over algorithmic/TEI-HTTP/candle-local/ONNX runtimes, frozen contract + content-addressed `LensId`, hot-swap add/retire/park + lazy backfill, capability cards, default panels + temporal lenses E2/E3/E4. PH17ŌĆōPH22. | `calyx-registry` |

| `15_STAGE5_LOOM_ASSAY.md` | S5 Loom + Assay | Agreement graph + lazy cross-terms + abundance reports; KSG MI, partitioned NMI, bootstrap CI, logistic probe, differentiation contract, `n_eff`, sufficiency, attribution. PH27ŌĆōPH30. | `calyx-loom`, `calyx-assay` |

| `20_STAGE10_ANNEAL_J.md` | S10 Anneal + `J` | Tripwires + shadow-first + reversible rollback; self-heal; mistake-closure + online heads; autotune loops; `J` objective + growth curve + `intelligence_report`. PH43ŌĆōPH48. | `calyx-anneal` |

## 6. How plan Ōåö code divergence is captured

These docs are **design intent**, not a claim of shipped behavior. Per `_SPEC.md`, where the implemented code diverges from a plan, the divergence lives in the per-subsystem reference docs:

- Storage format / on-disk reality ŌåÆ [04_storage_and_schema.md](04_storage_and_schema.md), [06_aster_storage_engine.md](06_aster_storage_engine.md)
- Lenses / Registry ŌåÆ [08_registry_lenses.md](08_registry_lenses.md)
- Search ŌåÆ [09_sextant_search.md](09_sextant_search.md)
- DDA / bits ŌåÆ [10_loom_associations.md](10_loom_associations.md), [11_assay_signal_bits.md](11_assay_signal_bits.md)
- Kernel / graph ŌåÆ [12_lodestar_kernel.md](12_lodestar_kernel.md), [17_graph_mincut_paths.md](17_graph_mincut_paths.md)
- Guard ŌåÆ [13_ward_guard.md](13_ward_guard.md)
- Provenance ŌåÆ [14_ledger_provenance.md](14_ledger_provenance.md)
- Self-opt / Oracle ŌåÆ [15_anneal_optimization.md](15_anneal_optimization.md), [16_oracle_prediction.md](16_oracle_prediction.md)
- MCP / CLI / daemon ŌåÆ [19_mcp_api_tools_reference.md](19_mcp_api_tools_reference.md), [20_cli_and_daemon_reference.md](20_cli_and_daemon_reference.md)
- Counts/health snapshot ŌåÆ [22_verification_report.md](22_verification_report.md); remaining work ŌåÆ [24_roadmap.md](24_roadmap.md)

A concrete plan-vs-shipped example already visible in the plan's own status text (`16_STAGE6_LODESTAR.md` / `00_README.md`): the kernel's "Ōēł1% compact-kernel" is a **raw target**, while signed acceptance is the **measured final/tuned recall** with explicit `raw_recall`/`tuned_recall`/`pass_mode` ŌĆö documented in [12_lodestar_kernel.md](12_lodestar_kernel.md).

## Gaps / not covered
- This is a navigation/intent map; it does **not** restate the full content of any plan doc. Read the source doc for detail.
- The 60+ `PHnn-*/` per-phase task-card subdirs are summarized at the convention level only, not card-by-card.
- The PDFs (`docs2/*.pdf`) are summarized from filename + DOCTRINE ┬¦2 context, not from reading the PDF bodies.
- Plan docs describe intent; for shipped behavior and any divergence, see the per-subsystem docs in ┬¦6.

# 24 ŌĆö Roadmap & Remaining Work (Open Issues + Planning State)

**Sources covered:**
- GitHub open issues (`ChrisRoyse/Calyx-Dev`, 25 open as of 2026-06-16; 29 open at `32cc7dea`; **38 open as of 2026-06-29 through `dd500623`**) ŌĆö dump in `_open_issues.json`; bodies read via `gh issue view`. The grouped breakdown below reflects the 2026-06-16 snapshot; ┬¦1.2 lists what landed and the new issues filed since.
- `docs/dbprdplans/19_ROADMAP_FSV_BUILD_DONE.md` (phasing, FSV protocol, `BUILD_DONE` predicate, performance targets).
- `docs/implementation/03_PHASE_MAP.md` (PH00ŌĆōPH72, stage status, FSV gates).
- `docs/dbprdplans/29_STATE_GITHUB_ISSUES.md` (issue-tracker discipline).
- `docs/implementation/FSV_NOTES.md` (what "FSV-verified" means).
- `README.md` "Project status" section.
- Pinned context issues #689, #688, #23 ("You are here").
- "Gaps / not covered" sections of sibling docs 05ŌĆō20 in this set.

> **Status-source caveat.** This doc reports two states that disagree because the
> planning docs lag the live tracker. The committed phase map
> (`03_PHASE_MAP.md`, dated 2026-06-10) records the frontier at **Stage 9 PH40ŌĆōPH42**.
> The pinned `[CONTEXT] You are here` issue #23 (last verified 2026-06-10, commit
> `5ebd8e85`) records work having since advanced into **Stage 10 PH43 (Anneal)**,
> with PH43 T01ŌĆōT05 (#394ŌĆō#398) closed and PH43 T06 (#399) `status:in-progress`.
> Where they differ, the live issue state is the more current claim; neither is a
> byte-level FSV verdict, which is the only authority per `DOCTRINE ┬¦0`.

## 1. Current status (what is built)

Per the phase map (`03_PHASE_MAP.md`) and README "Project status", Calyx is **pre-1.0,
under active development**; on-disk format and public interfaces may still change.

| Stage | Phases | Crate(s) | Status (per phase map / #23) |
|---|---|---|---|
| S0 Foundation | PH00ŌĆōPH04 | calyx-core | DONE |
| S1 Aster | PH05ŌĆōPH11 | calyx-aster | DONE, FSV-signed-off |
| S2 Forge | PH12ŌĆōPH16 | calyx-forge | DONE, FSV-signed-off (CPU SIMD + CUDA sm_120 + TurboQuant + MXFP4/grouped GEMM + autotune) |
| S3 Registry | PH17ŌĆōPH22 | calyx-registry | DONE, FSV-signed-off |
| S4 Sextant | PH23ŌĆōPH26 | calyx-sextant | DONE, FSV-signed-off |
| S5 Loom + Assay | PH27ŌĆōPH30 | calyx-loom, calyx-assay | DONE, FSV-signed-off |
| S6 Lodestar | PH31ŌĆōPH34 | calyx-paths, calyx-mincut, calyx-lodestar | DONE, FSV-signed-off |
| S7 Ledger | PH35ŌĆōPH36 | calyx-ledger | DONE, FSV-signed-off |
| S8 Ward | PH37ŌĆōPH39 | calyx-ward | DONE, FSV-signed-off |
| S9 Temporal & Dedup | PH40ŌĆōPH42 | aster/loom/sextant (cross) | Closed out per #23 (PH40ŌĆōPH42 + follow-ups FSV-backed) |
| S10 Anneal + Objective J | PH43ŌĆōPH48 | calyx-anneal | **Active frontier** ŌĆö PH43 T01ŌĆōT05 closed; PH43 T06 (#399) in-progress |
| S11ŌĆōS20 | PH49ŌĆōPH72 | various | Pending |

README's prose summary matches: storage, math, lens registry, multi-signal search,
association/information layers (Loom/Assay), grounding kernel (Lodestar), guard
(Ward), ledger, self-optimization (Anneal), and **first** oracle capabilities are
"built and working"; the rest is expansion toward 1.0 (┬¦3).

The kernel-first search funnel referenced in planning (KernelFirst@1e8 SLO target) is
the subject of the active scale work (PH68, issue #550), not yet closed.

### 1.1 Landed since the 2026-06-16 issue snapshot (through `96cbc84f`, 2026-06-27)

The issue groupings in ┬¦2 are the 2026-06-16 dump; several items have since landed and the
following are now in the tree (verified against code at `96cbc84f`):

- **Read-only HTTP API** ŌĆö a new `calyx-web-api` crate (issue #889 and follow-ups
  #890ŌĆō#937) serves 6 loopback `/v1/*` routes (`health`, `measure`, `search`, `guard`,
  `kernel`, `provenance/{id}`) behind fail-closed bearer auth, per-request guardrails, and a
  bounded TTL cache. Each route is wired to the real engine (Ward verdict for `/v1/guard`
  #574, measured kernel recall for `/v1/kernel` #575/#1900, Ledger answer-trace for
  `/v1/provenance` #577, HHEM faithfulness liveness in `/v1/health` #579/#1908). See
  [25_web_api.md](25_web_api.md).
- **Shared search path** ŌĆö `calyx-search` (#573/#900) was extracted so the CLI and
  `/v1/search` run one Sextant recall ŌåÆ fusion ŌåÆ rerank ŌåÆ provenance path. Vector fusion is
  now fail-closed until `PlanStep::VectorFusion` is wired to real slot indexes.
- **Kernel at corpus scale** (#871, #943) ŌĆö scalable `betweenness_auto` (sampled pivots),
  `O(V+E)` candidate scoring, iterative Tarjan SCC / cycle check (no stack overflow on the
  ~199k-node corpus), the `calyx kernel-build` command grounding the kernel on the persisted
  graph with an exact-index recall gate, and the `blind-spot-sweep` sweep command.
- **Ingest & ops** ŌĆö raw audio/video ingest (`calyx.ingest_media` MCP tool +
  `ingest_media`), `rebuild-search-index` with streamed sidecar serialization to fix an
  ingest-finalization hang (#939), and `panel warm` warm-readiness guardrails + cross-platform
  GPU runtime hardening (#938, #941).

These advance, but do not by themselves close, the 1.0 scope in ┬¦3; treat ┬¦2 as the
baseline tracker state.

### 1.2 Landed since `96cbc84f` through `dd500623` (65 commits, 2026-06-27 ŌåÆ 2026-06-29)

Verified against the commit log between `32cc7dea` and `dd500623`. These are
ingest/discovery/ops hardening lines, not new 1.0 scope:

- **Resident GPU lens-worker service for CLI ingest** (#1004) ŌĆö batch ingest now routes
  through a warm, long-lived resident worker service (`panel_commands/resident/*`,
  `cmd/ingest/worker/resident.rs`, `constellation/resident_batch.rs`) rather than cold
  per-batch spawns; `measure` moved to a binary resident IPC path. Follow-ups remain open:
  warm from the active vault panel/registry (#1029, p0), replace JSON IPC for large
  multi-vector payloads (#1002), ONNX Runtime I/O-binding for warm inference (#1011).

  preservation and readback verification (#999, #986); fail-closed JSONL batch preflight
  before vault startup, rejecting mixed-batch identity conflicts (#1009); persisted
  lens-ingest isolation and runtime diagnostics (#978).

  derived-text artifacts with modeled, persisted provenance (`media_artifact.rs`,
  `media_derived_text.rs`); derived-text routing enforced.
- **Registry contract audit & repair** (#1000, #990) ŌĆö audit and repair persisted registry
  contract drift without runtime sessions, avoid artifact rehash during audits, materialize
  built-in panel registry snapshots.

  plus FSV docs for the probe matrix (#879), grounded discovery chain (#878), spectral
  community mining (#877), and cross-domain bridge mining (#876); Lodestar LP-mincut DFVS

  search-filter artifact pruning (#982, #984) with binary-sidecar / batch-provenance FSV
  fixtures; `calyx-web-api` exposes origin artifacts honestly.
- **Ops/CI** ŌĆö aiwonder `calyxd` VRAM ceiling raised, aiwonder nextest gate repaired
  (#1025), tmp-guard foreign-owner check (#1021), CLI ingest clippy gate (#1023), Aster
  ledger verification snapshot stabilization, legacy `verify-chain` vault resolution.

## 4. Known implementation gaps (consolidated from docs 05ŌĆō20)

These are stubs, `todo!()`-equivalents, fail-loud-only paths, and unimplemented
branches found while documenting each subsystem. They are **code-state facts**,
distinct from open-issue work and from aspirations. Source doc in the last column.

| Subsystem / crate | Gap (what the code actually does) | Source doc |
|---|---|---|
| calyx-core | `CALYX_TEMPORAL_INVALID_WINDOW` declared but raised by no core path; module-local error codes sit outside the closed PRD-18 catalog (pending governance). | 05_core.md |
| calyx-aster | No quantization/compression codec here ŌĆö slot CFs are raw big-endian IEEE bits; ANN/DiskANN/SPANN live in Sextant, not aster; single-level `SstLevel` (no L0/L1 fan-out); JSON manifest; compaction cadence fixed (`FIXME(PH46)` Anneal hook not wired). | 06_aster_storage_engine.md |
| calyx-forge | Deferred backend ops (`knn`, `histogram_nmi`, `spmm_sparse_ops`, `bilinear_cross_term`, `graph_ops`, `colbert_maxsim`) declared, not implemented; no native FP4 cuBLAS GEMM (custom kernel); no runtime CPUŌåöGPU auto-dispatch/fallback. | 07_forge_math_runtime.md |
| calyx-registry | `MultimodalAdapterLens` / `CommissionedLens` produce **hash-derived** vectors, not learned outputs; `bits`/`redundancy` in `LensExplanation` are placeholders pending Assay; real model paths are `#[ignore]`/env-gated. | 08_registry_lenses.md |
| calyx-sextant | GPU parity unimplemented (`cpu_gpu_delta` always returns `CALYX_SEXTANT_GPU_PARITY_UNAVAILABLE`); DiskANN prefetch is Unix-only (no-op on Windows); DiskANN/token-DiskANN inserts are **non-incremental** (full rebuild); planner cost model is a heuristic, not measured latency. | 09_sextant_search.md |
| calyx-loom | Interaction is **Hadamard only** (no low-rank `vŌéÉßĄĆW vßĄ”`); only `StaticPairGainGate` (constant) ŌĆö no live Assay/Sextant integration; `mean_agreement` == `raw_mean_agreement`; `n_eff`/DPI are carried inputs, not computed; `SignatureResult::NewContent` never produced; graph recomputed per call (no persisted adjacency). | 10_loom_associations.md |
| calyx-assay | No Forge/GPU execution (`project_gpu` is a stub; all math CPU, O(n┬▓)); thresholds hard-coded consts (not per-vault config); logistic "probe" is a mean-difference linear classifier, not fitted regression; no auto park/retire loop; `n_eff` reports but does not prune; `admit_lens` never returns `admitted:false` (rejects via `Err`). | 11_assay_signal_bits.md |
| calyx-lodestar | **LP relaxation not wired to a solver** ŌĆö direct LP-round requests fail closed with `CALYX_KERNEL_LP_UNAVAILABLE` unless a valid external solution is supplied; build pipeline does not measure recall (fields 0 until separate test); every answerable `kernel_answer` path, including a direct self-hit, requires the ledger-backed variant; incremental rebuild is whole-graph; time-travel summarization partial. | 12_lodestar_kernel.md |
| calyx-mincut / calyx-paths | **No min-cut / max-flow / FVS solver** despite the crate name ŌĆö `lp_scaffold` only formulates the LP (missing cycle-elim constraints); `LpSolution`/`SolveStatus` are data carriers until an external solver supplies validated values; `reach` ignores edge weights; in-edge access O(E); `gft_project/reconstruct` panic on mismatch; spectral routines treat directed graph as undirected, dense O(n┬▓)/O(n┬│); recursive Tarjan SCC (stack-overflow risk). | 17_graph_mincut_paths.md |
| calyx-ward | `AnnealHook` is an interim object-safe seam ("until Anneal's PH48 queue is live"); ONNX needs real model files + CUDA (no CPU fallback); novelty classification fails closed when recurrence data absent; Polis civic guard is a synthetic-persona proof surface. | 13_ward_guard.md |
| calyx-ledger | Payload schemas are conventions, not types (`payload: Vec<u8>` opaque, enforced only by readers); no key management (caller supplies `[u8;32]`); `DirectoryLedgerStore` is "manual FSV before Aster group-commit"; `LedgerGroupCommitHook::on_commit` is a **disabled stub**; plan API name drift (`verify_chain` returns enum). | 14_ledger_provenance.md |
| calyx-anneal | `heal/` and `j/` (Objective-J machinery) summarized, not detailed; no `todo!()`/stub paths observed in the core files read (tripwire/shadow/rollback/budget/ledger are real). | 15_anneal_optimization.md |
| calyx-oracle | `OracleError::FlakyAnchor` declared but **never constructed** (dead constructor); no confidence-based refusal beyond the sufficiency gate; **no code for Objective `J` / `intelligence_report` / `growth_curve`** in this crate; PRD-22 butterfly/reverse operate on a generic graph, separate from the vault-backed production path. | 16_oracle_prediction.md |
| calyx-hazard-soak / testkit | No crate module doc; **H24 (DR drill) intentionally incomplete** ŌĆö restic restore gated behind `CALYX_PH59_RESTIC_DR=1`, skipped pending PH66 (passes on skip with `dr_restore_verified:false`); benchmark is a no-op off Linux; hazard probes reachable only via the binary. | 18_hazard_soak_and_testkit.md |
| calyx-mcp | No batch JSON-RPC at the binary; `initialize` ignores client params/version (fixed `2024-11-05`); only `{tools:{}}` advertised (no resources/prompts/logging); CLI/MCP search implementations still diverge and need a shared persisted-index execution path (#923). | 19_mcp_api_tools_reference.md |
| calyx-cli / calyxd | **MCP transport (T05) now wired into the running daemon** in server mode (production `CalyxMcpServer` + `register_all`, gated on `mcp_bind_addr` + mTLS, #959; `/metrics`-only when unconfigured); learner-origin worker API added (#813); CUDA path feature-gated (default build cannot serve in server mode, fails loud); most `CalyxMetrics` observers dormant in the daemon; many CLI subcommands are FSV/diagnostic harnesses, not production ops. | 20_cli_and_daemon_reference.md |

Several of these gaps have an explicit phase owner: Forge deferred ops (#338),
aster compaction cadence (PH46/Anneal), Sextant GPU parity & incremental DiskANN
(PH68 / #550), Lodestar LP-rounding + mincut solver (PH31/PH32 follow-up), Loom live
Assay/Sextant promotion (PH28+), MCP/daemon transport (PH63/PH64), DR drill (PH66/PH67).

## 5. Phase model ŌĆö what PH## and "done"/FSV-verified mean

### 5.1 Phases (`03_PHASE_MAP.md`)

Work is organized as **PH00ŌĆōPH72**, grouped into stages **S0ŌĆōS20**. Each phase is a
stable handle with: dependencies (phases that must be DONE first), the crate(s) it
lands in, the PRD roadmap phase + axioms it satisfies, and a one-line FSV exit gate.
Phase IDs referenced throughout the source (e.g. `FIXME(PH46)`, "until Anneal's PH48
queue is live") point into this map. Status markers: Ō£ģ DONE ┬Ę Ō¢Č ACTIVE ┬Ę ┬Ę pending.

The phase map maps onto the PRD's coarse roadmap phases P0ŌĆōP12 / P4bŌĆōP11b
(`19 ┬¦2`): P0ŌĆōP8 build the engine; P9ŌĆōP10 productionize; **P11 (Leapable Vault swap)
is the only required customer-shipping phase**; P12 (Discover hosting) is optional.

### 5.2 What "done" means ŌĆö `BUILD_DONE` (`19 ┬¦5`)

"Done" is a **mechanical predicate**, not a judgement: `BUILD_DONE` is a single
conjunction over ~26 clauses (CORE Ōł¦ LENS Ōł¦ SEARCH Ōł¦ DDA_BITS Ōł¦ KERNEL Ōł¦ GUARD Ōł¦
PROVENANCE Ōł¦ SELFOPT Ōł¦ MATH Ōł¦ ARRAYMATH Ōł¦ COMPRESS Ōł¦ UNIVERSAL Ōł¦ ORACLE Ōł¦
KERNEL_ANY Ōł¦ FORMULAS Ōł¦ RESOURCE Ōł¦ TEMPORAL Ōł¦ DEDUP Ōł¦ RECURRENCE Ōł¦ INTELLIGENCE Ōł¦
DATA Ōł¦ SECURITY Ōł¦ DEPLOY Ōł¦ SCALE Ōł¦ LEAPABLE Ōł¦ FSV). Each clause binds a phase gate
to measured threshold constants. Representative thresholds:

| Metric | Target |
|---|---|
| Multi-lens recall@10 vs single-lens (╬ö) | Ōēź +15% on a real labeled corpus |
| Kernel-only recall / full recall | Ōēź 0.95 |
| Guard injection-block rate @ calibrated FAR | Ōēź 99% |
| Anneal p99 improvement over 1e6 queries | Ōēź 20%, recall non-regressing |
| Forge matmul vs cuBLAS | within 10% on sm_120 |
| CPUŌåöGPU bit-parity | within 1e-3 rel tolerance |
| Differentiation contract | Ōēź 0.05 bits, Ōēż 0.6 corr |
| Search p99 (SingleLens / RRF-6 / KernelFirst@1e8 / Pipeline) | < 5 / < 15 / < 25 / < 60 ms |
| Vault migration fidelity (SQLiteŌåÆCalyx) | byte-exact on content; control-plane responses identical |

Issue #642 is the standing owner of the final clause-by-clause `BUILD_DONE` audit.

### 5.3 What "FSV-verified" means (`FSV_NOTES.md`, `19 ┬¦3`)

**FSV = Forensic Source-of-truth Verification.** A passing test or a function return
is a *claim*; the **bytes are the verdict** (`DOCTRINE ┬¦0`). The protocol:

1. Identify the bytes that prove the claim (Aster CF row, WAL record, SSTable, Ledger
   entry, on-disk file, Prometheus metric).
2. Read them **before** the action (baseline).
3. Execute the action.
4. Read them **after** (independent read ŌĆö never trust the function's return).
5. Inspect the delta; record command, SoT path, expected vs actual bytes, Ōēź3 edge
   cases, and fail-closed `CALYX_*` proof in the GitHub issue.

Rules: **FSV scripts/harnesses are banned** ŌĆö Calyx may ship *readback tools*
(`calyx readback --cf ŌĆ” --vault ŌĆ”`, `calyx verify-chain ŌĆ”`) that print bytes for a
human/agent to judge, never a green-checkmark harness. There is **no CI pipeline ŌĆö
FSV is CI**; everything is built/run/tested on the GPU host. Every "done" in ┬¦1 carries
a recorded FSV evidence root (`ŌĆ”/data/fsv-issue<N>-ŌĆ”`) with artifact hashes.

A per-merge code-quality gate also binds (`19 ┬¦3b`): `cargo check`/`test`/`clippy
-D warnings` green, **no `.rs` file > 500 lines** (over-limit ŌåÆ file a modularization
issue), and CPUŌåöGPU bit-parity on Forge-touching changes.

---

  #642) and the epics; the 7 context/state issues were read for #689/#688/#23 and

  were not enumerated here ŌĆö see #23 and `03_PHASE_MAP.md` for completed evidence roots.
- The ┬¦0 status disagreement (phase map PH40ŌĆōPH42 vs issue #23 PH43) is reported, not
  resolved: confirming the true frontier requires reading the GPU-host bytes, which is
  outside this documentation pass.
- ┬¦4 consolidates the gaps **as recorded in sibling docs 05ŌĆō20**; it does not re-derive
  them from source. If a doc's gap section is stale, this table inherits that staleness.

# 25 ŌĆö Web API Reference (`calyx-web-api`)

**Source files covered:**
- `crates/calyx-web-api/Cargo.toml` (lib + `[[bin]]` `calyx-web-api`)
- `crates/calyx-web-api/src/main.rs` (binary entry point, context loading, bind)
- `crates/calyx-web-api/src/lib.rs` (router, handlers, auth, guardrails, cache, error envelope)
- `crates/calyx-search/src/lib.rs` (the shared search path used by `/v1/search`)

> `calyx-web-api` is the workspace's **fourth surface**, added after the doc set's original
> `2e7b9a2` baseline (issue #889 and the #890ŌĆō#937 follow-ups). It is a **read-only**,
> loopback-only HTTP API; there are **no write routes**. It is documented here as observed in
> code at HEAD `96cbc84f`. Where a behavior is fail-closed or unwired, that is stated.

---

## 1. What it is

`calyx-web-api` compiles both a **library** (`lib.rs`) and a **binary** (`[[bin]]` named
`calyx-web-api`, `Cargo.toml`). The binary (`src/main.rs`) loads three contexts from the
environment ŌĆö a `MeasureCtx` (vault + panel), a `ProvenanceCtx` (ledger), and an `AuthCtx`
(bearer secret) ŌĆö **asserts the bind address is loopback** (`127.0.0.1:8121`), and serves
with [Axum](https://docs.rs/axum). Startup is **fail-loud**: a missing/unreadable vault,
ledger, or auth secret panics rather than serving a degraded surface. The service depends on
the shared `calyx-search` crate (┬¦8) so its `/v1/search` runs the exact same ranking path as
the `calyx` CLI.

| Property | Value |
|---|---|
| Framework | Axum (Tokio) |
| Bind | `127.0.0.1:8121` (loopback only; asserted at startup) |
| Upstream `calyxd` | `127.0.0.1:8120` (reported in `/v1/health`) |
| Mutability | **read-only** (no write/ingest routes compiled) |
| Auth | shared-secret bearer on every route (┬¦3) |
| Surfaces consumed | `calyx-search`, `calyx-registry`, `calyx-ward`, `calyx-lodestar`, `calyx-ledger` |

---

## 2. Routes

Production router, `build_app_with_measure_and_provenance()` (`src/lib.rs`):

```rust
let measure_route = Router::new()
    .route("/v1/health", get(health_full))
    .route("/v1/measure", post(measure))
    .route("/v1/search", post(search))
    .route("/v1/guard", post(guard_handler))
    .route("/v1/kernel", get(kernel_handler))
    .with_state(measure_ctx);
let prov_route = Router::new()
    .route("/v1/provenance/{id}", get(provenance_wired))
    .with_state(prov);
routes_base()
    .merge(measure_route)
    .merge(prov_route)
    .route("/metrics", get(metrics_handler))   // Prometheus surface (#945/#946/#597)
    .fallback(fallback_404)
    .method_not_allowed_fallback(fallback_405)
    .layer(middleware::from_fn_with_state(limiter, guardrails))
    .layer(middleware::from_fn_with_state(auth, require_bearer))
    .route_layer(track_metrics)                // per-route RED accumulation
    .layer(panic_catch_layer())
```

Layer order (outermost first): `panic_catch` ŌåÆ `require_bearer` ŌåÆ `guardrails` ŌåÆ route. So a
request is authenticated, then rate/size/timeout-checked, then handled; a panic in a handler
is caught and returned as a closed `Internal` envelope (┬¦4).

| Method | Path | Handler | Engine call | Cached |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| GET | `/v1/health` | `health_full` | `measure_query_vectors` + `probe_hhem_faithfulness` | no |
| POST | `/v1/measure` | `measure` | `calyx_registry::measure_constellation` | no |
| POST | `/v1/search` | `search` | `calyx_search::search_outcome` | yes (TTL) |
| POST | `/v1/guard` | `guard_handler` | `calyx_ward::guard` | no |
| GET | `/v1/kernel` | `kernel_handler` | `calyx_lodestar` measured kernel | yes (TTL) |
| GET | `/v1/provenance/{id}` | `provenance_wired` | `calyx_ledger` verify + answer-trace | yes (TTL) |
| GET | `/metrics` | `metrics_handler` | engine-native gauges + per-route HTTP RED (┬¦2.7) | no |

### 2.1 `POST /v1/measure`
- **Body:** `{ "text": String }`.
- **Returns:** the full `VaultPanelState` constellation (every active lens slot) for the text.
- **Calls:** `measure_constellation` (calyx-registry). GPU route (smaller body cap, tighter rate limit; ┬¦5).

### 2.2 `POST /v1/search` (issue #573/#900, #1898 cache, #930)
- **Body:** `{ "query": String, "k"?: usize=10 (>0), "guard"?: bool=false, "fusion"?: String="rrf" }`.
  `fusion` Ōłł `rrf | weighted-rrf | single-lens | kernel-first | pipeline`; `guard:true` ŌćÆ in-region guard.
- **Returns:** `{ query, k, guardTau, hits: [{ rank, cxId, score, provenance: { ledgerSeq, chainHash } }] }`.
- **Calls:** `search_outcome` (calyx-search) ŌĆö the same Sextant recall ŌåÆ fusion ŌåÆ rerank ŌåÆ
  provenance path the CLI uses. **Cached** keyed by `(k, guard, fusion, query)`.

### 2.3 `POST /v1/guard` (issue #574, #932, #1899)
- **Body:** `{ "answer": String, "evidence": String, "high_stakes"?: bool=true }`.
- **Returns:** `{ verdict: "accept"|"new-region"|"quarantine"|"refuse", overallPass, provisional,
  highStakes, far, farByAspect, perSlot: [{ slot, cosine, tau, pass, aspect }] }`.
- **`perSlot[].aspect`** is the slot's `SlotKind` label (`Identity`/`Content`/`Stylistic`),
  persisted in the guard profile calibration metadata (#1899); `null` if the slot was
  calibrated before `slot_kind` was persisted (never fabricated). `farByAspect` is the max
  conformal false-acceptance rate per aspect class.
- **Calls:** `read_guard_profile` (vault Guard CF) ŌåÆ measure ŌåÆ `calyx_ward::guard`.

### 2.4 `GET /v1/kernel` (issue #575/#1900, #905, #931)
- **Returns:** `{ kernelId, panelVersion, recallGate, members: [{ id, trust, recallContribution, label }],
  kernelSize, corpusSize, groundedFraction, recall: { measured, kernelOnly, full, ratio, gate, passed,
  nQueriesTested, approxFactor, warning } }`.
- **`members[].recallContribution`** is the **leave-one-out** recall drop for that member
  (`null` if the slot is not measurable); **`trust`** is `anchored` vs `provisional`;
  **`label`** comes from the constellation's `AnchorKind::Label` (`null`, never fabricated).
- **Calls:** `measured_kernel_with_contributions_from_vault` (calyx-lodestar). **Cached** under a
  constant key.

### 2.5 `GET /v1/provenance/{id}` (issue #577, #899, #906, #930)
- **Path param:** `id` (answer id).
- **Returns:** `{ id, found, trusted, complete, warnings, chain: { result, count|atSeq },
  entries: [{ seq, kind, subject, prevHash, entryHash, payload }] }`.
- **Calls:** ledger `scan` ŌåÆ `verify_chain` (BLAKE3 chain) ŌåÆ `get_answer_trace` (calyx-ledger).
  The web-api unifies provenance onto the vault's own ledger (one-vault origin, #906). **Cached**
  keyed by id.

### 2.6 `GET /v1/health` (issue #579/#1908, #915)
Always returns **200 OK** (even when degraded; the external breaker reads the fields):
`{ status, service: "calyx-web-api", readOnly: true, gpu, vault, faithfulness, panelVersion, upstream }`.
- `status` = `degraded` if `gpu != "ok"` **or** `faithfulness != "ok"`, else `ok`.
- `gpu` probed via `measure_query_vectors("health")` (ok iff any slot returns a dense vector).
- `faithfulness` probed via `probe_hhem_faithfulness()` (ok iff HHEM responds within the probe
  timeout; otherwise `degraded`, logged `CALYX_WEB_API_HHEM_PROBE_FAILED` / `ŌĆ”_TIMEOUT`).
- `panelVersion` from the loaded panel; `upstream` is the static `calyxd` address.

### 2.7 `GET /metrics` (Prometheus, #945/#946/#597, #1249 G11)
Prometheus text-format surface mounted by `build_app_with_measure_and_provenance()` (`metrics.rs`):
- **Engine-native gauges** from `MetricsCtx`, which shares the **same** loaded vault panel
  (`MeasureCtx`) and on-disk ledger (`ProvenanceCtx`) the `/v1` data endpoints serve ŌĆö so every
  gauge reflects the exact state the origin answers from, never a drift-prone separate health view.
- **Per-route HTTP RED metrics** (request **R**ate, **E**rrors, **D**uration) accumulated by the
  `track_metrics` route-layer middleware into a shared `HttpMetrics`: request counts, error counts,
  and latency histograms (cumulative `le` buckets on the exponential ladder
  `0.005ŌĆ”10.0 s`), rendered alongside the engine gauges so p50/p95 are derivable per route.

---

## 3. Authentication (`AuthCtx`, `require_bearer`)

Every route is behind a fail-closed shared-secret bearer check (issue #916/#1906):
- **Secret** from env `CALYX_WEB_API_BEARER_SECRET` (required; fail-loud at startup if unset).
- **Header:** `Authorization: Bearer <secret>`; compared in **constant time** (no timing oracle).
- **Failure:** `401` with the error envelope (┬¦4) plus `WWW-Authenticate: Bearer realm="calyx-origin"`.
- There is **no anonymous access** and no per-user identity ŌĆö it is a single origin secret.

---

## 4. Error envelope (`ErrorCode`)

Responses use a **closed** `{code, message, remediation}` envelope (`src/lib.rs`). The
`ErrorCode` enum has 9 variants ŌåÆ HTTP status:

| Variant | Status | Code string |
|---|---|---|
| `BadRequest` | 400 | `CALYX_WEB_API_BAD_REQUEST` |
| `Unauthorized` | 401 | `CALYX_WEB_API_UNAUTHORIZED` |
| `NotFound` | 404 | `CALYX_WEB_API_NOT_FOUND` |
| `MethodNotAllowed` | 405 | `CALYX_WEB_API_METHOD_NOT_ALLOWED` |
| `PayloadTooLarge` | 413 | `CALYX_WEB_API_PAYLOAD_TOO_LARGE` |
| `RateLimited` | 429 | `CALYX_WEB_API_RATE_LIMITED` |
| `NotImplemented` | 501 | `CALYX_WEB_API_NOT_IMPLEMENTED` |
| `Timeout` | 504 | `CALYX_WEB_API_TIMEOUT` |
| `Internal` | 500 | `CALYX_WEB_API_INTERNAL` |

Messages are caller-safe: they never leak the bearer secret, raw query strings, or panic
details.

---

## 5. Per-request guardrails (`guardrails` middleware)

| Guardrail | Non-GPU routes (`health`, `kernel`, `provenance`) | GPU routes (`measure`, `search`, `guard`) |
|---|---|---|
| Body size cap | `MAX_BODY_BYTES = 8 KiB` | `MAX_GPU_BODY_BYTES = 4 KiB` (ŌåÆ 413) |
| Rate limit (token bucket) | 60 capacity, 30 refill/s | 8 capacity, 2 refill/s (ŌåÆ 429 + `Retry-After: 1`) |
| Request timeout | `REQUEST_TIMEOUT = 5 s` (ŌåÆ 504, aborts slow upstream) | same |

Buckets are **per-route global** (loopback-only; not per-IP). The timeout has no env override
in production; the limiter is injected at startup.

---

## 6. Response cache (`ResponseCache`)

A bounded TTL cache (issue #1898/#930) is applied to the idempotent reads `/v1/search`,
`/v1/kernel`, and `/v1/provenance/{id}`:
- **TTL:** env `CALYX_WEB_API_CACHE_TTL_SECS` (default **30 s**; `0` disables caching).
- **Capacity:** env `CALYX_WEB_API_CACHE_CAPACITY` (default **256** entries; oldest evicted on overflow).
- Keys join free-text fields with the unit separator `\u{1f}` to avoid collisions.
- A hit replays the original response **byte-for-byte** with `X-Cache: HIT` and an `Age` header.

---

## 7. Environment variables (summary)

| Var | Purpose | Default |
|---|---|---|
| `CALYX_WEB_API_BEARER_SECRET` | bearer secret (required) | ŌĆö (fail-loud) |
| `CALYX_WEB_API_CACHE_TTL_SECS` | response-cache TTL | 30 |
| `CALYX_WEB_API_CACHE_CAPACITY` | response-cache entries | 256 |

(Vault, panel, ledger, and bind/upstream addresses are loaded by `main.rs`; see the crate for
their exact env names.)

---

## 8. The shared `calyx-search` crate (issue #573/#900)

`calyx-search` (`crates/calyx-search/src/lib.rs`) is a shared, extracted search index + query
stack so **both** `calyx` (CLI) and `calyx-web-api` (`/v1/search`) run the **same** Sextant
recall ŌåÆ fusion ŌåÆ rerank ŌåÆ provenance path ŌĆö no mocks, no duplicated ranking logic. It exports
`FusionChoice`, `GuardChoice`, `SearchOutcome`, `measure_query_vectors()`, and
`search_outcome()` (the idempotent ranking entry point). This resolved the earlier
CLI-vs-API search divergence noted in [01_system_overview.md](01_system_overview.md) ┬¦9.

---

## 9. Gaps / not covered

- **Read-only by design:** no ingest/anchor/write routes exist on this surface; mutation goes
  through the CLI or MCP ([19](19_mcp_api_tools_reference.md), [20](20_cli_and_daemon_reference.md)).
- **Loopback only:** the binary asserts a `127.0.0.1` bind; it is not a public/Internet-facing
  service and has no TLS termination of its own.
- **Single-secret auth:** bearer auth is one origin secret with no user identity, scopes, or
  rotation logic in-crate.
- **Vector fusion fail-closed:** like the CLI, real per-slot vector fusion remains unwired
  (`PlanStep::VectorFusion`), so `/v1/search` fusion modes depending on it fail closed rather
  than returning synthetic scores (see [12_lodestar_kernel.md](12_lodestar_kernel.md) and
  [01_system_overview.md](01_system_overview.md) ┬¦9).
- **Exact field shapes** above are summarized from the handler code at `96cbc84f`; consult
  `src/lib.rs` for byte-exact serialization (field casing is camelCase in responses).
